[p.3] / āryamañjuśriye kumārabhūtāya namaḥ / / uttamajano hi prāyaśo guruṃ śraddhādevatāṃ cābhyarcyakarmasu pravartata
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / ma dhyan nta bi bham ga t'i k'a / / bod skad du / / dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel bshad / / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo / / ya rabs dag ni phal cher bla ma dang dad pa'i lha la mchod nas las rnams la 'jug ste /
ityayamapyahamuttamajananayamanuvartī madhyāntavibhāgasūtrabhāṣyaṃ
# dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i mdo rnam par bshad par 'dod pas / / bdag la yang 'di ni ya rabs kyi tshul can no zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir /
cikīrṣustatpraṇeturvaktuś ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā tadarthavibhāgāya prayukta
# de mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la mchod nas / / de'i don rnam par dbye bar zhugs so zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
iti pratipādayannāha -
# bstan bcos 'di ni rab mdzad pa /
śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram / ityādi / / evaṃ kṛtvā ko guṇaḥ prāpyate ?
# zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so / / de ltar byas na yon tan ci zhig thob ce na /
guṇavato hitakāriṇaś ca pūjayatāmeṣāṃ puṇyamupacīyate /
# yon tan dang ldan pa dang phan 'dogs 'dogs pa la mchod na bsod nams 'phel bar 'gyur ro /
puṇya upacite samārambhād vighnavināyakairanupahatānalpena prayāsena / samāpayantīti /
# bsod nams 'phel na yang dag par rtsom pa la bar chad dang bgegs kyis mi tshugs par tshogs chung ngu rdzogs par 'gyur ro /
athavā praṇetṛpraṇeyapravacanāt sūtrapraṇetṛvaktṛvṛttīṣu
# yang na mdzad pas gsungs pa dang 'chad pas bshad pa yang dag par byin par bsnyad pas /
gauravotpādanārthamāha- / śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram / iti sarvam /
# mdzad pa dang 'chad pa dang mdo dang 'brel ba la gus pa bskyed par bya ba'i phyir / / bstan bcos 'di ni rab mdzad pa / / zhes bya ba thams cad smos so /
tatra praṇetṛvacanāt sūtre gauravam utpadyate /
# de la mdzad pas bshad par bstan pas mdo la gus pa skye ste /
yasyā'sya kārikāśāstrasyāryamaitreyaḥ praṇetā /
# 'di ltar bstan bcos tshig le'ur byas pa'i mdzad pa po ni 'phags pa byams pa ste /
sa caikajātipratibandhāt sarvabodhisattvābhijñādhāraṇīpratisaṃvit / samādhīndriyakṣāntivimokṣaiḥ paramaṃ pāraṃ gataḥ sarvāsu
# de yang skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i phyir / / byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa dang gzungs dang so so yang dag par rig pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang dbang dang bzod pa dang rnam par thar pa thams cad kyi dam pa'i pha rol tu son pa /
bodhisattvabhūmiṣu [p.4] / niḥśeṣam api prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ /
# byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad la sgrib pa yang ma lus par spangs pa'o /
vaktṛsamādānadvāreṇa vṛttau gauravam utpadyate /
# 'chad pas yang dag par byin pa'i sgo nas 'grel pa la gus pa skye bar 'gyur te /
vaktā punar atrācāryā'saṅgaḥ tasmācchrutvācāryambhadantavasubandhuḥ / tad bhāṣyam akarot /
# 'di la 'chad pa ni slob dpon thogs med do / / de las slob dpon btsun pa dbyig gnyen gyis gsan nas 'di'i 'grel pa mdzad de /
tayor uttaram aprajñāvator abhrānti prativedhadhāraṇopadeśasāmarthyād / atra sūtrārtho'bhrāntam upadiṣṭa iti vṛttau gauravam utpadyate /
# de gnyis kyang shes rab mchog dang ldan pas ma nor bar rtogs pa dang bzung ba dang ston nus pas 'dir mdo'i don ma nor ba bstan to zhes 'grel pa la gus pa skye ste /
evaṃ ye pudgalaṃ pramāṇīkurvanti teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyo gauravotpattiḥ / / ye ca dharmānusāriṇas teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyoḥ śubhārthā'vabodhaḥ /
# de ltar gang dag gang zag tshad mar byed pa de dag ni / / mdo dang 'grel pa la gus pa skye'o / / gang yang chos la ston pa de dag ni mdo dang 'grel pa'i don bzang po khong du chud de /
jāte ca niścaye iyaṃ praṇeturvaktuś ca pratītyā prabhāvanā na tu
# nges pa skyes na 'di mdzad pa dang 'chad pa yang rtogs pas rab tu phye ba yin gyis /
tarkāgamamātreṇa prabhāvaneti praṇetṛvaktṛgauravotpattiḥ /
# rtog ge dang lung tsam gyis rab tu phye bar ni zad do zhes mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la gus pa skye'o /
idam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ - / kīdṛśaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ /
# da ni bstan bcos kyi rang bzhin ci 'dra ba dang ci'i phyir bstan bcos zhes bya ba 'di bshad par bya'o /
śāstraṃ kim iti cet nāma-pada-vyañjanakāyaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ
# ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs su snang ba'i rnam par rig pa rnams ni bstan bcos so /
śāstraṃ / / atha vā lokottara-jñānaprāpakaśabdaviśeṣaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ
# yang na 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes thob par byed pa'i sgra'i khyad par du snang ba'i rnam par rig pa rnams bstan bcos so /
śāstraṃ / / kathaṃ vijñaptayaḥ praṇīyanta ucyante vā ?/ / praṇetṛ-vijñaptiprabhatvat prajñaptīnāṃ nātra doṣaḥ /
# rnam par rig pa rnams ji ltar mdzad cing brjod ce na / / mdzad pa dang 'chad pa'i rnam par rig pa las nyan pa'i rnam par rig pa rnams skye bas 'di la nyes pa med do / / slob ma 'chos pa'i phyir bstan bcos te /
śiṣyadhārmiko hi śīlasamādhiprajñāviśeṣotpādāt
# slob ma'i 'chos pa ni tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi khyad par bskyed pa'i phyir /
kāyavāṅmanasāṃbhārānutpatīkarmaṇo nivartate sambhārotpattikarmāṇi / ca pravartate /
# lus dang ngag dang yid tshogs par mi 'byung ba'i las las bzlog pa dang tshogs par 'byung ba'i las la 'jug pa'o /
atha vā śāstralakṣaṇasya śāsanācchāstraṃ /
# yang na bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid du 'thad pa'i phyir bstan bcos te /
svalakṣaṇaṃ yad upadeśo bhāsamānasarva kleśaprahāṇāya / nirantaradīrghavividhatīvraduḥkhabhītyāś ca durgater bhavāc ca / santrāyate / / tasmāt kleśaripuśāsanād bhavadurgatisantārāc ca śāstralakṣaṇaṃ /
# lung mnos pa goms par byas pas bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa spong bar 'gyur ba dang bar chad med pa yun ring ba'i sdug bsngal drag po sna tshogs kyis 'jigs pa'i ngan song rnams dang srid pa las skyob pa gang yin pa de ni bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid do / / de'i phyir nyon mongs pa'i dgra 'chos pa dang ngan 'gro dang srid pa las skyob pas bstan bcos kyi mtshan nyid de /
etac ca dvayam api sarvasmin mahāyāne sarvasmiṃś ca tad vyākhyāne / vidyate nānyatreti /
# de gnyis kyang theg pa chen po thams cad dang de bshad pa thams cad la yod kyi gzhan la med de de'i phyir 'di ni bstan bcos so /
ata etac chāstraṃ / / āha ca - / yacchāsti ca kleśaripūn aśeṣān
# de la smras pa / / nyon mongs dgra rnams ma lus 'chos pa dang /
santrāyate durgatito bhavāc ca /
# ngan 'gro srid las skyob pa gang yin pa /
tacchāsanā (tttrāṇa-) guṇāc ca śāstraṃ / etad dvayaṃ cānyamateṣu nāsti //
# chos skyob yon tan phyir na bstan bcos te / / gnyis po 'di dag gzhan gyi lugs la med /
asyeti / / kriyānadvāreṇa saptavastusaṅgrahasya
# 'di ni zhes bya ba ni / / theg pa gsum gyi sgo nas dngos po bdun du bsdus pa /
kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaprāpakasya madhyāntavibhāgakārikāśāstrasya / hṛdi sthitatvād asyeti pratyakṣopadeśaḥ /
# nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa spong ba thob pa dang bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa 'di ni sems la gnas pa'i phyir dang 'di zhes mngon sum du bstan to /
praṇetārm iti kartāraṃ / / yadyapy ayaṃ dhātuḥ prāpaṇārthas tathāpi pra-śabdasaṃyogāt
# rab mdzad pa zhes bya ba ni byed pa po'o / / skad kyi dbyings 'di thob par byed pa yin mod kyi /
viśeṣārthako draṣṭavyaḥ /
# 'on kyang rab kyi sgra dang sgrogs na byed par lta ste /
uktaṃ hi - [p.5] / upasargeṇa dhātvartho balād anyaḥ pratīyate /
# skad dbyings don gyi stobs ldan yang / / nye bar bsgyur bas zil non 'gyur / / gang g'a'i chu ni mngar mod kyi /
gaṅgāsalilamādhuryaṃ sāgareṇa yathāmbhasā //
# rgya mtsho'i chu ni ji bzhin no / / zhes bshad do /
sugatātmajam iti /
# bde gshegs nyid skyes zhes bya ba ni /
suṣṭhu gataḥ savāsana kleśāvaraṇāj jñeyāvaraṇāc cāpratiṣṭhitaṃ / virvāṇam iti sugataḥ /
# bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa las mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das par shin tu gshegs pas bde bar gshegs pa'o /
sa ca sarvavāsanāvaraṇaprahīṇaḥ sarvathā sarvadharmāvabodhasvarūpaḥ / sarvavibhūtyāśrayabhūta-ṇiratnavad acintyaprabhāvavigrahaḥ
# de yang bag chags kyi sgrib pa thams cad spangs pa / / chos thams cad rnam pa thams cad du thugs su chud pa'i rang gi ngo bo 'byor ba thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa / / yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che ltar bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mthu mnga' ste /
sarvasattvānāmanābhogena sarvārtha raṇasamartho
# sems can thams cad kyi don thams cad lhun gyis grub par mdzad par spyod pa /
nirvikalpakajñānaviśeṣātmakaḥ sugataḥ taj janitatvān nirvikalpasya / jñānasya / / tasmāt tasmin vā jātaḥ sugatātmajaḥ / / athavā sugatātmanā jāta iti sugatātmajaḥ / / yathoktaṃ sūtrāntare -jāto bhavati tathāgatavaṃśe tadātmakavstu / pratilābhād iti / / evaṃ sati bodhisattvasya daśamyāṃ bhūmau pratiṣṭhitasya sarvākāraṃ
# rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi khyad par gyi bdag nyid ni bde bar gshegs pa'o / / de'i bdag nyid ni rnam par dag pa'i deb zhin nyid de / / de las rnam bar mi rtog pa'i ye shes rab tu byung ba'i phyir de las sam / / der skye bas na bde gshegs nyid skyes so / / yang na bde bar gshegs pa nyid du skyes pas / / bde gshegs nyid skyes te / / mdo gzhan las de'i bdag nyid kyi chos rab tu rnyed pas / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung du skyes pa yin no zhes ji skad gsungs pa lta bu'o / / de lta bas na byang chub sems dpa' sa bcu pa la rab tu gnas pa ni /
jñeyaṃ vastu karatalastham ivāmalakaṃ
# shes bya'i dngos po'i rnam pa thams cad sgyu ru ra lag mthil du gzhag pa /
tattvaṃśukāvacchāditalocanasyevābhāsamāyāti /
# dar lva srab mos g yogs pa'i mig la snang ba bzhin no /
bhagavataḥ punar apanītalocanāvaraṇasyevetyayaṃ viśeṣaḥ /
# bcom ldan 'das kyi ni mig gi sgrib pa bsal ba bzhin te / / 'di ni khyad par ro /
atra hi sugatātmajasya śāstrapraṇetur avabodhasampat pradarśitā / lābhasatkāranirapekṣasya śāstrapraṇetṛtvena karuṇāsampat
# 'dir ni bde bar gshegs pa'i bdag nyid las skyes pas / / bstan bcos mdzad pa de kho na thugs su chud pa phun sum tshogs par bstan pa dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti la mi lta bar bstan bcos mdzad pas /
prajñāsampacca / / vaktāram iti vyākhyānasya kartāraṃ /
# thugs rje phun sum tshogs pa dang shes rab phun sum tshogs par bstan pa'o / / 'chad pa ni bshad par byed pa ste /
abhyarhyeti sambadhyate /
# mngon par mchod ces bya ba dang sbyar ro /
sugatātmajamityapītyapare / / sa punar āryā'saṅgaḥ /
# kha cig na re bde gshegs nyid las skyes pa zhes kyang bya'o zhe'o / / de ni 'phags pa thogs med do /
tasya hīdaṃ śāstram abhivyaktaṃ ākhyātaṃ cāryamaitreyādhiṣṭhānāt
# de la ni 'phags pa byams pa'i byin rlabs kyis na / / chos kyi rgyun gyis bstan bcos 'di mngon du gyur cing bshad do /
dharmasantānena /
# su la 'chad pa zhe na /
ceti samuccaye pādapūraṇe'dhikavacane vā /
# bdag sogs la zhes bya ba ste / / bdag thog mar byas pa gang yin pa de dag ni bdag la sogs pa ste /
anyān api buddhabodhisattvānarcayitvā na kevalaṃ praṇetāraṃ / vaktārañceti /
# 'di ni bdag nyid kyi mi slu ba las lung mnos par ston to / / yang zhes bya ba ni bsdu ba'am /
kebhyo vaktāraṃ /
# rtsa ba bskangs pa'am /
asmad ādibhya iti /
# lhag pa'i tshig ste /
vayam ādir yeṣāṃ te'samadādayas tebhyo'smadādibhyaḥ / / anenātmana upadeśasyāmṛṣātvaṃ vyajyate /
# mdzad pa dang 'chad pa nyi tshe la ma yin gyi / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gang yang rung ba dag la mchod par bya'o /
abhyarhyeti abhyarcya /
# mngon mchod ces bya ba ni rjed pa'o /
abhitaḥ purataḥ sākṣād iva sthitaṃ /
# mngon par zhes bya ba ni mdun nam mngon sum dang 'dra bar gnas pa'o /
arhitvā arcayitvā kāyavāṅmanobhiḥ /
# mchod pa ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyis rjed pa'o /
śāstrasya praṇetāraṃ vaktāraṃ cābhyarcya kiṃ kariṣyasītyāha -
# bstan bcos mdzad pa dang 'chad pa la mngon par mchod nas ci zhig bya zhe na /
yatīṣye'rthavivecane // iti /
# don rnams dbye phyir 'bad par bya /
yatnamārapsye arthavivecane arthavivareṇe pṛthagbhāvakaraṇe vā /
# zhes bya ba smos so / / don dbye ba'i phyir ram; don dgrol ba'i phyir ram /
iyaṃ ca nimittārthā saptamī / / arthavivecananimittam ityarthaḥ // [p.6]
# so sor dbye ba'i phyir bsgrim par bya ba'i phyir zhes bya ba 'di ni rgyu'i don te /
arthaḥ punar atra śāstraśarīram iti /
# don rnam par dbye ba'i rgyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyanta iti vacanāt / / kim artham idaṃ śāstraṃ praṇītaṃ /
# don ni 'dir bstan bcos kyi lus yin te zhes bya ba don bdun po 'di dag bstan bcos 'di las 'chad do zhes 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ samyag nirvikalpa-jñānotpādanārthaṃ / / dharmanairātmyadeśanatayā nirvikalpajñānotpādāt tadabhyāsāc ca
# ci'i phyir bstan bcos 'di bshad ce na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes bskyed pa'i phyir te /
niḥśeṣasavāsana kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇam avāpyate / / ayaṃ punardharmanairātbhyasyavirodhavādo yat sarvadharmarahitatā
# chos la bdag med pa bstan pas rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes bskyed pa dang de goms pas bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa ma lus par spangs pa thob par 'gyur ro /
dharmanairātmyam/ / antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā ca dharmanairātmyam ityatas tat pratiṣedhena
# chos la bdag med pa yang chos thams cad med pa nyid chos la bdag med pa dang nang na byed pa'i skyes bu med pa nyid chos rnams la bdag med pa'o zhes mi mthun par smra ba de dag bkag pas /
tathābhūtanairātmyapratipādanārthaṃ śāstrārambhaḥ /
# chos la bdag med pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du bstan par bya ba'i phyir bstan bcos brtsam mo /
lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣv apratipannavipratipannānāṃ samyag avabodhotpādanād / apratipattivipratipattyapanayanārtham ity anye / / atha vā pañcākārajñeyaṃ lokadhātusattvadharmavineyopāyadhātvātmake
# gzhan dag na re mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa la sogs pa ma rtogs pa dang log par rtogs pa rnams yang dag par rtogs pa skyed pas ma rtogs pa rnams dang log par rtogs pa bsal ba'i phyir ro zhe'o / / yang na 'jig rten gyi khams dang sems can dang chos dang 'dul ba dang thabs kyi bdag nyid de /
pratyekam anantaprabhedatvād durvijñeyam iti bodhisattvānāṃ
# shes bya rnam lnga re re la yang rab tu dbye ba mtha' yas pa'i phyir shes par bya dka'o snyam du /
yaścittasaṅkocas tad apanayanārtham āha -
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems zhum pa gang yin pa de bstsal ba'i phyir /
lakṣaṇaṃ hyāvṛtis tattvaṃ / iti /
# mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa dang de kho na zhes bya ba dag smos so /
tatrāditaḥ śāstraśarīraṃ vyavasthāpyata iti /
# de la thog ma kho nar bstan bcos kyi lus rnam par gzhag ste zhes bya ba la /
tatreti śāstrasyārthavivecane śāstre [p.7]
# de la zhes bya ba ni bstan bcos kyi don rnam par 'byed pa de la'am /
vā / / ādita iti prathamata iti /
# bstan bcos la'o / / thog ma kho nar zhes bya ba ni /
śāstraṃ vivaraṇaṃ /
# dang po kho nar ro /
taccharīraṃ saṃkṣepaḥ piṇḍārtho vāśrayārthena vā śarīraṃ / / yathā hi bāhyādhyātmikāyatanāśrayaḥ kāyaḥ śarīram ity ucyate evaṃ
# bstan bcos ni bshad par zad do / / de'i lus ni mdor bsdus pa'am / / don bsdus pa'o / / gnas kyi don ni lus so / / dper na phyi dang nang gi skye mched kyi gnas ni khog pa ste / / lus zhes bya ba de bzhin du /
yānarthān niścitya śāstraṃ pravartate te'rthās tasya śarīraṃ /
# don gang dag la gnas te / / bstan bcos la 'jug pa'i don de rnams ni de'i lus so /
te ca saptyārthā lakṣaṇādayaḥ /
# de dag kyang don bdun po dag ste /
vyavasthāpyata iti prajñāpyate ākhyāyata ityarthaḥ /
# mtshan nyid la sogs pa dag go / / rnam par gzhag ces bya ba ni bcas pa ste /
nanu śāstrāvabhodhenaiva taccharīraṃ vijñāsyata iti nirarthakam ādau
# bshad ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / bstan bcos khong du chud pa nyid kyis de'i lus shes par mi 'gyur ram /
tad vyavasthāpanaṃ / / na nirarthakaṃ śiṣyā'nugrahārthatvāt /
# de bas na thog ma de rnam par gzhag pa ni don med do / / slob ma rnams la phan gdags pa'i phyir don med pa ma yin no /
gatārtho hi śiṣyaḥ sukhaṃ vistaram ucyamānaṃ pratipādyate / / dṛṣṭā bhūmir niḥśaṅkam aśvavāhaneneva nānyathā /
# slob mas don khong du chud na rgyas par brjod kyang bde blag tu khong du chud par 'gyur te dkyus kyis bstan pa'i rta thags thogs med par rgyug pa bzhin te /
ityete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyante / / itiḥ śāstraśarīrasamāptyarthaḥ /
# gzhan du ma yin no zhes bya ba don bdun po 'di dag bstan bcos 'di las 'chad do zhes bya ba la zhes bya ba ni / / bstan bcos kyi lus rdzogs so zhes bya ba ni tha tshig go /
eta iti ye lakṣaṇādaya uddiṣṭāḥ / / sapteti saṃkhyāparyantādhigamārtham upādānaṃ /
# shes par bya ba yin pas don de khong du chud par bya ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / bdun po zhes bya ba ni grangs so /
arthyanta ityarthā adhigamyanta iti yāvat /
# 'di dag ces bya ba ni mtshan nyid la sogs pa smos pa gang yin pa rnams so /
asmin śāstra iti madhyāntavibhāgasaṃjñake /
# bstan bcos 'di las zhes bya ba ni dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya'o /
upadiśyanta ityākhyāyante viniściyante vā /
# 'chad ces bya ba ni bstan pa'am gtan la 'bebs pa'o /
yad uta iti tathā'rthapratipādananipātaḥ / / lakṣaṇam iti / / lakṣyante'neneti lakṣaṇaṃ / / tac ca dvividhaṃ saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ vyavadānalakṣaṇāñca /
# 'di lta ste zhes bya ba ni de'i don khong du chud par byed pa'i tshig gi phrad do / / mtshan nyid ces bya ba ni / / 'dis mtshon par byed pas mtshan nyid do / / de yang rnam pa gnyis te / / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid do /
tatra saṅkleśalakṣaṇaṃ navavidhaṃ /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam pa dgu ste /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
ityārabhya yāvat / saptadhā'bhūtakalpanāt iti /
# ces bya ba nas bzung ste / / rnam bdun yang dag min rtog las / / zhes bya ba'i bar du'o /
śeṣeṇārdhena vyavadānalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ / / yadi lakṣyante'neneti laksaṇam ityevaṃ sati lakṣaṇasya
# lhag ma ni rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid du bstan to / / gal te 'dis mtshon par byed pas mtshan nyid ces bya na /
saṅkleśavyavadānabhedo bhaved iti naitad evaṃ /
# de lta na ni mtshan nyid kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang tha dad par 'gyur ro zhe na /
svabhāva eva hi bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ / / tad yathā pṛthivīdhātuḥ kharalakṣaṇo na ca kharatvāt pṛthivīdhātuḥ
# de ni de lta ma yin te dngos po rnams kyi rang bzhin nyid mtshan nyid de / / dper na sa'i khams kyi mtshan nyid ni sra ba ste /
pṛthagastīti / / atha vā lakṣyate tad iti lakṣaṇaṃ /
# sra ba nyid las sa'i khams gud na med pa lta bu'o; / / yang na des mtshon par bya bas mtshan nyid de /
evaṃ hi saṅkleśo vyavadānañca saṅkleśavyavadānātmatvena lakṣyata iti / lakṣaṇaṃ /
# de ltar kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba yang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i bdag nyid kyis mtshon par bya bas mtshan nyid du 'gyur ro /
atha vā dvayoḥ saṅkleśavyavadānayor lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ svalakṣaṇañca
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis las mtshan nyid rnam pa gnyis te /
sāmānyalakṣaṇañca / / āvaraṇam iti / / āvṛṇoti kuśalān dharmānāvriyante'nena kuśaladharmā utpattivibandhāt
# rang gi mtshan nyid dang spyi'i mtshan nyid do / / sgrib pa zhes bya ba ni dge ba'i chos rnams la sgrib par byed pa'am / / 'dis dge ba'i chos rnams bsgrib pas sgrib pa ste /
ityāvaraṇaṃ / / tat punas tripañcāśat prakāraṃ / / tattvam iti /
# skye ba la bgegs byed pa'i phyir sgrib pa'o / / de yang lnga bcu rtsa gsum mo /
tadevedaṃ tat tasya bhāvas tattvam aviparyāsa ityarthaḥ /
# de kho na zhes bya ba ni 'di nyid de yin pas de'o / / de'i dngos po ni de kho na ste / / phyin ci ma log ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tac ca daśa prakāraṃ / [p.8] / vipakṣaprahāṇārthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ / / sa sārgaḥ /
# de yang rnam pa bcu'o / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs spangs pa'i phyir / / phyogs ni gnyen po ste de ni lam mo /
tadabhyāso bhāvanā / / avasthā tasyaiva santānenotpattiviśeṣaḥ /
# de goms par bya ba ni bsgom pa'o; / / gnas skabs ni de nyid rgyun gyis skye ba'i khyad par ro /
sā punar ekānnaviṃśatiprakārā gotrāvasthādikā / / phalasya lābhaḥ phalaprāptiḥ /
# de yang rnam par bcu dgu ste / / rigs kyi gnas la sogs pa'o / / 'bras bu thob pa ni 'bras bu rnyed pa'o /
tat punaḥ pañcadaśaprakāraṃ vipākaphalādi /
# de yang rnam pa bco lnga ste / / rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu la sogs pa'o /
yānānuttartham iti / / gamyate'neneti yānaṃ /
# theg pa bla na med pa zhes bya ba ni 'dis 'gro bas theg pa ste /
yānac ca tadānuttaryañceti yānānuttaryaṃ /
# de ni theg pa yang yin la bla na med pa yang yin pas theg pa bla na med pa'o /
tat punastrividhaṃ pratipattyānuttaryādi /
# de yang rnam pa gsum ste / / bsgrub pa bla na med pa la sogs pa'o /
saptamo'rtha iti niyamārtham anukramārthañcāha /
# don bdun pa zhes bya ba ni / / nges pa'i don dang go rims kyi don du smos pa ste /
etāvanta evārthā nirdiśyante nāto'nya iti / / anukramaḥ punar ayaṃ lokottarajñānānukūlyārthaḥ /
# don 'di rnams 'dir bshad kyi de las gzhan ma yin no / / yang go rims 'di ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes dang mthun pa'i phyir te /
tathā hi bodhisattvenādhimukticaryābhūmisthitena śīlapratiṣṭhitena
# 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' mos pas spyod pa la gnas pa / / tshul khrims la rab tu gnas pas /
prathamaṃ saṅkleśavyavadānakuśalena bhavitavyaṃ /
# thog mar kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba la mkhas par bya'o /
tataḥ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya yad āvaraṇaṃ tasya taj jñeyaṃ /
# de'i 'og tu dge ba'i chos rnams kyi gang gis sgrib pa gang yin pa de shes par bya ste /
tasyāprahāṇād vimukter asambhavād avijñānañca prahātuṃ na śakyate / doṣadarśanāt /
# de ma spangs na rnam par grol mi srid la / / rnam par mi shes na yang nyes pa ma mthong bas spong mi nus so /
tatas tadāvaraṇād yenālambanena cittaṃ vimucyate tatttvaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# de'i 'og tu sgrib pa de las dmigs pa gang gis sems rnam par grol bar 'gyur ba de ni de kho na yin par khong du chud par bya'o /
tatastenālambhanenatadāvaraṇasya yena prayogena kṣayo bhavati sā / pratipakṣabhāvanā jñeyā/
# de'i 'og tu dmigs pa des sgrib pa de sbyor ba gang gis zad par 'gyur ba de gnyen po bsgom par shes par bya'o /
tatas tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvāyāṃ vipakṣahānyā pratipakṣavṛddhyā
# de'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa ni de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs 'bri ba dang gnyen po 'phel ba la gnas skabs su shes par bya ste /
cā'vasthā jñeyā gotrāvasthādikā /
# rigs kyi gnas skabs la sogs pa'o /
tato lokottaradharmābhimukhīkaraṇaṃ phalāni srota apatti phalādīni
# de'i 'og tu 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos mngon du gyur pa ni 'bras bu rnams te /
veditavyāni / / sarvam apyetat srottaratvācchrāvakādibhiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ / / yathoktaṃ sūtre - / sa pravrajitaḥ śrāvakaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate
# rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la sogs par shes par bya'o / / de dag thams cad kyang bla ma dang bcas pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang nyan thos la sogs pa dang thun mong ste / / mdo las ji skad du / / rab tu byung ba de nyan thos kyi bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la yang slob po /
pratyekabuddhaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate
# rang sangs rgyas kyi bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la slob po /
bodhisattvaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate / / bodhisattvānāṃ tvānuttaryam asādhāraṇaṃ / / saptamo'rtha ānuttaryaṃ /
# byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang yang dag par spyod pa la yang slob po zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ni bla na med pa thun mong ma yin pa ste don bdun pa bla na med pa'o /
anyastvāha / / saṅkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇe kauśalotpādanārtham ādau laksaṇaṃ /
# gzhan na re kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid la mkhas par bya ba bskyed pa'i phyir thog mar mtshan nyid do /
tatra yaḥ saṅkleśas tadāvaraṇaṃ /
# de la kun nas nyon mongs pa gang yin pa de ni / / sgrib pa'o /
yad vyavadānaṃ tat tattvaṃ /
# rnam par byang ba gang yin pa de ni de kho na'o /
āvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ ca tattvādhigamād bhavatītyata āvaraṇatattvaṃ / / tat prahāṇopāyapradarśanārthaṃ tataḥ saparivāraḥ pratipakṣo mārgaḥ / / tasya mārgasyādimadhyānteṣu mṛdumadhyādhimātraprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ
# de kho na nyid khong du chud pas sgrib pa spong bar 'gyur te / / de'i phyir sgrib pa dang de kho na'o / / de spang ba'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir / / de'i 'og tu gnyen po 'khor dang bcas pa ni lam mo / / lam de'i thog ma dang bar ma dang tha mal chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po rab tu dbye bar bstan pa'i phyir de'i gnas skabs so /
tatrāvasthā / / avasthānurūpaṃ phalamāvahatīti tad anantaraṃ phalaṃ /
# gnas skabs dang mthun pa'i 'bras bu thob par byed pas / / de'i 'og tu 'bras bu'o /
etac ca sarvaṃ bodhisattvasya śrāvakādisādhāraṇam ity
# de dag thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos la sogs pa dang thun mong ste /
asādhāraṇa-mahāyānanayaprakāśanārthaṃ yānānuttaryam iti / / apare punar āhuḥ /
# de bas na thun mong ma yin pa dang theg pa chen po'i tshul rab tu bstan pa'i phyir bla na med pa zhes bya'o zer ro /
sadasal lakṣaṇajñāpanārthaṃ prathamato lakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re yod pa dang med pa'i mtshan nyid shes par bya ba'i phyir thog mar mtshan nyid bshad do /
lakṣaṇaṃ jñātvāvaraṇaṃ prahātavyaṃ tattvaṃ ca sākṣāt kartavyam iti tad / anantaram āvaraṇatattvaṃ / [p.9]
# mtshan nyid shes nas sgrib pa spang bar bya ba dang de kho na mngon sum du bya bas de'i 'og tu sgrib pa dang de kho na'o /
tayoś ca prahāṇasākṣātkaraṇayor ayam upāya iti pratipakṣabhāvanā / / tasyāś ca tāratamyam avasthāviśeṣaḥ / / tat kṛtañca prahāṇaṃ phalaṃ / / tad anantaraṃ yānānuttaryam iti prakāśanārtham ayam anukrama iti /
# de gnyis spang ba dang mngon du bya ba'i thabs ni 'di yin te / / gnyen po bsgom pa'o / / de'i 'bring dang mchog ni gnas skabs kyi khyad par ro / / des spang bar bya ba ni 'bras bu'o / / de'i 'og tu theg pa bla na med pa'o zhes bya bar rab tu bstan pa'i phyir 'di ni go rims so zhes zer ro /
anyacca sattvasya sadasad dharmasaṃmohāpavādasamāropaprahāṇārthaṃ / lakṣaṇanirdeśaḥ / / prahīṇasaṃmohasyāvaraṇakauśalārtham āvaraṇaṃ /
# gzhan yang sems pa yod pa dang med pa'i chos la rmongs nas / / skur pa 'debs pa dang sgro 'dogs pa spang ba'i phyir mtshan nyid bshad do / / rmongs pa spangs nas sgrib pa la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir sgrib pa'o /
tenāvṛtaṃ tattvam iti tattvakauśalārthaṃ tad anantaraṃ tattvaṃ /
# des de kho na bsgribs pas de kho na la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir de'i 'og tu de kho na'o /
tattvapratividdhabhāvanayāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ bhavatīti tattvānantaraṃ / pratipakṣabhāvanā /
# de kho na rab tu rtogs pa bsgoms pas sgrib pa spong bar 'gyur bas de kho na'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa'o /
tat prabhedakauśalārtham avasthā /
# de'i dbye ba la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir gnas skabs so /
avasthayāṃ phalaṃ prabhāvitavyam ityavasthānantaraṃ phalaṃ tat / kauśalotpādanārthaṃ /
# gnas skabs kyis 'bras bu rab tu phye bas de la mkhas par bya ba bskyed pa'i phyir gnas skabs kyi 'og tu 'bras bu'o /
sarvam etan mahāyānamāgamyeti yānānuttaryam ante nirdiṣṭaṃ //1-1// / tatra lakṣaṇam ārabhyāha -
# de dag thams cad kyang theg pa chen po la brten pas theg pa bla na med pa tha mar bshad do snyam mo / / de la mtshan nyid las brtsams nas /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / / śūnyatā vidyate tv atra tasyām api sa vidyate // iti /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod / / de la yang ni de yod do / / zhes bya bar gsungs so zhes bya ba la /
tatreti lakṣaṇāvaraṇādisaptārtheṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu lakṣaṇam adhikṛtyoddiśyāha
# de la zhes bya ba ni mtshan nyid dang sgrib pa la sogs pa dngos po bdun smos pa dag gi nang nas mtshan nyid las brtsams nas de'i dbang du mdzad de /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti /
# de'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
yathoddiśas tathā nirdeśa iti kṛtvā /
# ces bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / ji ltar bstan pa de bzhin du bshad de /
lakṣaṇañca prāg uddiṣṭamatastasyaiva śeṣebhyo nirdeśaḥ prāgārabhyate /
# thog mar mtshan nyid bstan pas de'i phyir lhag ma rnams pas de nyid bshad pa sngar brtsam mo /
kecit virundhanti sarvadharmāḥ sarvathā niḥsvabhāvāḥ śaśaviśāṇavad / ityataḥ sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārthamāha -
# la la dag chos thams cad ri bong gi rva ltar rang bzhin ye med do / / snyam du sems pa de'i phyir thams cad la skur ba dgag pa'i don du /
abhūtaparikalpo'stīti / / svabhāvata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya bar gsungs te / / rang bzhin gyi zhes bya ba tshig gi lhag ma'o /
nanv evaṃ sūtravirodhaḥ - sarvadharmāḥ śūnyā iti śāstre vacanāt / / nāsti virodhaḥ yasmāt - / dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate /
# de ltar na mdo las chos thams cad stong pa'o zhes bshad pas / / mdo dang mi 'gal lam zhe na / / mi 'gal te 'di ltar / / de la gnyis po yod ma yin /
abhūtaparikalpo hi grāhyagrāhakasvarūparahitaḥ śūnya ucyate na tu / sarvathā niḥsvabhāvaḥ / / ato na sūtravirodhaḥ / / yadyevaṃ dvayaṃ śaśaviṣāṇavat sarvathā nāsti /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i ngo bo dang bral bas stong pa zhes bya ba'i rang bzhin ye med pa ni ma yin te / / de'i phyir mdo dang mi 'gal lo / / gal te de ltar gnyis po ni ri bong gi rva ltar ye med la /
abhūtaparikalpaś ca paramārthataḥ svabhāvato'styevaṃ
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa ni / / don dam par rang bzhin gyis yod na /
śūnyatā'bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ /
# de lta na ni stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro zhe na /
naitad evaṃ yasmāt - [p.10] / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra
# de ni de lta ma yin te 'di ltar / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod /
iyam eva hi -śūnyatā yā grāhagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpasyeti na
# yang dag ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa nyid gang yin pa de stong pa nyid yin pas stong pa nyid med par mi 'gyur ro /
śūnyatāyā nāstitvaṃ bhavati /
# gal te gnyis po med pa stong pa nyid yin la /
yadyadvayā śūnyatā sā cābhūtaparikalpe'sti kasmād vayamamuktāḥ / / vidyamānā ca kasmān na gṛhyata iti saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ - / tasyām api sa vidyate /
# de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa la yod na / / ci'i phyir bdag cag ma grol / / yod na yang ci'i phyir ma rtogs snyam pa'i dogs pa bsal ba'i phyir / / de la yang ni de yod do /
ityāha / / yasmācchūnyatāyām apyabhūtaparikalpo vidyate tasmād bhavanto na
# zhes bya ba gsungs te / / 'di ltar stong pa nyid la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod pas de'i phyir khyed ma grol lo /
muktāḥ / / ata eva ca samalatvān na prasannābdhātavad gṛhyate /
# de bas na dri ma dang bcas pas chu'i khams dangs pa bzhin rtogs par mi rung ngo /
atha vā cittacaittebhyo'nyatra rūpādayo dravyatvena santīti yad darśanaṃ / tat pratiṣedhārtham āha -
# yang na sems can dang sems las byung ba rnams dang gzugs dang rdzas nyid du yod par gang dag lta ba de dgag pa'i phyir /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
dravyataḥ / / nāsti rūpaṃ tad vyatiriktaṃ dravyata iti /
# ces gsungs te de nyid rdzas su yod do / / gzugs ni de las logs shig na yang med la /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# rdzas su yang med do /
yasmāt - / dvayaṃtatra na vidyate /
# ci'i phyir zhe na / / 'di ltar de la gnyis po yod ma yin /
na hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kasyacid grāhako nāpi kenacit gṛhyate / / kiṃ tarhi grāhyagrāhakatvaṃ bhāvamātram eva /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni ci la yang 'dzin pa ma yin / / sus kyang gzung bar bya ba ma yin gyi / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i dngos po tsam nyid de /
yato vijñānād bahī rūpādayo na gṛhyante / / svapnāadivad vijñānaṃ rūpādyābhāsam utapdyate /
# 'di ltar rnam par shes pa las phyi rol na gzugs la sogs pa gzung ba med par rmi lam la sogs pa bzhin du / / gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ngo /
na ca yad yasya kāraṇaṃ tad abhāve tasyotpattir yujyate /
# gal te rgyu yin na de med par de 'byung bar mi rung ngo /
tasmān nirālambanam eva svapnādāviva /
# de'i phyir dmigs pa med pa nyid de / / da rmi lam la sogs pa bzhin no /
anyatrāpi svabījaparipākād arthābhāsaṃ vijñānam utpadyate ity / avaseyaṃ /
# gzhan la yang rang gi sa bon yongs su smin pa las don du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar shes par bya'o /
grāhyābhāve grāhakasyābhāvād grāhye'sati grāhako bhavituṃ na
# gzung ba med na 'dzin pa med par 'gyur bas gzung ba med na 'dzin pa yod par mi rung ste /
yujyate / / tasmān na rūpam abhūtaparikalpāt pṛthag asti /
# de bas na gzugs ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa las gud na yod pa ma yin no /
yadi tarhi grāhyabhāvastena viśuddhyālambanābhāvān mokṣābhāvaḥ /
# gal te gzung ba med na de'i phyir rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa med pas thar pa yang med par 'gyur ro zhe na /
naitad evaṃ yasmāt - / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / 'di ltar / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod /
tu śabdo yasmād arthaḥ / / śūnyatā hi vuśuddhyālambanā /
# ni zhes bya ba'i sgra ni gang gi phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / stong pa nyid ni rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa ste /
sā ca grāhyagrāhakarahitatā 'bhūtapraikalpe'stīti na mokṣābhāvaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba nyid de / / de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la yod pas thar pa med par mi 'gyur ro /
yady abhūtaparikalpe'sti sā vidyamānā kimarthaṃ na gṛhyate /
# gal te yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa la yod na / / de yod pas ci'i phyir mi rtogs she na /
abhūtaparikalpāvṛtatvān na gṛhyata ākāśanairmalyavat na tu asattvād / iti pratipādayann āha -
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pas bsgribs pas nam mkha' dri ma med pa bzhin du rtogs par mi rung gi med pa ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir; de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba gsungs so /
tasyām api sa vidyata iti / / atha vā sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārtham āha - [p.11] / abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti /
# yang na thams cad la skur ba 'debs pa dgag pa'i phyir / / yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod / / ces bya ba gsungs te /
na sarvam asat nāpi sadātmakaṃ vijñānapariṇāmāatmanā'stīti kṛtvā /
# rnam par shes pa gyur ba'i bdag nyid yod pas / / thams cad med pa yang ma yin bdag nyid yod pa yang ma yin no /
ye tu manyante yathaiva rūpādayaḥ prakhyāyante tathiavābhūtaparikalpāt / svabhāvataḥ pṛthag vidyanta iti tān pratyāha / abhūtasamāropapratiṣedhārthaṃ -
# gang dag sems pa gzugs la sogs pa ji ltar snang ba de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa las logs shig na rang bzhin du yod do zhes / / yod pa ma yin pa la sgro 'dogs pa dgag pa'i don du de'i phyir /
dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate / iti /
# de la gnyis po yod ma yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
abhūtaparikalpamātraṃ vidyata ityabhiprāyaḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam yod par dgongs pa'o /
kenacit dvayor abhāvo vo vnadhyāputravat cheda rūpo gṛhyate / / anyair antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā dharmāṇāṃ śūnyate'tyucyate / / ataḥ śūnyatāpavādapratiṣedhārthaṃ bhūtanairātmyakhyāpanārthañcāha / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iti / / yadyabhūtaparikalpe śūnyatāstyevaṃ sati sarvaprāṇinām aprayatnena
# kha cig gnyis po med pa ni mo gsham gyi bu bzhin du dngos po med de zhes chad pa'i dngos po'i ngo bor 'dzin pa dang gzhan dag nang na byed pa'i skyes bu med pa nyid ni / / chos rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes smra ba de'i phyir / / stong pa nyid du skur pa 'debs pa dgag pa'i don dang bdag med pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod ces bya ba gsungs so / / gal te yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la stong pa nyid yod na de lta na ni /
mokṣaprasaṅgaḥ / / nāsyetad yasmāt - / tasyām api sa vidyate /
# bsgrim mi dgos par srog chags thams cad thar bar 'gyur ro zhe na / / de lta ma yin te 'di ltar / / de la yang ni de yod do /
na hyaviśodhitāyāṃ śūnyatāyāṃ mokṣo'sti saṅkliṣṭā ca mahatā yatnena
# stong pa nyid kyang rnam par ma sbyangs kyi bar du thar pa med pa'i phyir te / / kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa ni /
viśodhyata iti nāsty ayatnena mokṣaḥ /
# 'bad pa chen pos rnam par sbyang dgos pas 'bad pa ma byas par thar pa med do /
atha vā lakṣaṇaṃ saṅkleśavyavadānābhidhānād anyan nāstītyataḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇapradarśanārthamāha -
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dag gi mtshan nyid brjod pa las gzhan med pas de'i phyir kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid bstan pa'i don du /
abhūtaparikalpo'sti
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog yod /
iti vistaraḥ /
# ces rgya cher gsungs so /
abhūtaparikalpasvabhāvaḥ saṃkleśo bhrāntilakṣaṇatvāt /
# 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rang bzhin ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'o /
katham etaj jñātavyaṃ bhrāntilakṣaṇam iti ?
# 'di 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid du ji ltar shes par bya zhe na /
yena - / dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate
# 'di ltar de la gnyis po yod ma yin /
svātmanyavidhyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa pratyānād / bhrāntisvarūpeṇa jñayate/
# bdag nyid du med par gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang bas 'khrul ba'i ngo bo nyid du mngon ngo /
edāniṃ vyavadānasvarūpapradarṣana arthamāḥ - / śūnyatā vidyate tvatra
# da ni rnam par byang ba'i ngo bo brtag pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid ni 'di la yod /
iti/ / śūnyatāsvabhāvo hi vyavadānaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāt / / atra ca śūnyatāprabhāvitatvāt mārganirodhayor api grahaṇamṃ veditavyaṃ
# ces bya ba gsungs so / / gnyis po med pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin ni rnam pa byang ba'o / / stong pa nyid kyis rab tu phye bas lam dang 'gog pa dag kyang 'dir bsdu bar rig par bya'o /
saṅkleśapakṣād eva vyavadānapakṣo mārgayitavyo na punaḥ pṛthaktvam / asyāstīti pradarśanārtham āha atreti /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs nyid las rnam par byang ba'i phyogs nyid btsal bar bya ba'i rang gi rgyud gud na med par rab tu bstan pa'i phyir 'di la zhes bya ba gsungs so /
yadi dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ tasyāṃ vidyamānāyāṃ loko bhrānta ityāha - / tasyām api sa vidyate iti /
# gal te gnyis po med na ci'i phyir de yod par 'jig rten 'khrul bar gyur zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba gsungs te /
grāhyagrāhakavikalpo hastyādyākāraśūnyamāyāyām iva
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o / / sgyu ma ni gang po che la sogs pas stong yang /
hastyākārādayaḥ / / abhūtam asmin dvayaṃ parikalpyate'nena vetyabhūtaparikalpaḥ / / abhūtavacanena ca yathā'yaṃ parikalpyate grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā / nāstīti pradarśayati /
# glang po che la sogs par snang ba lta bu'o / / yang dag pa ma yin pa gnyis po de la'am / / des yongs su rtog pas yang dag pa ma yin pa gnyis por yongs su rtog pas yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa'o / / yang dag pa ma yin pa'i tshig gis ni / / ji ltar 'di la gzung ba dang 'dzin par kun rtog pa de bzhin du med par ston to /
parikalpavacanena tvartho yathā parikalpyate tathārtho na vidhyate iti / pradarṣayati/
# kun rtog pa'i tshig gis ni don ji lta bur kun rtog pa don de lta bur yod pa ma yin zhes ston te /
evam asya grāhyagrāhakavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati / / kaḥ punar asau ?
# de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa las rnam par grol ba de'i mtshan nyid bshad pa yin no /
atītānāgatavartamānā hetuphalabhūtās traidhātukā anādikālikā / nirvāṇaparyavasānāḥ saṃsārānurūpāścittacaittā / aviśeṣeṇābhūtaparikalpaḥ /
# de yang gang yin zhe na sems dang sems las byung ba 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi dang rgyu dang 'bras bur gyur pa dang khams gsum pa dang thog ma med pa'i dus can dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i mthar thug pa dan / / 'khor ba'i rjes su mthun pa dag ni / / khyad par med par yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'o /
viśeṣeṇa [p.12] / tu grāhyagrāhakavikalpaḥ / / tatra grāhyavikalpo'rthasattvapratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ / / grāhakavikalpa ātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ /
# khyad par ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa rnam par rtog pa'o / / de la gzung bar rnam par rtog pa ni; don dang sems can du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'o / / 'dzin par rnam par rtog pa ni bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba'o /
dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañceti / / tatra grāhyaṃ rūpādi / / grāhakaṃ cakṣūr vijñānādi /
# gnyis po ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba de la gzung ba ni gzugs la sogs pa'o / / 'dzin pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa'o /
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena virahitatā viviktatā hyabhūtaparikalpasya / śanyatā /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po dang bral ba nyid de / / dben pa nyid ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i stong pa nyid yin gyi /
na tv abhūtaparikalpo'pyabhāvaḥ yathā śūnyā rajjuḥ sarpasvabhāvenātat
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yang med pa ni ma yin te / / dper na thag pa ni sprul pa'i dngos po stong ste /
svabhāvatvāt sarvakālaṃ śūnyā na tu rajju svabhāvena tathehāpi /
# de'i rang bzhin ma yin pas dus thams cad du stong pa nyid yin gyi / / thag pa'i dngos po ni ma yin te / / 'dir yang de bzhin no /
tasyām api sa vidyata iti abhūtaparikalpaḥ / / evaṃ hy āgantukāvaraṇopakliṣṭatvāt tad agrahaṇam uktam abdhātvādivad  iti /
# de la yang ni de yod do zhes bya ba ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ste / / de ltar glo bur gyi sgrib pas nyon mongs pa'i phyir / / de chu khams la sogs pa bzhin du rtogs par mi rung ngo zhes bstan pa yin no /
evaṃ yad yatra nāsti tat tena śūnyam iti yathābhūtaṃ samanupaśyatīti / / kiṃ kutra nāsti ?
# de ltar gang na gang med pa de ni / / des stong par yang dag par rjes su mthong ngo zhes bya ba la / / ci zhig gang na med ce na /
abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po ste /
ato'bhūtaparikalpaṃ dvayena śūnyaṃ paśyati /
# de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis kyis stong par mthong ngo /
yat punar atrā'vaśiṣṭaṃ tat sat / / kiṃ punar ihāvaśiṣṭaṃ ?
# 'di la lhag ma gang yin pa de ni yod pa de 'di la lhag ma gang yin zhe na /
abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca / / tad ubhayam ihāstītyanādhyāropānapavādena paśyan yathābhūtaṃ
# yang dag ma yin pa kun rtog pa stong pa nyid dang de gnyi ga yang 'dir yod par ma skur ba dang sgro btags pa med par mthong na yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so /
prajānāti / / tatrābhūtaparikalpe'dvayadarśanād anadhyāropaḥ / / abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāścāstitvadarśanād anapavādaḥ /
# de la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po med par mthong ba'i phyir sgro mi 'dogs so / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa dang stong pa nyid yod par mthong ba'i phyir te /
aviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇam udbhāvitaṃ bhavati / / yac chūnyaṃ tasya sad bhāvāt yena śūnyaṃ tasya tatrābhāvāt / / sarvabhāve sarvābhāve vā nāviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ /
# skur pa mi 'debs te / / stong pa nyid gang yin pa de yod pa dang gang gis stong pa de de la med pa'i phyir / / stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid phyin ci ma log par bstan pa yin no /
śūnyatāyā evābhāvaprasaṅgāt / / na śūnyasaṃjñā'satyāṃ śūunyatāyāṃ yujyate /
# thams cad med pa'am thams cad yod pa ni stong pa nyid kyang mtshan nyid phyin ci log yin te /
dharmatāyā hi bhāvāyāt tattvād anityatvādivat / / dvayam astīti śūnyatābhāvaḥ /
# stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro / / stong pa zhes bya ba med na stong pa nyid du mi rung ste /
yadi śaśaviṣāṇakalpanena dvayaṃ kathaṃ tenābhūtaparikalpasya
# chos nyid ni dngos po la rag lus pa'i phyir mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa bzhin no / / gnyis po yod do zhe na /
śūnyatāsambhavaḥ ?
# stong pa nyid med par 'gyur ro /
anyena hy anyasya śūunyatā dṛṣṭā yathā bhikṣubhir vihārasya / / naitad evaṃ /
# gal te gnyis po ni ri bong gi ra dang 'dren yang ji ltar des yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa stong ste /
yathā rajjur māyā vā svātmany avidyamānena sarpākāreṇa puruṣādinā / prabhāsate / / tatra kasyacid grāhanirvartanārthaṃ sarpapuruṣādibhiś ca śūnyety ucyate
# dper na dge slong rnams kyis gtsug lag khang bzhin du gzhan gyis gzhan stong par mthong zhe na; dper na thag pa la'am sgyu ma la bdag nyid kyis med par sbrul gyi rnam pa dang skyes bu la sogs pa lta bur snang ba de la kha cig 'dzin pa bzlog pa'i phyir / / sbrul dang skyes bu la sogs pas stong ngo zhes brjod pa de bzhin du /
evam abhūtaparikalpo'pi svātmany avidyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa / prakhyāyamāno bālānāṃ tad grāhābhiniveśaty ājanārthaṃ dvayena
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa la yang bdag nyid kyis med par gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang ba de la byis pa rnams 'dzin cing mngon par zhen pa dor bar bya ba'i phyir gnyis kyis ston zhes bshad do /
śūnyam ity ucyate //1-2// [p.13] / na śūnyaṃ nā'pi cā'śūnyaṃ iti / / kim artham asau śloka ārabdha iti ? / sarvasya saṃskṛtasyāsaṃskṛtasya ca dvayarahitatājñāpanārthaṃ /
# stong pa ma yin mi stong min / / zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di ci'i phyir brtsams she na / / 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas thams cad gnyis dang bral ba nyid du shes par bya ba'i phyir ro /
evaṃ ca hyekāntapratikṣepeṇa sarvam idaṃ na śūnyaṃ nāśūnyam iti / prajñāpāramitāpāṭhābhiprāyatāviṣkṛtā bhavati /
# de ltar mtha' gcig bkag pas 'di thams cad stong pa yang ma yin mi stong pa yang ma yin pa zhes shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i nang nas bshad pa'i dgongs pa bstan pa yin no /
anyathā pūrvāparaviruddham etat syāt /
# gzhan du na ltag 'og 'gal bar 'gyur ro /
kiñca madhyamāpratipat prakāśanārthaṃ /
# gzhan yang dbu ma'i lam rab tu bstan pa'i phyir te /
anyathaikāntikaśūnyataivāśanyānto vā syāt /
# gzhan du na ni gcig tu stong pa kho na'am / / mi stong pa'i mthar 'gyur ro /
apavādasamāropapratiṣedhopasaṃhārārthaṃ vā'syārambhaḥ /
# yang na skur pa 'debs pa dang sgro 'dogs pa dgag pa bshad ma thag pa mjug bsdu ba'i don du de brtsams so /
hetupratyayapratibaddhātmalābhād abhūtaparikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ / / śūnyatā punas tan nirapekṣatvād asaṃskṛtaṃ /
# rgyu dang rkyen dang 'brel pa las skyes pa'i phyir / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni 'dus byas te / / de la mi ltos pa'i phyir stong pa nyid ni 'dus ma byas so /
vidhīyate prajñāpāramitādimadhye paṭhyate /
# bshad pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa'i nang nas 'byung ba'o /
sattvād abhūtaparikalpasya na saṃskṛtaṃ śūnyam abhūtaparikalpātmatvena
# yod pas zhes bya ba ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ste / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i bdag nyid kyis 'dus byas stong pa ma yin no /
asatvād dvayasya /
# med pas zhes bya ba ni gnyis po ste /
grāhyagrāhakātmanā śūnyaṃ / / śūnyātāyās tu sarvam abhūtaparikalpe tad dharmateti kṛtvā / / śūnyatāyām apy abhūtaparikalpo dharmirūpeṇa vidyate / / evam asaṃskṛtam api dharmatārūpeṇa na śūnyaṃ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyis stong pa'o / / stong pa nyid ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la de'i chos nyid du yod de / / stong pa nyid la yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa chos can gyi ngo bor yod do / / de ltar 'dus ma byas kyang chos nyid kyi ngo bos stong pa ma yin te /
abhāvasaṃjñakena dvayena svarūpaśūnyaṃ /
# dngos po med ces bya ba gnyis kyi ngo bos stong pa'o /
sā ca madhyamā pratipad iti ratnakūṭādimadhye'stīti kāśyapāyam / eko'ntaḥ / / nāstītyayaṃ dvitīyo'ntaḥ /
# de ni dbu ma'i lam yin no zhes bya ba ni dkon mchog brtsegs pa la sogs pa'i nang nas / / 'od srungs yod ces bya ba 'di ni mtha' gcig go / / med ces bya ba 'di ni mtha' gnyis te /
yadetayor dvayor antayor madhyamiyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad
# 'od srungs mtha' gnyis po 'di dag gi dbus gang yin pa 'di ni chos rnams la yang dag par so sor rtog pa'o zhes 'byung ba gang yin pa ste /
dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti sā madhyamā pratipadevam anulomitā / / sarvam iti saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca /
# de ltar dbu ma'i lam de dang mthun par byas pa yin no / / thams cad ces bya ba ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas so /
naikāntena śūnyam ity abhūtaparikalpasya tac chūnyatāyāś ca [p.14] / sadbhāvāt /
# gcig tu stong pa yang ma yin zhes bya ba ni / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog dang de la stong pa nyid kyang yod pa'i phyir ro /
nāpyekāntenāśūnyaṃ dvayasyābhāvāt /
# gcig tu mi stong pa yang ma yin pa ni gnyis po med pa'i phyir ro /
sarvanāstitvaṃ sarvāstitvaṃ vā'nta eva syāt /
# thams cad yod pa'am thams cad med pa ni mtha' nyid du 'gyur gyi /
na madhyamā pratipad //1-3// / evam abhūtaparikalpasya sal lakṣaṇam asallakṣaṇañca khyāpayitveti /
# dbu ma'i lam ma yin no / / de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i yod pa'i mtshan nyid dang med pa'i mtshan nyid brjod nas zhes bya ba 'di /
idaṃ sattvena lakṣyata iti sattvam eva sallakṣaṇaṃ /
# yod par nye bar mtshon pas yod pa nyid / / yod pa'i mtshan nyid de /
abhūtaparikalpo vidyata ity anenābhūtaparikalpasya sattvaṃ / pradarśayatīty arthaḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod ces bya ba des yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod par ston zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
evam asattvena lakṣyata iti asatvam evāsal lakṣaṇāt /
# de bzhin du med par nye bar mtshon pas med pa nyid med pa'i mtshan nyid de /
tat punar yad grāhyagrāhakabhāvenāsattvaṃ /
# de yang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po med pa ste /
yasmād abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāsti tasmād abhūtaparikalpo'pi / dvayātmanā nāstīty uktaṃ bhavati /
# 'di ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la gnyis po med pas de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yang gnyis kyi bdag nyid kyis yod pa ma yin no zhes bstan pa yin no /
svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti / / ko viśeṣo'sti sallakṣaṇasvalakṣaṇayoḥ ? / sallakṣaṇaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid brjod de zhes bya ba la yod pa'i mtshan nyid dang rang gi mtshan nyid gnyis khyad par ci yod ce na / / yod pa'i mtshan nyid ni spyi'i'o /
svalakṣaṇam tu viśeṣaḥ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid ni bye brag yin no /
yadi svalakṣaṇam anākhyātamatra kiṃ syāt ?
# gal te rang gi mtshan nyid ma bshad na ci zhig tu 'gyur zhe na /
śarīram abhūtaparikalpasya noktaṃ syāt / / atas tac charīrapratipādanārtham ucyate - / arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i lus ma bshad par 'gyur te / / de bas na de'i lus khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir / / don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni / / rab tu skye'o de'i don med /
vijñānaṃ nāsti cā'syārthas tadabhāvāt tadapyasat // iti / / atha vā grāhyagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpamātrate'ty ucciṣṭaṃ / / tasyām abhūtaparikalpamātratāyām indriyaviṣayavijñānaṃ yathā
# de med pas na de yang med / / ces bya ba gsungs so / / yang na gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa'i yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam nyid yod do zhes bstan pa yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam de la /
vyavasthitaṃ na jñāyata / / abhūtaparikalpapratibhāsabhedena tad vyavasthitajñāpanārtham
# dbang po dang yul dang rnam par shes pa ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa mi shes pas yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i snang ba tha dad pa de la rnam par gzhag go zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir /
abhūtaparikalpasya svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati - / arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid bshad de / / don dang sems can bdag rnam rig /
iti vistaraḥ / [p.15]
# snang ba'i zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o; /
atha vā 'bhūtaparikalpo'stītyanena tat sattvamātraṃ jñāyate na tu / tat svabhāvaḥ /
# yang na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod ces bya ba des de yod pa tsam du shes par byed kyi /
dvayābhāve'pi yad grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśakāraṇaṃ na vijñāyate dvayaṃ / ca nāstīti yataḥ pratīyate tad api noktam ityatas tat pratipādanārtham
# de'i rang bzhin ni ma yin pa dang gnyis po med par yang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa'i rgyu gang yin pa rnam par mi shes pa dang gang gi phyir gnyis po med par yid ches par bya ba de yang ma bshad pas de bstan pa'i phyir /
āha - / arthasattvātmavijñapti pratibhāsaṃ / iti vistaraḥ /
# don dang sems can bdag rnam rig / / snang ba'i zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
tatra vijñānasvabhāvo'bhūtaparikalpaḥ /
# de la yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin no /
tac ca vijñānaṃ sasamprayogam abhipretaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa de yang 'dir mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas par dgongs te /
pradhānena tu vijñānaṃ gṛhītaṃ / / sa eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśo'rthasattvādipratibhāsanibandhanaḥ /
# gtso bor ni rnam par shes pa gzung ngo / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa de nyid kyi rgyu ni don dang sems can la sogs par snang ba'o /
nāsti cāsyārthas tadabhāvāt tad apyasat / iti / / dvayābhāvakāraṇaṃ / / tatrārthasattvapratibhāsamālayavijñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ /
# de'i don med de med pas na de yang med ces bya ba ni gnyis po med pa'i rgyu'o / / de la don dang sems can du snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ste /
tac ca vipākatvād avyākṛtam eva /
# de yang rnam par smin pa'i phyir lung du ma bstan pa nyid do /
ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ sasaṃprayogaṃ / / tac ca nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ kleśasaṃprayuktatvād uktaṃ /
# bdag tu snang ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o / / de yang bsgribs la lung du ma bstan pa ste / / nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir bstan pa'o /
vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaṃ sasamprayigañcakṣur / vijñānādi ṣaṭkaṃ / / tadetānyarthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsānyaṣṭau vijñānāni / sasamprayogāṇi samudayasatyasaṅgṛhītāt sahakāripratyayāpekṣād
# rnam par rig par snang ba ni / / mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa la sogs pa drug po mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'o / / don dang sems can dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba rnam par shes pa brgyad po mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa de dag ni kun 'byung ba'i bden par bsdus pa /
ālayavijñānāt yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pañcagatiṣu prabhavanti / / kaścit / kuśalā'kuśala-avyākṛtadharma-vāsanāpariṇāmaviśeṣo'sty-ālayavijñānasya
# lhan cig byed pa'i rkyen la ltos pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las ji ltar mthun mthun du 'gro ba lnga rnams su rab tu 'byung ngo / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos kyis bag chags 'gyur ba'i khyad par 'ga' zhig yod de /
yadādhipatyena parasparabhinnābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prajāyate / / katham asatyarthādau vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam utpadyate ?
# de dbang gis phan tshun tha dad par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa rab tu skye'o / / don la sogs pa med pa der snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ji ltar skye ste /
na hi puruṣe'sati sthāṇuḥ puruṣābhāso bhavatīti /
# mi med na sdong po mi snang bar mi 'gyur ba lta ba'o zhe na /
naiṣa doṣaḥ /
# de ni nyes pa ma yin te /
arthādyābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ bālā vijñānāt pṛthag / arthāstitvenā'bhiniviśante taimirikasya keśoṇḍukādivat / / tasmāt tadabhiniveśatyājanārtham ucyate - / vijñānam evedam arthādyābhāsam utpadyate taimirikāṇām iva
# don la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa la byas pa rnam par shes pa las don gud na yod par mngon par zhen te / / rab rib can la skra shad 'dzings pa la sogs pa bzhin no / / de'i phyir de la mngon par zhen pa spangs pa'i phyir / / rnam par shes pa 'di nyid don la sogs par snang bar 'byung ste /
keśoṇḍukādyābhāsaṃ vināpyarthasattvādineti / / evaṃ cāṣṭavijñānavastukaḥ paratantro'bhūtaparikalpa ity uktaṃ bhavati / / rūpādabhāveneti rūpa-śabda-gandha-rasa-spraṣṭavya dharmasvarūpeṇa / pratibhāsaṃ tadākāreṇotpannatvāt /
# rab rib can la skra shad 'dzings pa la sogs pa snang ba de bzhin du med par yang don dang sems can la sogs par snang ngo zhes brjod do / / de ltar na rnam par shes pa brgyad kyi dngos po can / / gzhan gyi dbang ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog par bshad pa yin no / / gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos por zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg pa dang chos kyi ngo bor snang ba ni de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
sattvapratibhāsaṃ yat pañcendriyatvena svaparasantānayoḥ / / pratibhāsa ity adhikṛtaṃ /
# sems can du snang ba'i dbang po lngar bdag dang gzhan gyi rgyud la gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni / / snang ba zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
adhikasaktisthānatvāt pañcasv indriyeṣu sattvākhyā /
# dbang po lnga la sems can zhes bya bar lhag par chags pa'i gnas su gyur pa ste /
tais teṣu vā sajjata iti sattvaḥ /
# de dag gis sam / / de dag la chags pas sems can te /
tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam iti / / ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ ātmamohādisamprayogād iti kliṣṭasya / manasa ātmamohenātmadṛṣṭyā ātmatṛṣṇāyā'smimānena ca nityaṃ
# de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir / / de snang ba'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o / / bdag tu snang ba zhes bya ba dang bdag tu snang ba ni bdag tu rmongs pa la sogs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir /
samprayuktatvāt [p.16] / teṣāñcātmālambanatvādy uktam ātmapratibhāsatvaṃ kliṣṭasya manasaḥ / / vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ ṣaḍ vijñānānīti / / viṣamagrāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānāt tadākārotpattitām upādāya / vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ / / nāsti cāsyārtha iti catuṣṭayasyākārasyeti /
# nyon mongs pa can gyi yid do zhes bya ba la nyon mongs pa can gyi yid ni bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag la chags pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang rtag tu mtshungs par ldan pa dang de dag kyang bdag tu dmigs pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa can gyi yid ni bdag tu snang bar rigs so / / rnam par rig par snang ba ni rnam par shes pa drug rnams so zhes bya ba ni yul 'dzin pa'i ngo bor snang bas de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir rnam par rig pa snang ngo / / de'i don med ces bya ba ni rnam pa bzhi char gyi'o /
arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca / vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt
# don dang sems can du snang ba rnam pa med pa dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba ni log par snang ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni don dang sems can du snang ba gnyis gzung ba'i ngo bor snang bas /
ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti / arthasattvapratibhāsayor grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānād / vitathapratibhāsatvāsambhavād anākāratvam evārthābhāve kāraṇaṃ / / na tv anyayor grāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānād anākāraḥ / / vitathapratibhāsatvem evārthābhāve kāraṇam uktaṃ / / ākāro hyālambanasyānityādirūpeṇa grahaṇaprakāraḥ / / sa cānayor nāsti grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānāt / / ato'nākāratvād agrāhakatvād ityarthaḥ /
# log par snang ba mi srid pa'i phyir / / rnam pa med pa nyid ni don med pa'i rgyu'o / / gzhan dag ni 'dzin pa'i ngo bor snang bas rnam pa med pa ma yin te / / log par snang ba nyid ni don med pa'i rgyu'o zhes bshad do / / rnam pa ni dmigs pa la mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i ngo bor 'dzin pa'i rnam pa yin na / / de yang de dag la med de / / gzung ba'i ngo bor snang bas de'i phyir rnam pa med pa ni 'dzin pa ma yin no zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ālambanasamvedanaṃ vākāraḥ /
# yang na dmigs pa yang dag par tshor ba la rnam pa zhes bya ste /
tac ca tayor nāstīty upalabdhyabhāvād anākāraḥ /
# de yang de dag la med pas dmigs pa med pa'i phyir rnam pa med do /
yadyubhayam apy anākāraṃ parasparabhinnasvarūpac ca rūpādivac
# gal te gnyis ka yang rnam pa med pa dang phan tshun tha dad pa'i ngo bo yin te / / gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa bzhin no /
cakṣurādivac ca evaṃ sati lokaśāstraprasiddhebhyo / rūpādibhyaścakṣurādibhyaś ca vijñānasya ko'sāvātmātiśayo yatas tān
# de lta yin na ni 'jig rten dang bstan bcos las grags pa'i gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa las rnam par shes pa rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa ci yod na / / 'di ltar de dag ni gsal la /
nirākritya tair abhinnarūpaṃ vijñānaṃ gṛhyate tad
# de dag dang tha dad pa med pa'i ngo bo rnam par shes pa ni yongs su bzung zhe na /
avyatiriktasyārthasyāsambhavāt ?
# de las lhag pa'i don mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
etad evaṃ vyavasthāpyate -
# de ni 'di ltar rnam par gzhag ste /
yasmād bhinnarthasvarūpamasannapicittāsantānapratiniyamena svabījāt
# 'di ltar tha dad pa'i don gyi ngo bo med kyang sems kyi rgyud so sor nges pas /
pratyekātmagrahītaṃ bhinnārthādipratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prasūyate /
# rnam par shes pa nyid so sos zin pa tha dad pa'i don la sogs par snang bar rang gi sa bon las rab tu 'byung ste /
tathāhi pretā apaḥ pūyapurīṣamūtrādipūrṇā dhṛtadaṇḍapāṇibhir / ubhayataḥ purusaiḥ saṃrakṣyamāṇāḥ paśyanti manuṣYādayaḥ punaḥ / svacchaśītalodakaparipūrṇā nirvibandhā ity upalabhante / / yoginaścāśubhamanasikārādy abhyastā nirantaraṃ pṛthivīṃ
# 'di ltar yi dags rnams kyis chu rnag dang phyi sa dang gcin la sogs pas gang ba dang skyes bu la gan dbyig pa thogs pa rnams kyis dogs gnyis bsrung bar mthong la / / mi la sogs pas ni chu dang ba dang bsil ba dang bkrur rung ba dang btung du rung ba dang 'jug tu rung bas gang zhig bgegs byed pa med par shes so / / rnal 'byor pa mi sdug pa yid la byed pa la sogs pa goms pas ni /
kaṅkālapūrṇāṃ paśyanti / / tathā pṛthivyādi kṛtsneṣu sarvaṃ pṛthivayādibhir vyāptaṃ paśyati / / na cārthapratibuddhātmalābhasya-arthamantareṇa-arthasvarūpād vā
# rgyun mi 'chad par sa la keng rus kyis gang bar mthong ngo / / de bzhin du sa la sogs pa zad par la thams cad sa la sogs pas khyab par mthong ngo / / don la rag las te bdag nyid thob pa ni don med par ram /
bhinnākārasya vijñānāsya prasūtir yuktā /
# don gyi rang gi ngo bo tha dad pa'i rnam pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar mi rigs so /
tasmāt tad arthamantareṇa sarvam arthasattvādinirbhāsaṃ vijñānam eva / prasūyata iti niścīyate /
# de bas na don med par yang don dang sems can la sogs pa thams cad du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid rab tu 'byung ngo zhes bya bar nges so /
grāhyābhāve dvayor ātmavijñaptipratibhāsayor grāhakākāreṇa / prakhyānāt vitathapratibhāsatvaṃ /
# gzung ba med par bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba gnyis 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang bas log par snang ba nyid do /
atha vā yathā vijñānenārthaḥ parikalpyate tathārthasyābhāvo
# yang na ji ltar rnam par shes pas don yongs su brtags pa de bzhin du bdag dang rnam par rig par don med de stag la sogs pa thob pa ltar /
vyāghrādiśrutyādiṣv iva vitathālambanatvād vitathapratibhāsatā / / tathā hi vijñaptir api vijñapty antaraparikalpitenātmanā śūnyeti / siddhāntaḥ / / ataścārthasattvavijñānasyevātmavijñaptipratibhāsasyāpyarthābhāvaḥ /
# log par dmigs pa'i phyir / / log par snang ba nyid do / / 'di ltar rnam par rig pa yang rnam par rig pa gzhan gyis kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis stong ngo zhes grub pa'i mtha' las 'byung ngo / / de'i phyir don dang sems can du snang ba bzhin du / / bdag dang rnam par rig par snang ba'i don yang med do /
arthābhāvāt tad vijñānam asat /
# don med pas rnam par shes pa de yang med do /
vijānātīti vijñānaṃ grāhyābhāve vijānanāpy ayuktaṃ /
# rnam par rig pas na rnam par shes pa ste / / de yang gzung ba med na rnam par shes pa por mi rigs te /
tasmād arthābhāvād vijñātṛtvena vijñānam asad na [p.17] / tv arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsatayā /
# de lta bas na don med pa'i phyir rnam par shes pa kho nar rnam par shes pa med kyi don dang sems can dang bdag dang rnam par rig par snang bas na med pa ma yin no /
tad asattve hi sarvathā'bhāvaprasaṅgaḥ / / tad avyatirekeṇa vijñānasvabhāvānirdeśāt / / tad bhinnasvabhāve sati tad vijñānaṃ kathaṃ yujyeta kathaṃ parasparaṃ
# de med du zin na de ma gtogs par rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin ma bstan pa'i phyir ye med par thal bar 'gyur ro / / de dang tha dad pa'i rang bzhin yin na ni de ji ltar rnam par shes par rung /
bhinnaṃ bhavet ? //1-4// / evaṃgrāhyagrāhakābhāvāt tat pratibhāsavijñānasadbhāvāc ca yat / pūrvaṃ pratijñātaṃ - / abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate /
# ji ltar phan tshun tha dad par 'gyur / / de ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa ni med la de snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni yod pas / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni yod /
iti tat prasiddham iti pradarśayann āha -
# gnyis po ni de na yod pa ma yin par sngar dam bcas pa de grub po zhes rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
abhūtaparikalpatvaṃ siddham asya bhavatyataḥ /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa / / de ni de phyir grub pa yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
abhūtaparikalpatvañca teṣāñcaturṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ siddhaṃ / / ata ity anantaroktād hetorarthābhāvāt tad apy asad iti punar apy / abhūtaparikalpāstitvaprasādhanārthaṃ dvayābhāvaprasādhanārthañcāha
# rnam par shes pa bzhi po de yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun du rtog pa grub pa yin no / / de phyir zhes bya ba ni bshad ma thag pa'i rgyu de'i phyir te / / don med pas na de yang med ces bya'o / / yang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod par bsgrub pa dang gnyis po med par rab tu bsgrub pa'i phyir /
na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt
# de bzhin ma yin ye med min /
ityādi / / atha vā ata iti vakṣyamāṇādvetoḥ /
# zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / yang na de'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'og nas 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
tameva pradarṣayannāh
# de nyid rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt
# de bzhin ma yin ye med min /
iti/ / na tathā'stitvān na ca sarvathā nāstitvāt tad
# zhes bya ba gsungs te / / de bzhin du yod pa ma yin pa dang ye med pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsam utpadyate /
# gang gi phyir gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba de skye ba ste /
tatra catuḥprakāre'py anākāratvād vitathākāratvāc ca yathāsambhavaṃ / grāhakatvābhāvaḥ /
# de la rnam pa bzhi po de yang rnam pa med pa dang log par snang ba'i phyir ji ltar mthun par 'dzin pa nyid du med do /
vijñaptyantaraparikalpitena cātmanā sarvasya śūnyatvād / grāhyatvābhāvaḥ /
# rnam par rig pa gzhan gyis kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyis thams cad stong bas gzung ba nyid du med do /
na ca sarvathā'bhāvo bhrāntimātrasyotpādād ityātmatvenābhāvo na tu
# 'khrul pa tsam 'byung ba'i phyir ye med pa yang ma yin no zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid kyis med kyang /
yadākāreṇa pratibhāsate tena bhrāntir ucyare māyāvat /
# rnam par snang ba gang yin pa de ni 'khrul pa zhes bya ste / / sgyu ma bzhin no /
mātra- śabdas tadadhikavyavacchedārthaḥ /
# tsam zhes bya ba'i sgra ni de las lhag ma rnam bar gcad pa'i tha tshig ste /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - / bhrāntivijñānasya sadbhāvān na sarvathā'bhāva iti /
# de ni 'di skad du 'khrul pa'i rnam par shes pa yod do / / ye med pa ma yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
kimartha punas tasya bhrāntivijñānasyā'bhāva eva neṣyate / grāhyagrāhakābhāvavat ?
# 'khrul pa'i rnam par shes pa de gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa bzhin du med pa nyid du ci'i phyir mi 'dod /
na hi kenacit tasyāstitvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate / sarvāvijñānaviṣayātikrāntatvād ity abhipretam iti cet /
# rnam par shes pa thams cad kyi yul las 'das pa'i phyir / / sus kyang de yod pa nyid du brtag par mi nus so zhes bsams pa'o zhe na 'di ltar /
yasmāt - / tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate / / ato'syābhāva eva neṣyate /
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod / / de'i phyir de med pa nyid du mi 'dod do /
kiṃ tarhi saṅkleśavyavadānapakṣasāmarthāt tad astitvam anumīyate / [p.18] / anyatheti yadi tasya sarvathābhāva eveṣyate na bandho na mokṣa iti /
# de ji lta zhe na kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i phyogs kyi mthus de yod par rjes su dpag go / / gzhan du na zhes bya ba ni gal te ye med pa nyid du 'dod na ni bcings pa yang med ces bya ste /
bhrāntimātre'py asati saṅkleśābhāvād bandho'pi nāsti /
# 'khrul pa tsam yang med du zin na / / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pas bcings pa yang med do /
pūrvaṃ baddho mucyata iti kṛtvā muktir api na syāt / / atha vā kathaṃ na yathā prakhyāti tathā bhāveneṣyate sarvathā
# sngar bcings pa las grol lo zhes bya na grol ba yang med par 'gyur / / yang na de ji ltar snang ba de bzhin du yod pa'am /
vā'bhāva iti parābhiprāyavyudāsārtham āha -
# yang na ye med par ci'i phyir mi 'dod ces gzhan de snyam du sems pa bsal ba'i phyir /
tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate /
# de zad nas ni grol bar 'dod /
tasmiṃścāparikṣīṇe bandha ityarthād uktaṃ bhavati /
# ces gsungs te / / de ma zad na bcings pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
anyathā hi na bandho na mokṣa iti saṅkleśavyavadānāpavādadoṣaḥ syāt / / yathā grāhyagrāhakatvena bhrāntir udbhāsitā'pi yadi tathā syāt
# de gzhan du na bcings pa dang grol ba med do zhes de skad bshad par 'gyur te / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa la skur ba 'debs pa'i nyes par 'gyur ro / / gal te ji ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nyid du phyugs yan chad la snang ba yang gal te de bzhin du don dam par 'gyur na ni /
paramārthata evaṃ sati nityaḥ saṅkleśaḥ syāt /
# de ltar yin du zin na rtag par kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur te /
tathā ca nirvāṇābhāvaḥ / / evaṃ ca bhrāntimātrasyāpy abhāve saṅkleśābhāvo nityañca vyavadānaṃ
# de ltar na mya ngan las 'das pa yang med par 'gyur ro / / de ltar 'khrul pa tsam med na yang kun nas nyon mongs pa med par 'gyur te /
prasajyeta / / evaṃ cobhayathāpi mokṣārthināṃ vyartho yatnaḥ syāt / / ato'vaśyam abhūtaparikalpabhāvo'bhyupagantavyo dvayābhāvaś ca //1-5//
# rtag tu rnam par byang bar 'gyur ro / / de ltar na gnyi gar yang thar pa tshol ba rnams kyi 'bad pa don med par 'gyur bas de'i phyir yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yod pa dang gnyis po med par gdon mi za bar khas blang bar bya'o /
saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti saṅgraha eva lakṣaṇaṃ / / atha vā yena saṅgraho lakṣyate tat saṅgrahalakṣaṇaṃ /
# bsdu ba'i mtshan nyid ston te zhes bya ba ni / / bsdu ba nyid mtshan nyid do / / yang na gang gis bsdu bar mtshon pa de bsdu ba'i mtshan nyid do /
tac ca kim artham uktaṃ ? / atra hi grāhyagrāhakarahitam abhūtaparikalpamātramevāstīty ayuktaṃ /
# de yang ci'i phyir bshad ce na / / 'dir ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang brla ba yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam nyid yod do zhes smras la /
sūtrāntareṣu punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ paṭhyante / / ataḥ sūtrāntarair avirodhapradarśanārthaṃ teṣām iha saṅgraha ucyate /
# mdo gzhan dag las ni / / ngo bo nyid gsum gsungs pas mdo dag dang mi 'gal bar rab tu bstan pa'i phyir de dag 'dir bsdu bar brjod de /
ata eva vṛttikāra āha -
# de lta bas na 'grel pa mdzad pas /
abhūtaparikalpamātre satīti vistareṇa -
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa tsam du zad na zhes bya ba rgya cher smos so /
kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca /
# brtag pa dang ni gzhan dbang dang / / yongs su grub pa nyid kyang ngo /
arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ // iti /
# don phyir yang dag min rtog phyir / / gnyis po med pa'i phyir bshad do /
grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ca svabhāvaśūnyatvād abhūtam apy astitvena / parikalpyata iti [p.19] / parikalpita ucyate / / sa punar dravyato'sannapi vyavahārato'stīti svabhāva ucyate /
# zhes bya ba ni / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa rang bzhin gyis stong pa las yang dag pa ma yin par yang yod par yongs su rtog pas kun brtags pa zhes bya'o / / de ni rdzas su med kyang tha snyad du yod pas ngo bo nyid ces bya'o /
paratantraḥ paravaśaḥ hetupratyayapratibaddhajanmakatvāt /
# gzhan gyi dbang ni rgyu dang rkyen la rag las te skye bas gzhan gyi kha na las pa'o /
āha ca -
# smras pa /
akalpitaḥ pratyayaco'nabhilāpyaś ca sarvathā /
# brtags min rkyen las skyes pa dang / / rnam pa kun tu brjod med pa /
paratantrasvabhāvo hi śuddhalaukikagocaraḥ //
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid / / 'jig rten pa yi spyod yul lo /
yā'bhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā sa pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ / tasyā'saṃskṛtatvāt nirvikāratvena pariniṣpannatvāt /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa nyid gnyis dang bral ba nyid gang yin pa de ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de / / de ni 'dus ma byas pas mi 'gyur bar yongs su grub pa'o /
āha ca - / kalpitena svabhāvena tasya yā'tyantaśūnyatā /
# brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis te / / shin tu stong nyid gang yin pa /
svabhāvaḥ pariniṣpanno 'vikalpajñānagocaraḥ //
# yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo ste / / mi rtog ye shes spyod yul lo /
arthād ityarthādhipatyād uktaṃ /
# don phyir zhes bya ba ni don gyi dbang du mdzad nas bshad pa ste /
evam abhūtaparikalpād dvayābhāvācceti vaktavyaṃ / / arthaḥ parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ityartho'tra rūpādayaścakṣurādaya ātmā / vijñaptayaś ca /
# de ltar yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'i phyir dang gnyis po med pa'i phyir ro zhes brjod par bya'o / / don ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya la / / don ni 'dir gzugs la sogs pa dang mig la sogs pa dang bdag dang rnam par rig pa rnams te /
sa ca kalpitena svabhāvenābhūtaparikalpe nāstīty asan parikalpitaḥ
# de yang rnam par brtags pa'i rang bzhin du yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la med pas /
svabhāva ucyate / / āha ca - / akalpito vikalpo hi vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ /
# med pa la kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya'o / / yang smras pa / / rnam rtog rnam par mi rtog ni / / rnam rtog gzhan gyis brtags pa ste /
svabhāvo nāstyasau tasya vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ //
# rnam rtog gzhan gyis brtags de yi / / rang bzhin de ni yod ma yin /
abhūtaparikalpaḥ paratantraḥ svabhāva iti / / parair hetupratyayais tantryate janyate na tu svayambhavatīti paratantraḥ /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba la rgyu dang rkyen gzhan dag gi dbang byed pa dang skyed pa ste / / rang mi 'byung bas gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
grāhyagrāhakābhāvaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti / / nirvikārapariniṣpattyā'viparītapariniṣpattyā ca parniṣpannatvāt
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid ces bya ba ni mi 'gyur bar yongs su grub pa dang phyin ci ma log par yongs su grub pas yongs su grub pa'i phyir /
pariniṣpanna ucyate /
# yongs su grub pa pa'o zhes bya'o /
atra hy abhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā grāhyagrāhakābhāva uktaḥ /
# 'dir ni yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa gnyis dang bral ba nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med par bstan pa yin gyi /
na tu dvayasyābhāvamātraṃ /
# gnyis po med pa tsam gyis ni ma yin no /
evañcābhūtaparikalpa eva hetupratyapāratantryāt paratantraḥ /
# de ltar na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa nyid rgyu dang rkyen gzhan gyi kha na las pas gzhan gyi dbang ngo /
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarūpeṇa svātmany avidyamānena prakhyānāt / parikalpitaḥ /
# de nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i ngo bor bdag nyid kyis med kyang snang ba'i phyir kun brtags pa'o /
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarahitatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ /
# de nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i phyir yongs su grub pa'o /
evam abhūtaparikalpe trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ saṅgrahītāḥ /
# de ltar na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa la ngo bo nyid gsum 'dus so /
etenā'bhūtaparikalpam anūdya parijñeyaṃ parijñāya prahātavyaṃ / parijñāya sākṣāt kartavyañca vastu sandarśitaṃ bhavati //1-6// [p.20]
# de ltar byas na yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa yongs su shes par bya ba dang spang bar bya ba dang yongs su shes par bya ba mngon du bya ba'i dngos po yang bstan pa yin no /
aparijñātāsal lakṣaṇo hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kleśakarmajanmasaṅkleśāya / sampravartate /
# yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa med pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su ma shes pa'i phyir / / nyon mongs pa dang las dang tshe'i kun nas nyon mongs par gyur to /
ato'sallakṣaṇaparijñānārtham upāyaṃ pradarśayann āha -
# de lta bas na med pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su shes par bya ba dang de'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir /
upalabdhiṃ samāśritya
# dmigs pa la ni brten nas su /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
abhūtaparikalpe tad upalakṣaṇam abhūtaparikalpo veti /
# yang dag ma yin kun rtog pa la de mtshon pa'am / / yang dag pa ma yin pa kun rtog pa'o /
grāhyagrāhakayor asattvam evā'sallakṣaṇaṃ / / tatrānupraveśas tad avabodhaḥ /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa gnyis med pa nyid ni med pa'i mtshan nyid do / / de la 'jug pa ni de khong du chud pa'o /
tasyopāyo yatas tad asallakṣaṇam anupraviśati /
# de'i thabs ni thabs gang gis de'i med pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rjes su 'jug pa'o /
sa punar dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthapratibodhaprayoganiśraya viśeṣaḥ
# de yang chos kyi dbyings kun tu 'gro ba'i don rab tu rtog par bya bar sbyor ba ni /
kuśalo dvividhaḥ / / tad upalakṣyā'yaṃ śloka uktaḥ / / vijñaptimātropalabdhiṃ niśrityā'rthā'nupalabdhir jāyata iti / / idaṃ vijñaptimātram ālambanārtharahitaṃ svabījaparipākād
# gnas kyi khyad par mkhas par rnam pa gnyis so / / de nye bar mtshon pa'i don du tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so / / rnam par rig pa tsam du dmigs pa la brten nas don mi dmigs pa skye'o zhes bya ba ni / / dmigs pa'i don dang bral ba 'di ni rnam par rig pa tsam nyid de /
rūpādyābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ pravartate na tu rūpādiko'rtho'stītyevaṃ / grāhakopalabdhiṃ niśritya grāhyānupalabdhiṃ praviśati /
# rang gi sa bon yongs su smin pa las gzugs la sogs par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa skye ba yin gyi / / gzugs la sogs pa'i don ni yod pa ma yin no zhes de ltar 'dzin pa dmigs pa la gnas te / / gzung ba mi dmigs par rab tu 'jug go /
evaṃ hy anena vicārayitavyaṃ -
# des 'di ltar brtags par bya ste /
utpadyamānam anutpannaṃ vā vijñānaṃ viṣayamālambeta /
# rnam par shes pa skye ba'i tshe'am / / skye sa zin pas yul la dmigs par 'gyur grang na /
tatrotpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ nālambate utpadyamānasyāsattvāt / / notpannam api viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpannatvāt /
# de la skye ba'i tshe ni med pas skye ba'i tshe yul la dmigs par mi rung ngo / / yul du snang ba'i bdag nyid du skyes pa'i phyir / / skyes pas kyang ma yin te /
na ca viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpattim uktvā vijñānasyānyā kriyā'sti / yāṃ kriyāṃ kurvat vijñānaṃ viṣayam ālambana ity ucyate /
# yul du snang ba'i bdag nyid du skye ba ma gtogs par / / gang byed na rnam par shes pa yul la dmigs pa'o zhes bya'o zhes bya ba'i rnam par shes pa'i bya ba gzhan med do /
yadi vālambanasya vartamāna eva vijñāne vyāpāro notpadyamāne evam
# gal te yang da ltar gyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyi dmigs pa byed pa yin gyi / / skye ba'i tshe ni ma yin no zhe na /
ālambanapratyayo na vijṇyānotpādakaḥ /
# de lta na ni dmigs pa'i rkyen rnam par shes pa'i skye ba ma yin te /
tat parikalpanaṃ nirarthakaṃ / / vartamānālambanagrahaṇe kṣaṇabhedadoṣo bhavati /
# der yongs su rtog pa don med do / / da ltar gyi dmigs pa 'dzin na ni skad cig pa 'jig pa'i gnod par 'gyur ro /
na cātmātiśayabhāve pūrvavad vijñānenālambanagrahaṇaṃ yujyate /
# rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa yang med pas snga ma bzhin te / / rnam par shes pas dmigs pa 'dzin par mi rung ngo /
athālambanagrahaṇakāle tasyātmātiśaya iṣyate evam apy
# 'on te dmigs pa 'dzin pa'i dus na / / de la rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur par 'dod na /
ātmātiśayasyānyata eva darśanād anyadevotpannam ālambanaṃ gṛhṇātīti
# de lta na yang rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa gzhan nyid du snang bas /
prasajyate / / anyo manyate -
# byung ba gzhan nyid kyis dmigs pa 'dzin par thal bar 'gyur ro /
nirudhyamāno'rtha evotpadyamānasya vijñānasyālambanapratyayaḥ /
# gzhan ni 'gag pa'i tshe'i don nyid skye ba'i tshe'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa'i rkyen nyid yin te /
sa ca svākārapratibhāsa jñānakāraṇatvena śeṣebhyaḥ pratyayebhyo / viśiṣyata / [p.21]
# de yang rang gi rnam par snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i rgyu yin pas rkyen lhag ma rnams las khyad par can no snyam du sems te /
iti / / tenāpi rūpādiparamāṇavastat samūho vālambanatvena parikalpyate / / ubhayathāpi cālambanābhāvaḥ / / sarvam eva hi vijñānaṃ ghaṭapaṭādipratibhāsam utpadyate na tu
# des kyang gzugs la sogs pa'i rdul phra rab bam / / de 'dus pa la dmigs pa kho nar kun tu brtag grang na / / de gnyi ga yang dmigs par mi 'gyur te / / rnam par shes pa thams cad ni bum pa dang snam bu la sogs par snang ba 'byung gi /
paramāṇupratibhāsaṃ / / na cā'rthākārasyā'nyanirbhāsasya vijñānasyānyad ālambanaṃ / / cakṣurādīnām apy ālambanatvaprasaṅga iti /
# rdul phra rab tu snang ba ni ma yin no / / don gyi rnam pa gzhan du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa ni gzhan ma yin te / / mig la sogs pa yang dmigs pa nyid du thal bar 'gyur ta re /
yo'pi manyate samuditāḥ paramāṇava ālambanaṃ na pratyekaṃ tasyāpy ayam / aparihāraḥ /
# gang gzhan yang rdul phra rab sil bu so so la dmigs pa yin pa snyam du sems pa de'i 'di yang lan du mi rung ste /
samuditā api hi te pratyekam evālambanatveneṣYante na tat samudāyena / / tatra paramāṇūnāṃ pratyekapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ notpadyate nāpi tat
# sil bu de ni de dag so so nyid la dmigs par 'dod kyi / / de dag gi 'dus pa la ni ma yin no / / der rdul phra rab so sor snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni mi 'byung gi /
samudāyapratibhāsaṃ / / tasmān na paramāṇūnām ālambanatvaṃ sambhavati /
# 'di ltar de dag gi 'dus par snang ba ste / / de bas na rdul phra rab rnams la dmigs pa mi srid do /
nāpi paramāṇusamūha ālambanaṃ prajñaptisataḥ kāraṇatvāsambhavāt /
# brtags par yod pa ni rgyur mi srid pa'i phyir / / rdul phra rab 'dus pa yang dmigs pa ma yin na /
vijñānakāraṇaṃ hi samanantarādipratyayavad ālambanapratyayo'pīṣyate / / tasmān na nirudhyamāno'pyālambanaṃ / / atha ca niruddha ālambanaṃ evaṃ satyātītānāgataṃ viṣayaḥ syāt / / svapnādau tu vijñānam anālambanam iti siddhaṃ /
# de ma thag pa la sogs pa'i rkyen ltar dmigs pa'i rkyen yang dag par shes pa'i rgyur 'dod de / / de'i phyir 'gag pa'i tshe yang dmigs pa'i rkyen du mi srid do / / ji ste yang 'gag pa nyid dmigs pa yin na / / de lta na ni 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa yul du 'gyur pa dang rmi lam la sogs pa la yang rnam par shes pa dmigs pa med par grub po /
nā'nālambanaṃ svapnādivijñānaṃ nimittālambanatvād iti kecit / / nimittaṃ punar arthapratibimbaṃ viprayuktasaṃskārasvabhāvaṃ /
# la lan re rmi lam la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa yang mtshan ma la dmigs pa'i phyir dmigs pa med pa ma yin no / / mtshan ma ni don gyi gzugs brnyan te ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi rang bzhin no zhe'o /
na hi svapnādāvasatyarthe tannimittaṃ yujyate mukhādyabhāve tat / pratibimbavat /
# rmi lam la sogs pa don med pa la de'i mtshan ma mi rung ste / / bzhin la sogs pa med par de'i gzugs brnyan mi 'grub pa bzhin no /
utpadyamānam utpannaṃ vālambanaṃ vijñānanimittam abhāvān nirodhāc
# 'byung ba'i tshe'am byung zin pa'i rnam par shes pas kyang mtshan ma la dmigs pa ma yin te /
ceti pūrvam uktaṃ / / vijñānameva arthapratibhāsatvād arthapratibimbaṃ / / ato na viprayuktasaṃskārātmakaṃ nimittaṃ yujyate /
# med pa dang dgag pa sngar bstan pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi rang bzhin mtshan mar mi rung bas / / rnam par shes ba nyid don du snang ba don gyi gzugs brnyan te /
avaśyaṃ cārthākāraṃ vijñānam abhyupagantavyaṃ /
# rnam par shes pa nyid don gyi rnam par gdon mi za bar khas blang dgos so /
anākāre hi tasmin grāhyagrāhakaniyama eva na syāt /
# rnam pa med na ni de la gzung ba dang 'dzin pa nges pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro /
anyastvapratighaṃ rūpameva svapne yogināṃ cāśubhādāvālambanaṃ manyate / tasyāpi varṇasaṃsthānādyātmakatvād apratighatvaṃ
# gzhan ni thogs pa med pa'i gzugs nyid rmi lam dang rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi mi sdug pa la sogs par dmigs pa'o snyam du sems te / / de'i yang kha dog dang dbyibs la sogs pa'i bdag nyid yin pas /
manomātraviṣayatvañca virudhyate /
# thogs pa med pa nyid dang yid 'ba' zhig gi yul du 'gal lo /
na cāvijñaptimātrād anyad apratighaṃ rūpaṃ śāstre varṇyate / / tasmāt kalpanāmātram eva /
# rnam par rig byed ma yin pa tsam ma gtogs par yang thogs pa med pa'i gzugs gzhan bstan bcos las mi bshad pas / / de'i phyir de nyid kyang rtog pa tsam nyid do /
