lokadhātau pratyekaṃ cātur dvīpakeṣu nirmāṇakāyenābhisambodhiṃ
# gzhan dag na re de bzhin gshegs pa gnyis kyang gling bzhi pa nyid du mi 'byung ngo zhes zer te /
parinirvāṇaṃ ca darśayanti / / tathā hi yadekasmiñcāturmahādvīpake tuṣiteṣu manuṣyeṣu ca / cyutijanmaparigraho bodhisattvānām prayojanaṃ / / taditareṣv api cātur dvīpakeṣu samānaṃ /
# sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi sku'i dbang gis stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su gling bzhi pa re rer yang sprul pa'i skus mngon par byang chub pa dang yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa yang ston to / / 'di ltar gling bzhi pa gcig tu dga' ldan dang mi rnams kyi nang du yang tshe yongs su 'dzin pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis dgongs pa ste /
tasmād akaniṣṭhabhavana evābhisambuddho bhagavān nirmāṇakāyena / trisāhasramahāsāhasre vantargateṣu sarvacāturdvīpakeṣu / tuṣiteṣūpapattiṃ manuṣyeṣu ca janmaparigrahādikaṃ sarvaṃ darśayatīti / manyante /
# de ni gling bzhi pa gzhan du'ang 'dra'o / / de lta bas na 'og min gyi gnas nyid du bcom ldan 'das mngon par sangs rgyas nas sprul pa'i skus stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i gling bzhi pa re rer yang dga' ldan du skye ba dang 'chi 'pho dang mi'i nang du tshe yongs su 'dzin pa la sogs pa thams cad ston to snyam du sems so /
tatra ca samasaṃvartanīyakarmāyattatā buddhacarkravartyutpatteḥ / sahabhāve pāratantryaṃ /
# 'di la sangs rgyas dang 'khor los sgyur ba 'byung ba ni mnyam par 'gyur ba ma yin pa'i las la rag lus pas lhan cig tu skye bar 'gyur ba gzhan gyi dbang nyid do /
ādhipatye pāratantryaṃ striyā cakravartitvādyakaraṇād iti / cakravartisaṃvartanīyasya karmaṇaḥ pumātmabhāva eva
# dbang byed pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni bud med 'khor los sgyur ba la sogs pa mi byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur ba'i las kyi rnam par smin pa ni skyes pa'i lus kyis smin par nus te /
vipākadānasāmarthyāt / / na hi strīḥ stryādiratnopabhogasamarthā /
# bud med la ni bud med rin po che la spyod pa'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro /
ādiśabdena śakratvādr gṛhyate /
# sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni brgya byin la sogs pa bsdu'o /
samprāptau pāratantryaṃ stryāpratyekānuttarabodhyanabhisambodhāt / / prāptir buddha-pratyekabuddhatvādhigamaḥ /
# 'thob pa'i gzhan gyi dbang ni bud med kyis rang byang chub dang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs par byang chub par mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la / / 'thob pa ni sangs rgyas dang rang byang chub nyid 'thob pa'o /
tatra pāratantryaṃ puruṣasya prāptir na tu striyaḥ /
# de la gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni skyes pas 'thob par 'gyur gyi bud med kyis 'thob par mi 'gyur te /
tasyā hi saṃsargābhāvāt khaḍgavat / tribhūmiśāstrītvāsambhavādyathākramaṃ /
# de ni go rims bzhin du bse ru lta bur 'dre ba med pa dang sa gsum gyi ston par mi srid pa'i phyir te /
sā punaḥ sarvadhūrtajanagamyā alpaprajñatvād / anācāryakābhisambodhāyogyā ceti /
# de'ang skye bo g yon can thams cad kyi spyod yul yin pa dang shes rab chung bas slob dpon med par mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i 'os ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
samudācāre pāratantryaṃ dṛṣṭisampannasya vadhādyasamudācārāt
# kun du spyod pa'i gzhan gyi dbang nyid ni lta ba phun sum tshogs pa gsod pa la sogs pa kun du mi spyod la /
pṛthagjanasya ca samudācārād iti / / dṛṣṭisampanno dṛṣṭasatyaḥ /
# so so'i skye bo ni kun du spyod pa'i phyir te zhes bya ba lta ba phun sum tshogs pa ni bden pa mthong ba'o /
vadhaḥ prāṇātipātaḥ / [p.116] / ādiśabdenādattādānādayaḥ saṃgṛhyante / / te vadhādayaḥ kāyavāk-kriyāsvabhāvā dṛṣṭisampannasya na samudācaranti
# gsod pa ni srog gcod pa yin; sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni ma byin par len pa la sogs pa bsdus te / / gsod pa la sogs pa de dag ni lus dang ngag gi bya ba'i rang bzhin no /
darśanamārgeṇa vadhādi-duścaritasamutthāpakakleśaprahāṇāt pṛthagjanasya / samudācaranti tad aprahāṇāt / / tad aprahāṇaṃ punas tat pratipakṣeṇa mārgānutpannatvāt /
# mthong ba'i lam nyid kyi gsod pa la sogs pa nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba'i nyon mongs pa spongs pa'i phyir lta ba phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa ni kun du mi spyod do / / so so'i skye bo ni de ma spangs pa'i phyir kun du spyod do / / de ma spangs pa yang de'i gnyen por lam ma skyes pa'i phyir ro /
evam aniṣṭādipāratantryānugatam asthānakauśalyaṃ puruṣeśvarādau / svātantryāgrāhapratipakṣaḥ /
# de ltar mi 'dod pa la sogs pa gzhan gyi dbang nyid kyi rjes su song ba / / gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa ni skyes bu dang dbang phyug la sogs pa rang dbang can du 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
yadi hi svatantraḥ kaścit syān na duścaritena durgatiṃ gacchet /
# gal te rang dbang can 'ga' zhig yod na ni nyes par spyad pa las ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro /
evam anyatrāpi vācyaṃ //3-19//
# de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang brjod par bya'o /
{ indriyārthaḥ } / sthānāsthānārthanirdeśānantaram indriyārtho vaktavya ityata āha -
# gnas dang gnas ma yin pa'i don bstan pa'i 'og tu dbang po rnams kyi don brjod dgos pas de'i phyir dbang po ni rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis te zhes bya ba smos te /
indriyaṃ dvāviṃśatividham iti cakṣurindriyaṃ yāvad
# mig gi dbang po nas kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po la thug gi bar du'o /
ājñātāvindriyāvasānaṃ /
# de la dbang po'i don ni dbang byed pa'i don to /
atra punar ādhipātyarthaṃ indriyārthaḥ /
# gang zhig gang la dbang byed pa de mi shes nas /
kasya punaḥ kvādhipatyam ityata āha -
# de'i phyir / / 'dzin dang gnas dang rgyun mi 'chad /
grahaṇasthānasandhānabhogaśuddhidvayārthataḥ / iti /
# spyod dang dag pa gnyis kyi phyir / / zhes bya ba gsungs te /
atra ca dvayādhipattyārthata iti yuktau kārikānukūlārtham / ādhipatyaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ /
# 'di la gnyis pa dbang byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba rigs pa las tshig le'ur byas pa dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir dbang byed pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni mi smos par blta'o /
tasmād bhāṣyakāra āha - teṣu tadādhipatyād iti / / grahaṇārtheneti / / arthaśabdo'tra prayojanavācī / / grahaṇaprayojanaṃ nimittaṃ tatrendriyam iti darśayati /
# de bas na bshad pa byed pas / / de dag la de dbang byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / 'dzin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la / / phyir zhes bya ba'i sgra ni 'dir dgos pa yin par brjod de / / 'dzin pa'i dgos pa ste ched yin la /
evam anyatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ /
# de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang ci rigs par brjod par bya'o /
teṣvityarthagrahaṇādiṣu ādhipatyam ityadhikaprabhutvam ityādhipatyaṃ / hetutvam ityarthaḥ / / rūpādayo dharmaparyantā rūpādiviṣayāḥ /
# de dag la zhes bya ba ni don 'dzin pa la sogs pa la'o / / dbang byed ces bya ba ni lhag par dbang bas na dbang byed pa ste rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gzugs la sogs pa chos la thug pa dag ni gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams te /
teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ cakṣurādivijñānaṃ / / tatra cakṣurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām ādhipatyaṃ / / cakṣuṣo niravaśeṣarūpaprabhedavijñānāśrayatvād rūpādīnām / adhikaprabhutvam itīndriyam ucyate / / na tu nīlarūpaṃ pītarūpādivijñānasyālambanaṃ bhavati /
# de dag la 'dzin pa ni mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'o / / de la mig la sogs pa dbang po drug dbang byed pa ni mig ni gzugs kyi bye brag ma lus pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rten yin pas gzugs la sogs pa la lhag par dbang byed pas na dbang po zhes bya ste / / gzugs sngon po ni gzugs ser po la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i dmigs par mi 'gyur ro /
evaṃ śrotrādiṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vistareṇa vācyaṃ / / sthāne jīvitendriyasyeti / / jīvitendriyaṃ punaḥ karmavāsanāvidhaṃ vipākasantāne'sati / vicchittipratyaye pūrvpūrvakṣāṇasarūpeṣūttarottarakṣaṇeṣu
# de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa la yang ci rigs su rgyas par brjod par bya'o / / gnas par bya ba la ni srog gi dbang po dbang byed de zhes bya ba la; srog gi dbang po ni sngon gyi las kyi bag chags kyis 'phangs pa'i rnam par smin pa'i rgyud la bar du gcod pa'i rkyen med na skad cig snga mas 'dra ba'i skad cig phyi ma phyi ma rnams su mtshams sbyor ba'i mthu yod pa'o /
pratisandhisāmarthyaṃ / / sthāne jīvitendriyasyādhipatyam ityatraiva kāraṇam āha - tad / ādhipatyenā'maraṇād iti /
# gnas par bya ba la ni srog gi dbang po dbang byed ces bya ba la rgyu smos pa / / 'di'i dbang gis mi 'chi ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ste /
amaraṇaṃ pūrvakarmākṣiptanikāyasabhāgānuvṛttiḥ / / satyapi sattvasthitikāraṇatve nāhārādīnām indriyatvaṃ /
# mi 'chi ba ni sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs rigs mthun pa'i rjes su 'jug go / / kha zas la sogs pa ni sems can gnas pa'i rgyu yin du zin kyang dbang po ma yin te /
tat sadbhāve'pyāyuṣaḥ kṣaye'vasthānā'sadbhāvāt / [p.117]
# de dag yod bzhin du tshe zad pa gnas pa med pa'i phyir ro /
rūpārūpyadhātāv asatyapi kavaḍīkārāhāre / jīvitendriyādevā'vasthānasadbhāvāt / / na ca tatra sparśādīnām avasthāna ādhipatyaṃ yujyate /
# gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na kham gyis za ba'i zas rnams med kyang srog gi dbang po nyid kyis gnas pa yod pa'i phyir ro / / de na reg pa la sogs pa ni gnas par dbang byed par mi rung ste /
nirodhā'saṃjñisamāpattyavasthāyām āsaṃjñike ca sparśādyabhāve'pi / sattvānāṃ sthitisambhavād iti / / kulasandhāne strīpuruṣendriyayor ādhipatyam iti / / putrotpattau kulāvyuparatatā vartata iti putrotpattiḥ kulasandhānaṃ /
# 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i gnas dang 'du shes med pa dag la reg pa la sogs pa med kyang sems can rnams gnas par srid pa'i phyir ro / / rigs 'tshob pa la pho dang mo'i dbang po gnyis dbang byed de zhes bya ba la / / bu byung na rigs rgyun mi 'chad par 'gyur bas bu 'byung ba ni rigs 'tshob pa'o /
etad eva darśayann āha - prasavādhipatyād iti /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'byung bar dbang byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
kāyendriyapradeśa eva kaścid ādhipatyaviśeṣāt strīpuruṣendriyākhyaṃ / pratilabhate / / yatra stīndriyaṃ puruṣendriyañcas tastatra kulavyavasthānam asti /
# lus kyi dbang po'i phyogs 'ga' nyid de / / dbang byed pa'i bye brag gis pho dang mo'i dbang po zhes bya ba 'thob po / / gang na pho'i dbang po dang mo'i dbang po yod pa de na rigs rnam par gzhag pa yod de /
tad vaśena kulo na vyuparamate /
# de'i dbang gis rigs rgyun mi 'chad do /
kāmāvacareṣv api ca deveṣu strīndriye puruṣendriye ca sati / kulavyavasthānaṃ nā'satīti / / nahi gandharvādīnāṃ tatrādhipatyaṃ satyapi gandharvādau paṇḍakādiṣu
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams la ni pho'i dbang po dang mo'i dbang po yod pa la rigs rnam par gzhag gi med pa la ni ma yin no / / dri za la sogs pa la dbang byed pa med de dri za la sogs pa yod du zin kyang /
strīpuruṣendriyayor asadbhāve putraprasavasāmārthyābhāvāt / / āhārādīnāṃ punaḥ sattve'saṃkhyātatvāt satyapyādhipatye nendriyatvaṃ
# pho dang mo'i dbang po med pa ma ning la sogs pa la bu 'byung ba'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro / / zas la sogs pa ni dbang byed pa yin yang sems can gyi grangs su ma gtogs pas dbang po zhes mi bya'o /
upabhoge vedanendriyāṇāṃ / / ādhipatyam ityadhikṛtaṃ / / katham ityata āha - kuśalākuśalakarmaphalopabhogād iti /
# nye bar spyod pa la ni tshor ba'i dbang po rnams te zhes bya ba ni dbang byed ces bya ba dang sbyar te / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu la nye bar spyod pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
vedanendriyāṇi pañca - sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saumanasyaṃ daurmanasyam upekṣā ca
# tshor ba'i dbang po ni lnga ste / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms so /
tarhi kuśalākuśalakarmaphala upabhujyate anubhavātmakatvāt /
# de dag ni myong ba'i bdag nyid yin pas dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu spyod kyi /
na nāmarūpasya tadādhipatyaṃ vedanāsambhārabhāvāt /
# ming dang gzugs ni de la dbang byed pa ma yin te / / tshor ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat sambhārabhāvaś ca vedanāpradhānatvād vipākasyeti / / laukikaviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ laukikakleśānāṃ / / tatra śraddhādīnām iti / śraddhā-vīrya-smṛti-samādhi-prajñā-pañcendriyāṇāṃ /
# de'i rgyu'i dngos po ni tshor ba rnam par smin pa'i gtso bo yin pa'i phyir ro / / 'jig rten pa'i rnam par dag pa ni 'jig rten pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams spang pa'o / / de la dad pa la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po dang lnga ste /
ādhipatyam iti vartate /
# dbang byed ces bya bar snyegs so /
teṣām aśraddhādipratipakṣetvena laukikamārgaprabhāvitatvāt /
# de dag ni ma dad pa la sogs pa'i gnyen po yin pa dang 'jig rten pa'i lam gyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
mokṣabhāgīyaprabhāvitatvād ity apare /
# gzhan na re thar pa'i cha dang mthun pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro zhe'o /
lokottaraviśuddhāvanājñānamājñāsyāmīndriyādīnām ityādhipatyam / iti vartate /
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa ni kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dbang byed do zhes bya bar snyegs te /
lokottaramārgeṇa kleśānāṃ prahāṇaṃ lokottaraviśuddhiḥ /
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyis nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa'o /
tatrānājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriyājñātāvīndriyāṇāṃ / trayāṇām ādhipatyaṃ /
# de la kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po gsum ni dbang byed pa ste /
teṣāṃ darśanabhāvanā'śaikṣamārgeṣu yathākramaṃ saṃgṛhītatvāt / / tatra śraddhādīnāṃ pañca manaḥsukhasaumanasyopekṣāṇi / cānāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa sambhavam adhikṛtyaitāni navendriyāṇi
# de dag mthong ba dang bsgom pa dang mi slob pa'i lam du rim pa bzhin du bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / de la dad pa la sogs pa lnga dang yid dang bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms rnams ni mi lcogs pa med pa la sogs pa la brten pa'i bye brag gis ci rigs pa'i dbang du byas te /
darśanamārge'nājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ /
# dbang po dgu ni mthong ba'i lam la ni kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po'o /
bhāvanāmārga ājñendriyaṃ /
# bsgom pa'i lam la ni kun shes pa'i dbang po'o /
aśaikṣaṃārga ajñātāvīndriyam ity ucyate /
# mi slob pa'i lam la ni kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o /
yogācārāṇāṃ tv anyathā vyavasthānaṃ / [p.118] / anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriye dvaye daśendriyāṇi /
# rnal 'byor pa rnams ni gzhan du rnam par 'jog ste / / kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa'i dbang po gnyis la ni dbang po bcu ste /
pūrvokteṣu navasu daurmanasyam adhikaṃ prakṣipya daśa bhavanti /
# sngar smos pa dgu'i nang du yid mi bde ba bsnan na bcur 'gyur ro /
ājñātāvendriyan tu navaiva / / tatra prayogamārge nirvedhabhāgīyātmake pañcadaśasu ca / darśanamārgakṣaṇeṣu manaindriyaṃ pañca / śraddhādīnyanāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa yathāsaṃbhavaṃ / sukha-saumanasya-daurmanasyopekṣendriyāṇāṃ cānyatamād daurmanasyendriyaṃ
# kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po la ni dgu nyid do / / de la nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i bdag nyid sbyor ba'i lam dang mthong ba'i lam skad cig bco lnga dag la ni yid kyi dbang po dang dad pa la sogs pa lnga dang mi lcogs pa med pa la sogs pa la brten pa'i bye brag gis ci rigs par bde ba dang yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms kyi dbang po rnams las gang yang rung ba'o /
punaḥ prayogakāle nirvedhabhāgīyapṛṣṭhenottaravimokṣaspṛhāsaṅgṛhītaṃ / veditavyaṃ /
# yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ni sbyor ba'i dus na nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i 'og tu thar pa mchog 'dod pas bsdus par rig par bya'o /
tadetat saṃbhavato daśavidham indriyaṃ /
# dbang po 'di bcu ni ci rigs par sbyar bar bya ste /
anājñātam evājñātuṃ pravṛttatvād anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyam / ucyate / / tadeva daśavidham indriyaṃ ṣoḍaśadarśanamārgakṣaṇādyāvad vajropamaḥ / samādhir ityetasmin śaikṣamārgam ājñendriyam ity ucyate
# sngon kun mi shes pa'i de kho na kun shes par bya ba'i phyir zhugs pas mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o / / mthong ba'i lam skad cig ma bcu drug nas rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bar du slob pa'i lam de la dbang po rnam pa bcu po de nyid kun shes pa'i dbang po zhes bya ba ste /
apūrvājñātājñeyābhāvāt /
# sngon mi shes pa shes par byar med pa'i phyir ro /
aśaikṣamārge daurmanasyendriyavyatiriktāni / śiṣṭānyājñātāvīndriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante /
# mi slob pa'i lam la yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ma gtogs par lhag ma rnams kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po'i ming 'thob po /
ājñātāvīndriyam iti ājñātāvīndriyam ucyate /
# kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po yin pas kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o /
evam indriyakauśalasya yaḥ puruṣanārāyaṇeśvarādiṣv adhipatigrāhaḥ sa / vyāvartate //
# de ltar na dbang po la mkhas pa ni skyes bu dang mthu bo che dang sred med kyi bu la sogs pa la dbang por 'dzin pa gang yin pa de ldog par 'gyur ro /
{ adhyārthaḥ } / indriyārthānantaram adhvatrayo vaktavya ityata āha -
# dbang po'i don gyi 'og tu dus gsum gyi don brjod dgos pas / / de'i phyir /
phalahetūpayogārthanopayogāt tathā'paraṃ // iti /
# 'bras bu rgyu rnams spyad zin dang / / de bzhin ma spyad gzhan yin no / / zhes bya ba smos te /
tatra janmakāraṇaṃ hetuḥ /
# de la rgyu ni skye bar byed pa'i rgyu'o /
phalaṃ janamasaṃgṛhītaṃ /
# 'bras bu ni tshes pa sdus pa'o /
phaladānaṃ hetor upayogaḥ /
# rgyu spyad zin pa ni 'bras bu phyung zin pa'o /
phalasyopāyogo'nubhūtasya parikṣayaḥ / / evam prakāraścātīto hetus tatphalaṃ cetyataḥ phalasya
# 'bras bu spyad zin pa ni myong nas yongs su zad pa ste / / rnam pa de lta bu'i rgyu dang de'i 'bras bu ni 'das pa'o /
taddhetoścopayogārthenānīto'dhvā / / tenaiva prakāreṇa phalasya hetoścā'nupayogārthenā'nāgato'dhvā /
# de'i phyir 'bras bu dang de'i rgyu spyad zin pa'i phyir 'das pa'i dus so / / rnam pa 'di nyid kyi 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i dus so /
vartamānaḥ punar adhvā vartamānaṃ janma / / hetordattaphalatvād hetūpayogārthena tatphalañca vartamānaṃ
# da ltar byung ba'i dus ni da ltar gyi tshe'i rgyus 'bras bu byin pa'i phyir rgyu spyad pa'i don dang de'i 'bras bu ni da ltar gyi tshe rjes su 'brang ba nyid de /
janmā'nuvartata eveti phalā'nuyogārthena ca veditavyaḥ /
# 'bras bu ma spyad pa'i phyir da ltar byung ba'i dus su rig par bya'o /
bhāvānāñca pratikṣaṇaṃ hetuphalabhāvatvena kṣaṇatvam / adhikṛtyā'dhvavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# dngos po rnams kyi skad cig so so ni rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos po yin pas skad cig nyid kyi dbang du byas te dus rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
tatra hetūpayogaḥ svaphalasyotpādānāt / / phalopayogaḥ phalasya janmānantaravināśāt / / evaṃ phalahetūpayogārthenātīto'dhvā phalahetvor
# de la rgyu spyad zin pa ni rang gi 'bras bu bskyed pa'i phyir ro / / 'bras bu spyad zin pa ni 'bras bu skyes ma thag tu 'jig pa'i phyir ro /
anupayogārthenānāgato'rdhveti prakṛtaṃ /
# de ltar 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i dus te /
kāryānutpādād anutpannasya ca vināśābhāvāt phalahetvor anupayogo / veditavyaḥ / [p.119] / hetūpayogaphalānupayogārtheneti kāryotpādanād hetūpayogaḥ /
# dgos pa ma bskyed pa dang ma skyes pa la zhig pa med pa'i phyir 'bras bu dang rgyu ma spyad par rig par bya'o / / rgyu spyad la 'bras bu ma spyad pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni dgos pa bskyed pa'i phyir rgyu spyad pa zhes bya'o /
kāryā'vināśātphalā'nupayogaḥ /
# dgos pa ma zhig pa'i phyir 'bras bu ma spyad pa zhes bya'o /
evam adhvakuśalasya nityātmeti grāho vyāvartate / / adhavyatiriktasyānyasyā'nupalabdhatvāt //3-20//
# de ltar dus la mkhas pa ni dus ma gtogs par gzhan mi dmigs pa'i phyir bdag rtag par 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro /
{ catussatyārthaḥ } / adhvatrayārthānantaraṃ catuḥsatyārtho vaktavya ityata āha - / vedanāsanimittārthatan nimittaprapattitaḥ /
# dus gsum gyi don gyi 'og tu bden pa bzhi'i don brjod dgos pas / / de'i phyir / / tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa'i don / / de yi rgyu ni sgrub pa yin /
iti vistaraḥ / / vedanā duḥkhārtha iti loke rūḍhaṃ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / tshor ba ni sdug bsngal gyi don to zhes 'jig rten na grags so /
śāstre ca yat kiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti vacanāt /
# bstan bcos las kyang gang ci tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug bsngal lo zhe'o /
satyavyavasthāyāṃ sarvā sāsravā sanimittā sukhā duḥkhā sukhāduḥkhā / ca vedanā duḥkhasatyārtha iti pradarśayan bhāṣyakāra āha - tatra
# bden pa rnam par gzhag pa ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa thams cad sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i don yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir bshad pa byed pas kyang /
duḥkhasatyaṃ vedanāsanimittārtheneti / / sarvā vedanā duḥkham iti kuta etat ?
# de la sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ni tshor ba rgyu dang bcas pa'i don zhes bya ba smos so / / tshor ba thams cad sdug bsngal yin par ci mngon zhe na /
ata āha - yatkiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti kṛtveti /
# de'i phyir gang ci tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'dir sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
sā ca vedanā duḥkha duḥkhatāvipariṇāmaduḥkhatā-saṃskāraduḥkhatābhir / yathāsambhavaṃ duḥkhā /
# tshor ba de dag kyang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rnams su ji ltar mthun du sbyar te / / sdug bsngal ba'o /
saṃskāraduḥkhatayaiva vā duḥkhā / / vedanānimittaṃ panar vedanāsthānīyā dharmā veditavyā iti /
# yang na 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyi sdug bsngal ba'o / / tshor ba'i rgyu ni tshor ba'i gnas kyi chos rnams su rig par bya'o zhes bya ba la /
sukhaduḥkhā'duḥkhāsukhavedanīyā dharmā vedanāsthānāni / / evaṃ pañcaskandhā duḥkhasatyaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ /
# bde ba dang sdug bsngal ba dang sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos rnams ni tshor ba'i gnas rnams so / / de ltar phung po lnga po dag ni sdug bsngal gyi bden par bstan pa yin no /
tan nimitta pratipattitaḥ samudayasatyam iti /
# de'i rgyu ni sgrub pa yin / / kun 'byung ba'i bden pa ste zhes bya ba la /
tac chabdena duḥkhasatyam abhisambadhyate / / duḥkhaṃ yayā pratipattyā janyate sā pratipattiḥ samudayasatyaṃ / / sā punar vedanāyāṃ vedanāsthāniyeṣu ca dharmeṣu tṛṣṇāhetupūrvikā / kāyavāṅmanaḥ pracalasvarūpā / / saṃkṣepataś ca bhavasamudbhavikaṃ karmasamudaya satyam ity uktam bhavati /
# de'i zhes bya ba'i sgra ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa dang sbyar ro / / sgrub pa gang gis sdug bsngal skyed pa ni bsgrub pa ste kun 'byung ba'o / / de yang tshor ba dang tshor ba'i gnas kyi chos rnams la sred pa'i rgyu sngon du song ba'i lus dang ngag dang yid rab tu g yo ba'i ngo bo nyid do / / mdor na yang srid pa kun nas slong ba'i las ni kun 'byung bar bstan pa yin no /
tayoḥ śamārthena nirodhasatyam iti /
# de gnyis zhi ba'i phyir 'gog pa'i bden pa'o zhes bya ba la /
tayor iti duḥkhasamudayasatyayoḥ /
# de gnyis zhes bya ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bden pa gnyis so /
śamārthenety utpādanārthena /
# zhi ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni mi skye ba'i phyir ro /
evañca sahetukaduḥKhānutpādalakṣaṇatvān nirodho dvividha uktaḥ
# de ltar rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal mi skye ba'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir 'gog pa la rnam pa gnyis su bstan pa yin te /
samudayaśamārthena sopadhiśeṣaḥ duḥkhopaśamārthena nirupādhiśeṣa iti / tayor evādhikṛtayor duḥkhasamudayayoḥ pratipakṣārthena / duḥkhasamudayanirodhagāminī pratipan mārgasatyaṃ /
# kun 'byung ba zhi ba'i phyir phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa'o / / sdug bsngal zhi ba'i phyir phung po'i lhag ma med pa'o / / de nyid kyi dbang du byas nas sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba gnyis kyi gnyen po'i phyir sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba 'gog par 'gyur ba'i lam ni lam gyi bden pa'o /
tadevaṃ satyakuśalasya saṅkleśavyavadānamātrāvagatatvāt tadanyaḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānagraho vyāvartate tasyābhāvād iti //3-21//
# de ltar bden pa la mkhas pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba tsam rtogs nas de dag las gzhan pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur te /
{ yānatrayā'rthaḥ } [p.120] / satyārthānantaraṃ yānatrayārthaṃ pratipādyata ityata āha - / guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena
# de med pa'i phyir ro / / bden pa rnams kyi don gyi 'og tu theg pa gsum gyi don bstan par bya ste / / de'i phyir / / yon tan skyon dang rnam mi rtog / / shes pas gzhan las bdag gis ni / / nges par 'byung phyir gzhan zhes bya /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes bya ba gsungs so /
jñānaśabda ubhayatra sambadhyate / / guṇadoṣajñānenā'vikalpajñānena ceti /
# shes pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni yon tan dang skyon shes pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba gnyis ka dang sbyar bar bya'o /
athavā'ntare vikalpaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ /
# yang na bar du rnam par rtog / / ces bya ba'i sgra zhig ma smos par blta bar bya'o /
tatra guṇadoṣajñānena parataḥ svayañceti ata evāha - vṛttau yathāyogam  iti / / tatra nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñāneneti / / nirvāṇaśabdenātra mārganirodhau saṅgṛhītau yathā praśāntaśabdaḥ /
# de la yon tan dang skyon shes pa ni gzhan las dang bdag gis zhes phye ste brjod par bya'o / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi ni bdag nyid kyis te / / de bas na 'grel pa las ci rigs su sbyar bar bya'o zhes bya ba smos so / / de la mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba la yon tan dang skyon du shes zhes bya ba la / / mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba'i sgra ni 'dir lam dang 'gog par gzung ste / / dper na rab tu zhi ba zhes bya ba'i sgra bzhin no /
tatra nirodhe śāntādyākāraiḥ mārge nairyāṇikādyākārair jñānaṃ / nirvāṇe guṇajñānaṃ /
# de la 'gog pa la ni zhi ba'i rnam pa la sogs pa dang lam la nges par 'byin pa'i rnam pa la sogs par shes pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa la yon tan du shes pa'o /
saṃsāro'pi duḥkhasamudayātmakaḥ /
# 'khor ba ni sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bdag nyid de /
tatrā'py anityaduḥkhādyākāraiḥ samudayapratyayādyākāraiś ca jñānaṃ / saṃsāre doṣajñānaṃ /
# de yang mi rtag pa dag sdug bsngal ba'i rnam pa la sogs pa dang kun 'byung ba dang rkyen gyi rnam pa la sogs par shes pa ni 'khor ba la skyon du shes pa'o /
parataḥ śrutveti buddhabodhisattvādibhyo nirvāṇasaṃsārayor / guṇānyathokān doṣāṃś ca śrutveti / / niryāṇārtheneti saṃsāranirgamārthena / / śrāvakayānam iti paradghoṣasaṃniśrayeṇa niryāṇāt śrāvakāyanm iti
# gzhan las thos zhes bya ba ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la sogs pa las mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis kyi yon tan dang skyon ji skad du smos pa thos pa'o / / nges par 'byung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'khor ba las byung ba'i phyir ro / / nyan thos kyi theg pa zhes bya ba ni gzhan gyi sgra la brten nas nges par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaṃ darśayati / / tenaiveti nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñānena svayam aśrutvā parato / buddhabodhasattvebhyo niryāṇārthena pratyekabuddhayānaṃ /
# nyan thos kyi theg pa zhes bya bas ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las bye brag tu ston to / / de nyid kyis zhes bya ba ni mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis la yon tan dang skyon du shes nas sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' gzhan las ma thos par bdag gis nges par 'byung ba'i phyir rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o /
svayam aśrutveti śrāvakayānād viśeṣaṇaṃ / / avikalpena jñāneneti saṃsāranirvāṇayor anabhilāpyadharmatāprativedhād / avikalpaṃ jñānaṃ /
# gzhan las ma thos par bdag gis shes par bya ba ni nyan thos kyi theg pa las bye brag tu bstan to / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis zhes bya ba ni 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i chos gnyis brjod du med par rtogs pa'i phyir rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes te /
svayam eva parato'śrutvā niryāṇārthena mahāyānaṃ /
# gzhan las ma thos par bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba'i phyir theg pa chen po'i /
atra hi jñāneneti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaḥ /
# 'dir ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las ye shes kyis bye brag tu byas so /
anye tvāhuḥ - pudgalanairātmyaviṣayeṇa guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena / parataḥ śrutvā niryāṇaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re gzhan las thos nas gang zag la bdag med pa'i yul can yon tan dang skyon du rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis nges par 'byung ba ni nyan thos kyi theg pa'o /
śravaṇanirapekṣasya svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ /
# mnyam pa la mi ltos par bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o /
dharmanairātmyaviṣayeṇā'pratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaprāpakenā'vikalpena jñānena / svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ mahāyānam ucyate /
# mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa thob par byed pa chos la bdag med pa'i yul can rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi bdag nyid kyis nges par 'byung ba ni theg pa chen po zhes bya'o /
etad vyākhyānaṃ bhāṣyeṇa virudhyate /
# rnam par bshad pa 'di ni 'grel pa dang 'gal lo /
evaṃ yānatrayakuśalasya yogamātradarśanād ātmā yogīti grāho
# de ltar theg pa gsum la mkhas pa ni rnal 'byor tsam du zad par mthong bas bdag rnal 'byor can du 'dzin pa ldog par 'gyur ro /
vyāvartate // [p.121] / [ saṃskṛtā'saṃskṛtārthaḥ }
# nga ni 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi don bstan pa'i phyir /
idānīṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtārthaṃ pratipādayann āha - / saprajñaptisahetukāt / / nimittātpraśamāt sārthāt paścimaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ // iti / / kim idaṃ paścimaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ? / ityata āha - saṃskṛtā'saṃskṛtam iti sarvapaścād udiṣṭatvāt /
# btags bcas rgyur bcas rgyu mtshan dang / / rab tu zhi ba don bcas ni / / tha ma nyid du bshad pa yin / / zhes bya ba gsungs so / / tha mar bshad pa de gang zhe na / / de'i phyir / / 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas so zhes bya ba smos te /
tatra saṃskṛtaṃ saprajñaptikāt sahetukāc ca nimittāt asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ
# thams cad kyi tha mar bshad pa'i phyir ro / / de la 'dus byas ni btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis rnam par gzhag go /
sārthāt praśamād vyavasthāpitaṃ /
# 'dus ma byas ni don dang bcas pa'i rab tu zhi bas rnam par gzhag go /
prajñaptihetunimittaṃ punar ajñānāt / / tat pradarśayann āha - tatra saprajñaptir nāmakāyādaya iti /
# btags pa dang rgyu dang rgyu mtshan yang mi shes nas de bstan par bya ba'i phyir / / de la btags pa ni ming gi tshogs la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
prajñapyete svabhāvaviśeṣau bhāvānāṃ nāmapadakāyābhyām iti / nāmapadakayau prajñaptiḥ /
# ming dang tshig gi tshogs kyi dngos po dag gi ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gnyis btags pas na ming dang tshig gi tshogs gnyis ni btags pa'o /
vyañjanakāyas tu tad ubhayābhivyañjakatvāt prajñaptiḥ /
# yi ge'i tshogs ni de gnyi ga gsal bar byed pa'i phyir btags pa'o /
hetuḥ punar bījasaṅgṛhītam ālayavijñānam iti / / tac ca sarvasāsravadharmavāsanānvitam adattaphalaṃ
# rgyu ni sa bon du bsdus pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya ba de yang zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi bag chags kyi rjes su song ba 'bras bu ma byin pa kun 'byung ba'i bden par bsdus pa nyid de /
samudayasatyasaṅgṛhītaṃ /
# 'bras bu byin pa las rnam par dbye ba'i phyir /
ata eva dattaphalād vyavacchedārthaṃ bījasaṅgṛhītam ityāha / / nimittaṃ pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṅgṛhītam ityālayavijñānam iti prakṛtaṃ /
# sa bon du bsdus pa zhes bya ba smos so / / rgyu mtshan ni gnas dang lus dang longs spyod du bsdus pa zhes bya ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
pravṛttivijñānasaṅgṛhītaśca manadugrahavikalpa iti / / tatra pratiṣṭhā bhājanalokaḥ /
# 'jug pa ni rnam par shes par bsdus pa yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog par bsdus pa'o zhes bya ba de la gnas ni snod kyi 'jig rten te /
tadābhāsam ālayavijñānaṃ / / pratiṣṭhātmanā saṅgṛhītam iti pratiṣṭhāsaṅgṛhītaṃ /
# der snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o / / gnas kyi bdag nyid du bsdus pas na gnas su bsdus pa'o / / lus su snang ba'i rang bzhin la lus su bsdus pa zhes bya'o /
dehaḥ sendriyaṃ śarīraṃ tadābhāsam ālayavijñānaṃ dehasaṅgṛhītaṃ
# lus ni dbang po dang bcas pa'i khog pa lus der snang ba'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
dehātmanopagatam ityarthaḥ / [p.122]
# lus su bsdus pa ni lus kyi bdag nyid dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
bhogasaṅgṛhītatamedevottaram uktaṃ / / tad dvayaṃ śeṣāṇi vijñānānyadhipativastutvena bhuñjata iti bhogaḥ /
# longs spyod du bsdus pa ni gong du bshad pa de nyid de / / de gnyis la yang rnam par shes pa gzhan dag dbang byed pa'i dngos por longs spyod pas na longs spyod do /
athavā annapānādiko'rtho bhujyata iti bhogaḥ /
# yang na bza' ba dang btung ba la sogs pa'i don la longs spyod pas na longs spyod de /
tan nirbhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ bhogasaṅgṛhītaṃ /
# der snang ba'i rnam par shes pa ni longs spyod du bsdus pa'o /
etat saprajñapti sahetukaṃ nimittaṃ sasamprayogaṃ / paratantrasvabhāvasaṅgṛhītatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ veditavyaṃ /
# btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan de ni mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo bsdus pa'i phyir 'dus byas su rig par bya'o /
samprayogaścaittāḥ / / tat saṃskṛtaṃ na kevalaṃ tadeveti darśayati /
# mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ni sems las byung ba ste / / 'dus byas de ni de nyid 'ba' zhig ma yin par bstan to /
kasya punas tannimittaṃ ?
# de yang gang gi rgyu mtshan zhe na /
nāmakāyādīnāṃ / / teṣāṃ tat svabhāvaviśeṣasaṃsūcakatvāt tadanusāreṇa ca
# ming gi tshogs la sogs pa'i rgyu mtshan te / / de ni de dag gi ngo bo nyid dang khyad par rjod par byed pa'i phyir ro /
svabhāvaviśeṣābhiniveśināṃ cittacaittānāṃ manaudgrahavikalpākhyānāṃ / nimittaṃ / / manaudgrahavikalpaścālayavijñānasya nimittaṃ /
# de dag gi rjes su 'brang bas rang bzhen dang bye brag la mngon par zhen pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa zhes bya ba rnams kyi rgyu mtshan yang yin no / / kha cig na re yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i rgyu mtshan te /
tasmin vāsanapoṣaṇatvād ityeke /
# de la bag chags brtas par byed pa'i phyir ro zhe'o /
anye tu manyante - svabhāvaviśeṣaprajñāpanāt prajñapter nimittaṃ
# gzhan dag ni rang bzhin bye brag tu 'dogs pas na 'dogs pa'i mtshan ma ni 'du shes te /
saṃjñāṃ nimittodgrahaṇātmiketi vacanāt /
# mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyi phyir ro /
pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṃgṛhītam ālayavijñānaṃ nidānanimittaṃ / vāsanāpoṣaṇatvāt / / ālambananimittañca mana udgrahavikalpā ālambananimittīkaraṇārthena /
# gnas dang lus dang longs spyod du bsdus pa kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni bag chags brtas par byed pa'i phyir gzhi'i rgyu mtshan no / / yid dang 'dzin pa dang rnam par rtog pa rnams ni dmigs pa mtshan mar byed pa'i phyir dmigs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang yin la /
ālambanālambana nimittaṃ cobhayathā nimittīkaraṇād iti /
# gnyi ga mtshan mar byed pa'i phyir dmigs pa dang dmigs par byed pa'i rgyu mtshan yang yin no snyam du sems so /
tatra mano yan nityaṃ manyanākāram iti /
# de la yid la gang rtag ru rlom sems pa'i rnam pa'o zhes bya ba la /
ahaṃ mameti yan nityaṃ manyate tanmata ucyate /
# bdag gam bdag gi zhes bya ba gang rtag par rlom sems pa de ni yid ces bya ste /
tac ca samprayuktam ātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmasnehātmamānaiḥ pañcabhiś ca / sarvatragair vedanāsaṃjñācetanāsparśamanaskārair iti /
# de ni bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag la chags pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang kun du 'gro ba lnga po tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa dang reg pa dang yid la byed pa dag dang mtshungs par ldan no /
udgrahaḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti viṣayasvarūpagrahaṇalakṣaṇatvāt / svasaṃvedyā ityākhyātum aśakyatvād udgraha ucyate / / vikalpo manovijñānaṃ /
# 'dzin pa ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga po zhes bya ba ni yul gyi rang bzhin gyi ngo bo 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro / / rang rig pa yin pas brjod mi nus pa'i phyir 'dzin pa zhes bya'o / / rnam par rtog pa ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa ste /
tasya dharmasvasāmānyalakṣaṇavikalpakatvād iti /
# de ni chos rnams kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la rnam par rtog pa can gyi phyir ro /
etatsarvaṃ saprajñaptisahetukaṃ nimittaṃ karmakleśābhyām / abhisaṃskṛtatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ / / asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ praśamaś ca nirodhaḥ praśamārthaś ca tathateti yuktaṃ
# btags pa dang bcas shing rgyu dang bcas pa'i rgyu mtshan 'di las nyon mongs pa gnyis kyis mngon par 'dus byas pa'i phyir 'dus byas so / / 'dus ma byas ni rab tu zhi ba'i 'gog pa dang rab tu zhi ba'i don de bzhin nyid de bzhin nyid de zhes bya ba la /
nirodhasya praśamasvarūpatvaṃ sannimittaduḥkhapraśamalakṣaṇāt / / kathaṃ tathatā praśamārtham ucyata iti ?
# rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi ba'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir 'gog pa ni rab tu zhi ba'i bar rung na / / de bzhin nyid ji ltar rab tu zhi ba'i don ces bya zhe na /
praśamasyārtha iti kṛtvā /
# rab tu zhi ba'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
nanu ca nirodhena tathatayā na kaścit sambandho'sti kathaṃ praśamārthatvaṃ / tathatāyā mārgālambanatvāt /
# 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid gnyis 'brel pa ci yang med pa snyam na / / ji ltar rab tu zhi ba'i don zhes bya zhe na / / de bzhin nyid ni lam gyi dmigs pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
mārgasya punaḥ kathaṃ praśamatvaṃ ?
# ji ltar na lam yang rab tu zhi ba nyid ces bya zhe na /
tena praśamanāt / / nirvāṇaṃ praśamaḥ praśamanāt / / anena ca praśamanāt praśamo mārgaḥ /
# des rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i phyir ro / / rab tu zhi ba'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa ni rab tu zhi ba'o / / 'dis rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i phyir lam yang rab tu zhi ba'o /
evaṃ vigrahabhedād ekābhidhānena nirvāṇamārgayor grahaṇaṃ praśama iti / / mārgasatyaṃ punaḥ kiṃ saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtaṃ ?
# de ltar na tshig rnam par sbyar ba tha dad pa'i phyir brjod pa gcig gis mya ngan las 'das pa dang lam gnyi ga rab tu zhi ba zhes bya bar bzung ngo / / ci lam gyi bden pa 'dus byas sam 'on te 'dus ma byas she na /
saṃskṛtaṃ utpādyatvāt /
# bskyed par bya ba yin pas 'dus byas so /
yadi karmakleśābhyām anabhisaṃskṛtād asaṃskṛtena ca prabhāvitād / asaṃskṛtam iti brūyān na doṣaḥ syād iti / / ityetenārthena skandhādiṣu jñānaṃ skandhādikauśalyaṃ veditavyam iti / [p.123]
# gal te las dang nyon mongs pas mngon par 'dus ma byas pa dang 'dus ma byas kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir 'dus ma byas zhes brjod na nyes pa med do / / de ltar don 'dis phung po la sogs pa shes pa ni phung po la sogs pa la mkhas par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba ni /
anekatvābhisaṃkṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ /
# thog ma du ma nyid dang ni / / bsdus dang yongs su phye ba'i don /
iti vistareṇa sarvatra vācyaṃ //3-22//
# zhes bya ba ste / / rgyas par thams cad la brjod par bya'o /
{ tattvapiṇḍārthaḥ } / tattvasya piṇḍārthaḥ / / samāsato dvividhaṃ tattvaṃ /
# de kho na'i don bsdus pa ni mdor bsdu na de kho na rnam pa gnyis so / / rgyas par ni rnam pa bcur bshad do / / de bas na mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis te zhes bya ba smos so /
vistareṇa daśavidham uktaṃ /
# rnam pa gnyis po ji lta bu zhe na /
ataḥ samāsato dvividham ityāha - ādarśatattvaṃ dṛśyatattvañca /
# me long lta bu'i de kho na dang snang ba'i de kho na'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra mūlatattvam ādarśatattvaṃ /
# de la rtsa ba'i de kho na de ni me long lta bu'i de kho na ste /
tat punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ /
# de yang ngo bo nyid gsum mo /
kim arthaṃ punas tad ādarśatattvam ityucyate ?
# ci'i phyir de la me long lta bu'i de kho na zhes bya zhe na /
śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇatattvādīnāṃ tatra darśanāt /
# mtshan nyid kyi de kho na la sogs pa lhag ma rnams der snang ba'i phyir ro /
dṛśyatattvaṃ yat lakṣaṇatattvādikaṃ pūrvanirdiṣṭaṃ navavidhaṃ /
# snang ba'i de kho na ni mtshan nyid kyi de kho na la sogs pa sngar bstan pa rnam pa dgu gang yin pa'o /
kimarthaṃ tad dṛṣyatattvam ity ucyate ?
# ci'i phyir de dag snang ba'i de kho na zhes bya zhe na /
tasya mūlatattve darśanāt nirabhimānadṛśyatattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvaṃ /
# rtsa ba'i de kho na la snang ba'i phyir ro / / nga rgyal med pa snang ba'i de kho na ni mtshan nyid kyi de kho na ste /
tena hi nirabhimāno bhavati / / pudgaladharmayor grāhyagrāhakayor bhāvābhāvayoś
# gang zag dang chos dang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa dang dngos po dang dngos po med pa la sgro mi 'dogs pa dang skur pa mi 'debs pa'i phyir des nga rgyal med par 'gyur ro /
cā'samāropānapavādaviparyāsa dṛśyatattvam aviparyāsalakṣaṇaṃ / / taddhi nityādiviparyāsapratipakṣabhūtaṃ /
# phyin ci log gi gnyen po snang ba'i de kho na ni phyin ci ma log pa'i mtshan nyid de / / de ni rtag pa la sogs par phyin ci log gi gnyen por gyur pa'o /
śrāvakayānaniryāṇadṛśyatattvaṃ phalahetumayaṃ tattvaṃ /
# nyan thos kyi theg pas nges par 'byung ba snang ba'i de kho na ni 'bras bu dang rgyu'i de kho na ste /
caturāryasatya prativedhabhāvanayā śrāvakaniryāṇaṃ /
# 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi rab tu rtogs shing bsgoms pas nyan thos nges par 'byung ngo /
mahāyānaniryāṇadrśyatattvaṃ sūkṣmaudārikatattvaṃ /
# theg pa chen pos nges par 'byung ba snang ba'i de kho na ni phra ba dang rags pa'i de kho na ste /
audārikena saṃvṛtisatyena sattvaparipācanāt sūkṣmeṇa paramārthasatyena / vimocanāt mahāyānena niryāti /
# rags pa kun rdzob kyi bden pas sems can rnams yongs su smin par byed pa dang phra ba don dam pa'i bden pas rnam par grol bar byed pa'i phyir theg pa chen pos nges par 'byung ba'o /
paravādinigrahadṛśyatattvaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ /
# phas kyi rgol ba tshar gcod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni grags pa'i de kho na'o / / ji lta zhe na /
katham ityata āha - dṛṣṭānasanniśrayeṇa yuktyā nigrahād iti /
# de'i phyir / / dpe la brten te rigs pas tshar gcod pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos te /
nigrahe lokaprasiddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ /
# tshar gcod pa la dpe ni 'jig rten du grags pa'o /
yuktiprasiddhaśabdāśrayād yuktiḥ /
# rigs pa ni rigs pas rab tu grub pa la brten pa'o /
mahāyānābhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ viśuddhijñānagocaratattvaṃ /
# theg pa chen po mngon par brjod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi de kho na ste /
[p.124] / taddhi kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarād anyasyābhidyotaka āgamaḥ /
# des ni nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gyi lung gzhan mngon par brjod pa ste /
tat punar mahāyānaṃ /
# de ni theg pa chen po'o /
sarvākārajñeyapraveśadṛśyatattvaṃ saṃgrahatattvaṃ / / tac ca pañca vastūni tatra sarvajñeyānupraveśāt /
# shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la 'jug pa snang ba'i de kho na la bsdu ba'i de kho na dngos po lnga ste / / de ni shes par bya ba thams cad la 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
avitathatā'bhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ /
# ma nor ba de bzhin nyid mngon par brjod pa snang ba'i de kho na ni rab tu dbye ba'i de kho na ste /
tena hi bhāvānāmavitathatathatā'nanyatathatayor abhidyotanāt /
# des dngos po rnams kyi ma nor ba de bzhin nyid dang gzhan ma yin pa de bzhin nyid mngon par brjod pa'i phyir ro /
ātmagrāhavastusarvābhisandhipraveśadṛśyatattvañceti kauśalayatattvaṃ / / tena hy ātmagrāhavastu sarvābhiprāyamukhena praviśatīti yathā pūrvam
# bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gzhi la dgongs pa thams cad rtogs par snang ba'i de kho na zhes bya ba ni mkhas pa'i de kho na ste / / des bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gzhi la dgongs pa thams cad kyi sgo nas rtogs te /
uktaṃ daśabhir abhiprāyaiḥ skandhādiṣv ātmagrāhapravṛttitvaṃ /
# bsam pa bcu po dag gis phung po la sogs pa la bdag tu 'dzin pa 'jug par sngar ji skad du bstan pa'o /
tattvapiṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhadhāraṇārtham arthād grantham ākarṣatīti /
# de kho na'i don bsdus pa smos pa ni bde blag tu 'dzin pa'i phyir te / / don gyis tshig 'dren pa'i phyir ro /
asammohāparikhedārthañca paridṛṣṭādhikāraparyantasya hi na parikheda
# rmongs pa med pa dang yongs su skyo ba yang med par bya ba'i phyir te /
upajñāyate nāpi sammoho yathoddeśanirdeśādhigamād utapdyate /
# skabs kyi mgo mjug yongs su mthong na yongs su skyo ba mi skye'o /
uktaṃ tattvaṃ // / // āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi / ramatyuparacitāyāṃ tattvaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ samāptaḥ // / %	pratipakṣabhāvanā'vasthāphalaparicchedaścaturthaḥ / { pratipakṣabhāvanā } [p.125] / tattvapratipādanānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā vaktavyā tatrā'vasthā / phalaprāptiś ca / / atas tatpratipādanārthaṃ caturthaparicchedārambhaḥ /
# ji ltar bstan pa bzhin du bshad pa rtogs pas rmongs pa yang mi 'byung ngo / / de kho na bshad zin to / / bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa las de kho na'i le'ur bcad pa ste gsum pa'i 'grel bshad do / / de kho na bshad pa'i 'og tu gnyen po bsgom pa dang de'i gnas dang 'bras bu thob pa bshad dgos te / / de bas na de bstan pa'i phyir le'ur bcad pa bzhi pa brtsams so /
tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt pratipakṣabhāvanāpratibaddhatvāc ca tad / avasthāphalaprāptyor uddeśaḥ /
# de kho na'i 'og tu bstan pa dang gnyen po bsgom pa la rag lus pa'i phyir de'i gnas dang 'bras bu thob pa gnyis kyang smos so /
sūtre pratipakaṣatvena bodhipakṣo'numata iti pradarśanārtham āha -
# bstan pa'i mdor byas pa las gnyen po ni byang chub kyi phyogs su bzhed par bstan pa'i phyir /
pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhipakṣyabhāveneti /
# gnyen po bsgom pa ni byang chub kyi phyogs bsgom pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
te hi yathoktāvaraṇavipakṣaprahāṇāya bhāvyamānaḥ prabhavantīti
# de dag bsgoms na mi mthun pa'i phyogs sgrib pa ji skad bstan pa rnams spang bar bya ba la mthu yod par 'gyur bas gnyen po rnams zhes bya'o /
pratipakṣā ucyante / / te punaḥ saptatriṃśat - catvāri smṛtypasthānāni yāvadāryāṣṭāṅga
# de rnams kyang sum cu rtsa bdun te / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi nas 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i bar du'o /
mārgāḥ / / tad bhāvanā bṛṃhaṇāropaṇā abhyāso bahulā kriyeti paryāyāḥ /
# de rnams bsgom pa ni spel ba dang bskyed pa dang goms par bya ba dang lan mang du bya ba zhes bya ba'i rnam grangs so /
sedānīṃ vaktavyā tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt /
# de yang de kho na'o 'og tu bstan pa'i phyir de yang brjod par bya'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaiva pūrvam ucyate nānyā / bodhipakṣabhāvanā ?
# byang chub kyi phyogs bsgoms pa la ci'i phyir dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid thog mar bshad kyi gzhan ni ma yin zhe na /
āha - tatra tāvadādau -
# de la re zhig dang por /
dauṣṭhulyāt tarṣahetutvāt
# gnas ngan len phyir sred rgyu'i phyir /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher smos so /
tatreti bodhipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ / / tāvacchabdārthaḥ kramārthaḥ / / ādau tāvat smṛtyupasthānabhāvanocyate /
# de la zhes bya ba ni byang chub kyi phyogs bsgoms pa la'o / / re zhig ces bya ba ni rim gyi don te / / thog mar dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ji bshad la /
paścād anyeṣām apīti /
# gzhan yang phyis bshad do zhes bya bar 'gyur ro /
nirvāṇasaṃsāryor guṇadoṣā'navabodhāt / / saṃskāreṣu sukhaśucinityātmābhiniveśena bālānāṃ bhavabhoge'bhivacanaṃ [p.126] / nirvāṇārthaṃ trāsaḥ / / sa ca guṇadoṣānavabodhaḥ sukhādyabhiniveśaś ca satyadarśanād vinivartata / ityataḥ saṃsārād udvajanārthaṃ nirvāṇe cābhimukhīkaraṇārthaṃ / catuḥsatyāvatārāya smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaivādāv uktā / / kāyena hi dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyata iti /
# mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'khor ba gnyis kyi yon tan dang nyes pa mo rtogs pa'i phyir 'du byed rnams la bde ba dang gtsang ba dang rtag pa dang bdag tu mngon par zhen pas byis pa rnams srid pa dang longs spyod la mngon par dga' zhing mya ngan las 'das pas skrag go / / yon tan dang nyes pa ma rtogs pa dang bde ba la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa de yang bden pa mthong nas ldog par 'gyur te / / de'i phyir 'khor ba la skyo bar bya ba'i don dang mya ngan las 'das pa mngon sum du bya ba'i don du bden pa bzhi la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid thog mar bshad do / / lus kyis ni gnas ngan len rab tu ston zhes bya ba la /
dauṣṭhulyaṃ duḥsthitatā / / tathā hi pratidinam abhisaṃskriyamāṇo vikriyata eva kāya iti kāyena / dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate /
# gnas ngan len ni ngan par gnas pa ste / / 'di ltar nyin gcig bzhin mngon par 'dus byas kyang lus 'gyur ba nyid pas lus kyis ni gnas ngan len rab tu ston to /
tataś ca kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati /
# de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go /
kim artham etad ityāha - tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti /
# de ci'i phyir zhe na / / de'i mtshan nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
yasmād duḥkhasatyasya sadauṣṭhulyāḥ saṃskārāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ svabhāvaḥ
# 'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i mtshan nyid ngo bo nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams yin la /
kāyena ca dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati / /
# lus kyis kyang gnas ngan len du rab tu ston pas / / de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go /
dauṣṭhulyaṃ na vijñāyata ityata āha - dauṣṭhulyaṃ hi saṃskāraduḥkhateti
# gnas ngan len mi shes pas de'i phyir / / gnas ngan len ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid de zhes bya ba smos so /
saṃskāro bhāvanām utpattiḥ /
# 'du byed ni dngos po rnams kyi skye ba'o /
sa ca sarvaviplavastv iti dauṣṭhulyamāryāṇāṃ pratikūlatvāc ca duḥkhatā / yathoktaṃ -
# de yang gnod pa thams cad kyi gzhi yin pas gnas ngan len yin la / / 'phags pa rnams dang mi mthun pa'i phyir sdug bsngal nyid de / / ji skad du /
anartho janmedaṃ sati hi janane santi ripavo
# skye 'di gnod yin pa skye ba yod na rga dang 'chi ba dang /
jarā-mṛtyu-vyādhi-vyasana-bandha-prabhṛtayaḥ /
# nad dang phongs pa gsod dang 'ching ba la sogs pa dgra rnams yod /
anarthās te na syur yadi na bhavato nāśavibhavā-
# gal te 'jigs mad skye ba med gyur gnod pa de dag med /
vajāte vṛkṣe syān na hi dahanadavavāyucyutir api //
# shing skyes med na me dang rlung dang nags mes 'gyel mi 'gyur / / zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
tayeti saṃskāraduḥkhatayā na vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatābhyāṃ / tayor āvyāpitvāt saṃskāraduḥKhatānimittatvāc ca /
# des zhes bya ba 'di 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyis so / / 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid gnyis kyis ni ma yin te; de gnyis khyab pa ma yin pa dang 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvaṃ sāsravaṃ vastvāryā duḥkhatā paśyanti nā'nāsavaṃ mārgasatyasya
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po thams cad 'phags pas sdug bsngal du gzigs kyi zag pa med pa ni ma yin te /
janmotpattipratipakṣatvāt na tu pṛthagjanā viparyāsasthānāśrayatvāt / / sūtre'py uktaṃ - samāsataḥ pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham iti /
# lam gyi bden pa na che'i gnyen po yin pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci log gi bsam pa nyams pa'i phyir so so'i skye bo rnams kyis ni ma yin no / / mdo'i sde las kyang mdor na nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga ni sdug bsngal lo zhes gsungs so /
saṃskāraduḥkhatā'karmaṇyatetyanye / / na dauṣṭhulyam akarmaṇyātetyapare /
# gzhan dag na re 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid ni las su mi rung ba'o zhes zer ro / / gzhan na re las su mi rung ba ni gnas ngan len ma yin no /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# ci'i phyir zhe na /
akarmaṇyātāyāḥ sāsravatvād avaśyaṃ sāsravatāṃ / bījakāraṇotpannā'bhyupagantavyā /
# las su mi rung ba'i zag pa dang bcas pa'i phyir nges par zag pa dang bcas pa ni sa bon gyi rgyu las byung bar khas blang dgos na /
sā tv abījāpyarthasantāne kadācid āhārādyapacārād bhavati /
# de ni dgra bcom pa'i rgyud la sa bon med kyang res 'ga' kha zas dang gnas pa la sogs pa drags pa las 'byung ngo /
na cāsau dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhavitum arhatya nāsravatvād iti /
# de ni zag pa med pa yin pa'i phyir gnas ngan len zhes byar mi rung ngo zhes zer ro /
ataś ca sāsravadharmabījam ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ / dauṣṭhulyenātreṣyate / / ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhā'sukhā'duḥkhasahitaḥ kāyastat phalaṃ /
# de bas na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos kyis sa bon gnas pa ni 'dir gnas ngan len du 'dod do / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal ba yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang lhan cig pa'i lus 'di ni de'i 'bras bu'o /
tasmāt sukhādyavakāśasahitena kāyena pratikṣaṇabhāvinā tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ
# de bas na bde ba la sogs pa'i gnas skabs dang lhan cig pa skad cig re re la 'byung ba'i lus kyi gnas ngan len de rab tu ston te /
prabhāvyate pratīyata ityarthaḥ /
# shes par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tadyathā khalavilāntargataṃ bījam aṅkureṇeti / / tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati / / atra kāraṇam āha - [p.127]
# dper na myu gus g yul gyi ser ga'i nang du song ba'i sa bon mngon pa lta bu'o / / de'i phyir lus la yongs su brtags pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go / / 'dir rgyu smos pa /
tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti sabījasaṃskārātmakatvād / ityarthaḥ / / saṃskāraduḥkhatā hi vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatādauṣṭhulyābhyām / anugatatvāt kāraṇatvāc ca dauṣṭhulyam ityktā /
# de'i mtshan nyid ni gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / sa bon dang bcas pa'i 'du byed kyi bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid ni 'gyur ba dang sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid ngag gnas ngan len gnyis kyi rjes su song ba dang de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal du bshad do /
ata eva saṃskāraduḥkhatayā sarvasāsravaṃ vastvāryaiḥ duḥkhatvenālokita / evaṃ kāyasmṛtyupasthānena duḥkhasatyam avataratīti /
# de bas na 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyis zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po thams cad 'phags pa rnams kyis sdug bsngal nyid du gzigs so / / de ltar na lus dran pa nye bar gzhag pas sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug go /
tṛṣṇāhetur vedanā - avidyāsaṃsparśajetyabhiprāyāt anāsravāyā atad
# sred pa'i rgyu ni tshor ba ste / / zhes bya ba ni ma rig pa'i 'dus te reg pa las byung bar dgos pa ste /
hetutvāt / / tatra sukhā vedanā tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ /
# zag pa med pa ni de'i rgyu ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / de la bde ba'i tshor ba ni de dang ldan zhing mi 'bral bar sred pa'i rgyu'o /
duḥkhā tad asaṃyogaviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ /
# sdug bsngal ni de dang mi phrad pa dang bral bar sred pa'i rgyu'o /
aduḥkhasukhā tad avasthābhir atitṛṣṇāyās tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyāś ca / kasyāṃcit samāptau hetur iti /
# sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa ni snyoms par 'jug pa 'ga' zhig la de'i gnas skabs la mngon par dga' ba'i sred pa'i rgyu dang de dang phrad cing mi 'bral par sred pa'i rgyu yin no /
sa duḥkhavedanayā spṛṣṭaḥ kāmasukham abhinandatīti vacanāt duḥkhāpi / vedanā sukhāyāḥ tṛṣṇayā hetur bhavati /
# de sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas reg na 'dod pa'i bde ba la mngon par dga'o zhes 'byung ba'i phyir / / sdug bsngal ba'i tshor ba yang bde ba la sred pa'i rgyur 'gyur te /
tat parīkṣayā samudayasatyam avatarati /
# de la yongs su brtags pas kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug go /
sa hi vedanāṃ svarūpataḥ kāraṇataḥ kāryato'nityato / duḥkhataścopaparīkṣamāṇaḥ samudayasatyam avatarati tṛṣṇāṃ tat
# de la tshor ba rnams la rang bzhin dang 'bras bu dang mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba nyid du nye bar yongs su rtog na kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug ste /
kāryatvenāvagacchatītyarthaḥ / / tṛṣṇā hi sūtre samudayasatyam ityuktā /
# sred pa ni de'i 'bras bur khong du chud do zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / mdo sde las sred pa ni kun 'byung ba'i bden par gsungs te /
ko duḥkhasamudayaḥ ?
# sdug bsngal kun 'byung ba gang zhe na /
paṭhyate - tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikānandā rāgasahagateti vistaraḥ /
# yang 'byung ba'i sred pa dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang ldan pa'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ngo /
evaṃ vedanāsmṛtyupasthānena samudayasatyam avatarati / / ātmābhiniveśavastu cittam iti / / anyasya nityādiguṇaviśiṣṭasyātmano'bhāvād ātmābhiniveśālambanaṃ / cittam eva / / tasmāt tat parīkṣayā nirodhasatyam avatarati śāntatvena /
# de ltar tshor ba dran pa nye bar gzhag pas kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la 'jug go / / bdag tu mngon par zhen pa'i gzhi ni sems te zhes bya ba la / / rtag pa la sogs pa'i yon tan khyad par can gyi bdag gzhan med pas na bdag tu mngon par zhen pa'i dmigs pa ni sems nyid do / / de bas na de yongs su brtags pas 'gog pa'i bden pa la zhi ba nyid du 'jug ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - ātmocchedabhayāpagamād iti / / citte hy anityatvādiparīkṣayā'tmābhiniveśo vyāvartate duḥkhasaṃjñā / pravartate /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / bdag chad bar dogs pa'i 'jigs pa med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / sems la mi rtag pa la sogs par yongs su brtags pas bdag tu mngon par zhen pa ldog cing sdug bsngal du 'du shes 'byung ngo /
ataścātmocchedabhayāpagamād duḥkhamātrasyocchedān nirodhasatyaṃ / śāntatvenāvataratīti / / evaṃ cittasmṛtyupasthānena nirodhasatyam avataratīti /
# de'i phyir bdag chad pa'i 'jigs pa med pas sdug bsngal ba tsam zhig gcod pa'i phyir 'gog pa'i bden pa la zhi ba nyid du 'jug ste / / de ltar sems dran pa nye bar gzhag pas 'gog pa'i bden pa la 'jug ces bya'o /
dharmaparīkṣayā sāṅkleśikavyāvadānikadharmāsaṃmohān mārgasatyam / avataratīti / / tatra sāṅkleśikā dharmāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ / / vyāvadānikās tu kleśopakleśapratipakṣabhūtāḥ premamaitryādayaḥ /
# chos la yongs su brtags pas kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i chos la rmongs pa med pa'i phyir lam gyi bden pa la 'jug go zhes bya ba de la kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos rnams ni nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams so / / rnam par byang ba rnams ni nye ba'i gnyen por gyur pa rnams te / / mi sdug pa dang byams pa la sogs pa'o /
teṣāṃ sāṅkleśikānāṃ vyāvadānikānāñca vipakṣapratipakṣabhāvaṃ / buddhvā sarvopadravātyantaprahāṇopāye mārgasatye'bhimukhībhavati / / evaṃ dharmasmṛtyupasthānena mārgasatyam avataratīti /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba de rnams la gnyen po dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi ngo bor shes nas gnod pa thams cad gtan du spang ba'i thabs lam gyi bden pa la mngon du phyogs par 'gyur te / / de ltar chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pas lam gyi bden pa la 'jug go /
avatāro'tra pratyekaṃ satye satyalakṣaṇāvabodhaḥ / / tatra kāyasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyato'nātmato'pi / anekā'śucidravyasvabhāvato'pi aśucibījato'pi aśuciniṣyandato'pi / aśucisthitihetuto'pi aśucivikārato'pi phenabhaṅga ivāsārato'pi gatito'pi / yonito'pi /
# 'jug pa ni 'dir bden pa so so la bden pa'i mtshan nyid du rtogs pa'o / / de la lus dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ni mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa dang mi gtsang ba du ma'i rdzas kyi rang bzhin dang mi gtsang ba'i sa bon dang mi gtsang ba'i rgyu mthun pa dang mi gtsang ba gnas pa'i rgyu dang mi gtsang bar 'gyur ba dang dbu ba rdos pa bzhin du snying po med pa dang 'gro ba dang skye gnas yin par bsgom mo /
vedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā punar / anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmato'pi svalakṣaṇato'pi hetuto'pi phalato'pi / dhātubhūmigatito'pi kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtato'pi vipakṣapratipakṣato'pi / / bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā evañcānupalambhākāreṇa
# tshor ba dang sems dang chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams bsgom pa yang mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba dang stong pa dang bdag med pa dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dang rang gi mtshan nyid dang rgyu dang 'bras bu dang khams dang sa dang 'gro ba dang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po yin par bsgom mo / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa ni 'di lta bu yang yin la rnam par rtog pa spangs pa'i phyir mi dmigs pa'i rnam par yang bsgom mo /
ca vikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ / / smṛtyupasthānānāṃ tu prajñāsvābhāvye'pi smṛtyupasthānavacanaṃ / smṛtibalenopasthānād etāsāṃ prajñānāṃ smṛtyupasthānam ucyate //4-1// [p.128] / { catvāri samyakprahāṇāni } / smṛtyupasthānabhāvanānantaraṃ samyakprahāṇabhāvanoktā /
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams shes rab kyi rang bzhin yin du zin kyang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i tshig ni dran pa'i stobs kyis nye bar gnas pa'i phyir ram / / 'di dag gis dran pa nye bar gnas pas dran pa nye bar gzhag pa zhes bya'o / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa'i 'og tu yang dag par spong ba bsgom pa bshad de /
kiṃ kāraṇam ata āha
# de ci'i phyir zhe na /
yasmāt - / parijñāte vipakṣe ca
# de'i phyir 'di ltar / / mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po rnams /
iti vistaraḥ / / smṛtyupasthānabhāvanayeti /
# rnam pa thams cad yongs shes nas / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
aviśeṣābhidhāne'pi dharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanayaiveti veditavyaṃ / / dhātubhūmyavakāśaiḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇādyākārais tathā
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgoms nas zhes khyad par med par brjod kyang chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bsgom pa nyid yin par rig par bya'o /
sāsravānāsravanadhātubhūmi-śaikṣāśaikṣādyākārais tathā / sāsravānāsravadhātubhūmi-śaikṣāśaikṣādibhedena ca vipakṣe pratipakṣe / ca sarvaprakāra parijñāte / / vipakṣāgamāyeti / / vipakṣāpagamamo'trotpannānāṃ prabandhacchedo'nutpannānāṃ cānutpādaḥ /
# khams dang sa'i spangs pa dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang de bzhin du zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa dang khams dang sa dang slob pa dang mi slob pa la sogs pa'i bye brag gis mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po rnam pa thams cad du yongs su shes na mi mthun pa'i phyogs gsal ba ni 'dir skyes pa rnams kyi rgyun chad pa dang ma skyes pa rnams mi skyed pa'o / / gnyen po bskyed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la / / gnyen po bskyed pa ni skyes pa rnams kyi rgyun gyis rjes su 'jug pa dang ma skyes pa rnams skyed pa'o /
pratipakṣopagamāya ceti / / pratipakṣāgama utpannānāṃ prabandhānuvṛttir anutpannānāñcotpādaḥ /
# brtson 'grus rnam pa bzhi rab tu 'byung zhes byang ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po gnyis skyes pa dang ma skyes pa tha dad pas brtson 'grus rnam pa bzhi 'byung ste /
vīryaṃ caturdhā pravartata iti vipakṣapratipakṣayor utpanānutpannabhedena / caturdhā vīryasya pravṛttiḥ / / utpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāyeti vistara
# sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spang ba'i phyir zhe rgya cher 'byung ngo zhes bya ba 'dis ni lung gis brtson 'grus nyid rnam pa bzhi 'byung bar ston to / / rgya cher zhes bya ba ni tshig lhag ma dang sbyar ba'o /
itīdam āgamena vīryasyaiva caturdhā pravṛttiṃ darśayati /
# de la 'di ni tshig lhag ma ste sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spangs pa'i phyir 'dun pa skyed do /
vistaravacanena śeṣagranthābhisambandhaḥ / / tatrāyāṃ śeṣo granghaḥ - prahāṇāya chandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam / ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samyakpradadhātīti /
# 'bad do / / brtson 'grus rtsom mo / / sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang dag par rab tu 'jog go zhes bya ba dang de bzhin du sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams mi bskyed pa'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
evam anutpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām anutpādāya / chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ /
# de bzhin du dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams bskyed pa'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do zhes rgya cher bya'o /
evam anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām utpādaya chandañjanayatīti
# dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams gnas pa dang phyir zhing 'byung ba dang yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir 'dun pa bskyed do /
vistaraḥ /
# 'bad do /
utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyai / asampramoṣāya paripūraṇāya chandañjanayati vyāyacchate vīryam / ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti / / samyak pradadhāti / / utpannānāṃ sthitir aparihāṇiḥ / / bhūyobhāvaḥ prabandhenotpādaḥ / / paripūriḥ prakarṣagamanaṃ / / chandañjanayatīti sagauravodyaktavīryasamṛddhiṃ darśayati /
# brtson 'grus brtsam mo / / sems rab tu 'dzin to / / yang dag par rab tu 'jog go zhes bya ba'o / / skyes pa rnams gnas pa ni yongs su mi nyams pa'o / / phyir zhing 'byung ba ni rgyun du skye ba'o / / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba ni phul du phyin par 'gyur ba'o / / 'dun pa skyed ces bya ba ni gus par brtson 'grus bsgom pa'i sbyor ba ston to /
vyāyacchata iti kausīdyaprahāṇāya kāyacitte'bhimukhīkarotītyarthaḥ / / vīryam ārabhata iti layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇārthaṃ /
# 'bad ces bya ba ni le lo spangs te / / lus dang sems mngon du byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / brtson 'grus rtsom zhes bya ba ni bying ba dang rgod pa bsal ba'i phyir ro /
katham ārabheta ?
# ji ltar rtsom zhe na /
līnaṃ cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samvejanīyapramodānīyadharmamanaskāraiḥ /
# yang dag pa shes par bya ba dang dga' bar bya ba'i chos yid la byed pas bying ba'i sems rab tu 'dzin to /
uddhataṃ cittaṃ tasminnevālambane samyak pradadhāti
# sems rgod par gyur na dmigs pa de nyid la yang dag par rab tu 'jog ste /
samvejanīyapramodanīyadharmamanaskārair dhārayatītyarthaḥ / / evañca [p.129] / samyakpradhānāni vīryātmakānīti jñāpitam bhavati / / samyag ebhiḥ kāyavāṅmanāṃsi dhārayantīti samyakpradhānāni //4-2// / { catvāraḥ ṛddhipādāḥ } / karmañatā sthites tatra
# 'dzin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de ltar yang dag par spong ba rnams ni brtson 'grus kyi rang bzhin du bstan pa yin te / / 'di rnams kyis lus dang ngag dang yid yang dag par 'dzin pas na yang dag par 'dzin pa rnams so / / der gnas las su rung ba nyid /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatreti tasyāṃ vipakṣapratipakṣāyāpagamavīryabhāvanāyāṃ /
# ces rgya cher 'byung ba la der zhes bya ba ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs bsal ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom pa de la'o /
karmaṇyatā cittasthiteḥ sarvārthasamṛddhiyogyatā / / sā ca karmaṇyatā chandavīryacittamīmāṃsādhipatyaprabhavetyata āha -
# sems gnas pa'i las su rung ba nyid ni don thams cad 'byor par nus pa nyid de las su rung ba nyid do / / las su rung ba de yang 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems pa dang dpyod pa'i dbang gis byung bas na de'i phyir /
karmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā iti / / sarvasyābhijñādikasyārthasya samṛddhi ṛddhiḥ / / tasyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthena ṛddhipādā ṛddhihetava ityarthaḥ / / ata evāha - sarvārthasamṛddhihetutvād iti /
# las su rung ba nyid ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi po dag ste zhes bya ba smos so; / / mngon par shes pa la sogs pa don thams cad 'grub par byed pa ni rdzu 'phrul lo / / de'i gnas yin pa'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa zhes bya ste / / rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
te punaścandasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādaḥ
# de bas na don thams cad 'byor pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro zhes smos te /
vīryasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādā cittasamādhiḥ / prahāṇasaṃskārasamanavāgata ṛddhipādaḥ mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ / prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipāda iti / / tatra cchandsamādhir yadā chandādhipatyād vīryabhāvanāyāṃ sagauravaṃ
# de dag kyang 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang sems kyi ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa zhes bya ba'o / / de la 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe 'dun pa'i dbang gis brtson 'grus rtsom pa la gus par 'jug pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
pravartamānaḥ spṛśati cittasyakāgratāṃ / / vīryasamādhir yadā vīryam ārabhamāṇaḥ sātatyaprayogāt spṛśati
# brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe brtson 'grus rtsom pa na rtag par sbyor bas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
cittasyaikāgratāṃ / / cittasamādhir yadā pūrvasamādhibījam āgamya citta eva cittaṃ dhārayan
# sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe sngon gyi ting nge 'dzin gyi sa bon la brten nas sems 'dzin cing gang sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ / / mīmāmsāsamādhir yadālambanapravicito'nuspṛśati cittasyaikāgratām iti
# dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang gi tshe dmigs pa rab tu rnam par 'byed pa na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
sthitiratra cittasthitiḥ samādhir veditavya iti samādhigrahaṇaṃ
# gnas pa ni 'dir sems gnas pa ste / / ting nge 'dzin du rig par bya'o zhes bya ba la /
saṃskṛtalakṣaṇād vyavacchedārthaṃ /
# ting nge 'dzin smos pa ni 'dus byas kyi mtshan nyid las dbye ba'i phyir ro /
yata ārabdhavīryasya cittakarmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā bhavanti ataḥ / samyak prahāṇānantaraṃ ṛddhipādā nirdiṣṭāḥ /
# 'di ltar brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni sems las su rung ba nyid rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhir gyur pa de'i phyir yang dag par spong ba'i 'og tu rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams bstan to /
sā punaḥ karmaṇyatā [p.130] / kim prayojanā kiṃ hetukā cetyata āha - / pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārabhāvanānvayā videtavyeti /
# las su rang ba de yang dgos pa ni gang / / rgyu ni gang zhe na de'i phyir / / nyes pa lnga spang ba'i phyir 'du byed bsgom pa'i rgyu las byung bar rig par bya'o zhes bya ba smos so /
anvayo hetuḥ //4-3//
# nyes pa lnga po de dag mi shes nas /
{ pañca doṣāḥ } / te ca pañcadoṣā na vijñāyanta ityataḥ pṛcchati katame pañca doṣā iti /
# de'i phyir / / nyes pa lnga po de dag gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de dag bstan pa'i phyir /
tat pradarśayann āha -
# le lo dag ni gdams ngag rnams /
kausīdyam avavādasya sammoṣo laya udbhavaḥ / / iti vistaraḥ / / ete hi ṣaḍdoṣā ityata āha - tatra layauddhatyam eko doṣaḥ kriyata iti
# brjed dang bying dang rgod pa dang / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / de dag ni nyes pa drug tu 'gyur ro snyam pa la / / de'i phyir / / de la bying ba dang rgod pa ni nyes pa gcig tu bsdu'o zhes bya ba smos te /
pañca bhavanti /
# de'i phyir lngar 'gyur ro /
tatra kausīdyaṃ prayogakāle doṣas tenāprayogāt /
# de la le lo ni sbyor ba'i tshe na nyes pa ste / / des mi sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
udyuktasyāvavādasammoṣo doṣas tena cittasamādhānabhāvāt /
# brtson pa'i tshe gdams ngag brjed pa ni nyes pa ste / / des sems mnyam par gzhag pa med pa'i phyir ro /
samāhitasya layauddhatyaṃ doṣastena cittakarmaṇyatā'bhāvāt /
# mnyam par gzhag pa la bying ba dang rgod pa ni nyes pa ste / / des sems las su rung ba med pa'i phyir ro /
anabhisaṃskāro layauddhatyapraśamanakāle doṣaḥ /
# bying ba dang rgod par gyur pa'i tshe mngon par 'du mi byed pa nyes pa'o /
anabhisaṃskāra upekṣā tayā tad dvayāśamanāt /
# mngon par 'du mi byed pa ni btang snyoms te / / des de gnyis rab tu zhi bar mi byed pa'i phyir ro /
abhisaṃskāraḥ praśāntau doṣa iti / / abhisaṃskāraścetanā /
# rab tu zhi ba'i tshe ni mngon par 'du byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni nyes pa zhes bya bar snyegs so / / mngon par 'du byed pa ni sems pa'o /
layauddhatyavigamāddhi samatāprāptatvāt praśāntam ity ucyate //4-4//
# bying ba dang rgod pa dang bral bas mnyam pa nyid du gyur pa'i phyir rab tu zhi ba zhes bya'o /
{ aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ } [p.131] / prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ prahāṇāya saṃskārāḥ / / kasya prahāṇāya ?
# spang bar bya ba'i phyir 'du byed rnams ni spong ba'i 'du byed rnams so / / gang spang ba'i phyir zhe na /
anantaroktānāṃ pañcānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ prahāṇāya / / yadyevaṃ tena vaktavyam eṣāṃ prahāṇāya katham aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārā
# bshad ma thag pa'i nyes pa lnga rnams spang ba'i phyir ro / / gal te de lta na des de dag spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa brjod dgos so /
vyavasthāpyanta iti / / tatra kausīdyaprahāṇāya catvāraś chandavyāyāmaśraddhāprasrabdhayaḥ / / tatra cchando'bhilāṣaḥ /
# de la le lo spang ba'i phyir bzhi ste / / 'dun pa dang rtsol ba dang dad pa dang shin tu sbyangs pa'o / / de la 'dun pa ni 'dod pa'o /
vyāyāmo vīryaṃ /
# rtsol ba ni brtson 'grus so /
śraddhā'bhisampratyayaḥ /
# dad pa ni mgon par yid ches pa'o /
prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatā /
# shin tu sbyangs pa ni las su rung ba nyid do /
kathaṃ punar ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya vyavasthāpyanta ityata āha - te
# ji ltar na le lo spang ba'i phyir de dag rnam par gzhag ce na / / de'i phyir /
punar yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ /
# de dag kyang go rims bzhin du rig par bya ste /
āśrayo'rthāśritas tasya nimittaṃ phalam eva ca / iti /
# gnas dang de la gnas pa dang / / rgyu dang 'bras bu nyid du'o /
ato'nyonyaprabhāvitatvād ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya samvartanta iti
# zhes bya ba smos so / / de dag gcig las gcig 'byung bas na le lo spong bar 'gyur ba ston to /
darśayati - āśrayaśchando vyāyāmasya āśrito vyāyāmaḥ /
# rtsol ba'i gnas ni 'dun pa'o / / gnas pa ni rtsol ba ste /
abhilāṣasya vyāyāmapūrvakatvāt /
# 'dod pa ni rtsol ba'i sngon du 'gro ba'i phyir ro /
tasyāśrayasya chandasya nimittaṃ śraddhā /
# gnas 'dun pa'i rgyu ni dad pa ste / / ji lta zhe na /
katham ityato bravīti - sampratyaye saty abhilāṣād iti /
# de'i phyir / / yid ches par gyur na 'dod pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
śraddadhānasya hi hetuphale kriyābhilāṣo bhavati /
# rgyu dang 'bras bu la dad pa dang ldan pa ni bya ba la 'dod par 'gyur ro /
tasyāśritasya vyāyāmasya phalaṃ prasrabdhiḥ /
# gnas pa rtsol ba de'i 'bras bu ni shin tu sbyangs pa ste /
katham ityata āha - prārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣā'dhigamād iti /
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / brtson 'grus brtsams na ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par thob pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
samādhiviśeṣagamanaṃ hi prasrabdhinimittaṃ /
# ting nge 'dzin khyad par du 'gro ba ni shin tu sbyangs pa'i rgyu'o /
ata ārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣagamanāt prasrabdhir vyāyāmaphalam / ityuktaṃ /
# de'i phyir / / brtson 'grus brtsams pa'i ting nge 'dzin khyad par du 'gro bas shin tu sbyangs pa ni rtsol ba'i 'bras bur bshad do /
tathā hy ārabdhavīryasya dauṣṭhulyavitarkādyapakṣālavigamāt pramoda / utpadyate /
# de ltar brtson 'grus brtsams pa gnas ngan len gyi rnam par rtog pa'i nyes pa dang bral bas dga' ba skye'o /
manaḥpramodāt kāyacittayoḥ prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatālakṣaṇatā /
# yid dga' bas lus dang sems gnyis shin tu sbyangs te las su rung ba nyid kyi mtshan nyid do /
tataḥ samādhiviśeṣagamanam iti / / atra ca vīryaṃ sahetukaṃ saphalaṃ ca kausīdyapratipakṣeṇoktaṃ /
# de bas na ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par thob pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'o / / 'dir ni brtson 'grus rgyu dang bcas shing 'bras bu dang bcas pa le lo'i gnyen por bshad do /
caturṇāṃ doṣāṇāṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ pratipakṣa iti / / tatra smṛtir avavādasammoṣasya pratipakṣaḥ /
# nyes pa bzhi'i gnyen por grangs bzhin no zhes bya ba de la / / dran pa ni gdams ngag brjed pa'i gnyen po'o /
samprayojanyaṃ layauddhatyasya /
# shes bzhin ni bying ba dang rgod pa'i gnyen po'o /
cetanā'nabhisaṃskārasya /
# sems pa ni mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i gnyen po'o /
abhisaṃskārasyopekṣeti saṃskāropekṣā'tra veditavyā /
# btang snyoms ni mngon par 'du byed pa'i gnyen po ste / / 'dir 'du byed kyi btang snyoms su shes par bya'o /
smṛtyādīnāṃ punar lakṣaṇavivakṣayedam āha - te punaḥ smṛtyādayo / veditavyā yathākramam iti /
# dran pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid brjod par 'dod pa'i phyir / / de dag kyang ngan pa la sogs pa rig par bya ste go rims bzhin zhes bya ba 'di smos so /
smṛtir ālambane'sammoṣa iti / [p.132]
# dran pa ni dmigs pa ma brjed pa'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ba la /
vistarīkṛtamālambanam iti cittasthāpanīyam avavādavastv abhilapanam / ityartaḥ /
# dran pa ni dmigs pa ma brjed pa'o zhes bya ba ni sems gnas par bya ba'i gdams ngag yid kyis brjod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
samprajanyaṃ smṛtyasampramoṣe sati layauddhatyāvabodha iti / / upasthitasmṛtir hi samprajanyavān bhavatyevetyata āha - smṛtyasampramoṣe
# shes bzhin ni dran pa ma brjed par gyur na bying ba dang rgod pa rtogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni dran pa nye bar gnas pa shes bzhin dang ldan par 'gyur ro /
satīti / / anubuddhyā layauddhatyaṃ śamathavipaśyane yuganaddhādaprayatnena / pravartetetyarthaḥ / / upekṣeti viṣayāntarānabhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ /
# de'i phyir dran pa ma brjed par gyur na zhes bya ba smos te / / bying ba dang rgod pa rtogs nas zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gnyis zung du 'brel par 'jug pa'i phyir bsgrim mi dgos par 'jug go zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / btang snyoms zhes bya ba ni yul gzhan la mngon par 'du mi byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - sūpasthitasmṛtiravavāde līnaṃ cittam uddhtaṃ vā / yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti / / layauddhatyavigamāya ca tad abhisaṃskaroti layauddhatyavigamāc copekṣāṃ / karotīti /
# de ni 'di skad du gdams ngag la dran pa shin tu nye bar gnas pa ni bying ba dang rgod pa'i sems yang dag pa ji ltar ba bzhin du shes shing / / bying ba dang rgod pa dang 'bral ba'i phyir de mngon par 'du byed la /
evaṃ tasya cittapraśaṭhatā karmaṇyatā / / atra ca karmaṇyatāsthitir iti svārthe bhāvapratyayaḥ svapeṭatvādivat //
# bying ba dang rgod pa dang 'bral na yang btang snyoms su byed do zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / de ltar na de'i sems rnal du 'jug pa las su rung ba nyid yin no /
{ pañcendriyāṇi } / ṛddhipādānantaraṃ pañcendriyāṇi śraddhādīnyuktānīti sambadhyate /
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i 'og tu dbang po lnga rnams te / / dad pa la sogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni bstan zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti kenārthenetyabhiprāyaḥ / / ata āha -
# de dag ji ltar rnam par gzhag ce na zhes bya ba ni gang gi phyir zhes dgongs pa'o / / de'i phyir /
ropite mokṣabhāgīye chandayogādhipatyataḥ /
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun bskyed na / / 'dun dang sbyor ba dbang byed do /
iti vistaraḥ / / ādhipatyata iti vartata ityanena cchandayogādhipatyata / ityatrādhipatyaśabdaḥ prayukta uttaratrāpyanuvartata iti darśayati /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / dbang byed pa zhes bya bar snyegs so zhes bya ba 'dis ni 'dun pa dang sbyor ba dbang byed ces bya ba'i sgra 'dir smos pa 'og ma rnams la yang snyegs so zhes ston to /
ṛddhipādaiḥ karmaṇyacittasyāropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle iti / / karmaṇyacittasya vimokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ cittasandhāne pratiṣṭhāṃ / pratilabhate chandādhipatyato yāvat pravicayādhipatyataḥ na tv
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis sems las su rung ba thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed nas zhes bya ba ni sems las su rung ba sems kyi rgyud la thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rab tu 'jog pa 'thob ste / / 'dun pa ni dbang byed pa nas rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ni dbang byed pa'i bar du 'gyur gyi /
akarmaṇyacittasya /
# sems las su mi rung ba la ni ma yin no /
sā ca cittakarmaṇyatā ṛddhipādair bhavati /
# sems las su rung ba nyid de yang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis 'gyur ro /
tasmād ṛddhipādānantaraṃ vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ / pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇīti vyavasthāpyante /
# de bas na rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i 'og tu thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pas dad pa la sogs pa dbang po lnga rnams rnam par gzhag go /
chandādhipatyata iti kāraṇe kāryopacārāśchraddhaivātra
# 'dun pa ni dbang byed zhes bya ba ni rgyu la 'bras bu btags nas dad pa nyid la 'dir 'dun pa'i sgrar bshad de /
chandaśabdenoktā /tadyathā dadhatrapuṣaṃ sadyojvara iti /
# dper na zho dang ga gon la 'phral du rims zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
athavāstitvaguṇaśaktiṣu yathākramam abhisampratyayaprasādābhilāṣāḥ / śraddhāyā lakṣaṇaṃ /
# yang na yod pa nyid dang yon tan can dang nus pa rnams la go rims bzhin du mngon par yid ches pa dang dang ba dang 'dod pa rnams ni dad pa'i mtshan nyid do /
ataścandagrahaṇenātrābhilāṣalakṣaṇā śraddhaiva gṛhyate na tu cchanda iti
# de bas na 'dun pa smos pas 'dir 'dod pa'i mtshan nyid dad pa smos par 'gyur gyi 'dun pa ni ma yin no /
prayogādhipatyata iti prayujyate 'neneti prayogaḥ /
# sbyor ba ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni 'dis sbyor bar byed pas na sbyor ba ste /
prayogaśabdena vīryam abhipretaṃ / / ālambanāsampramoṣādhipatyata iti smṛtīndriyādhipatyataḥ / / ālmbanābhilapanalakṣaṇaṃ smṛtīndriyaṃ /
# sbyor ba'i sgra ni brtson 'grus la bya bar dgongs pa'o / / dmigs pa mi brjed pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni dran pa'i dbang po dbang byed pa ste / / dmigs pa gsal ba'i mtshan nyid ni dran pa'i dbang po'o /
avisārādhipatyata iti samādhīndriyādhipatyataḥ /
# mi 'phro ba ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po dbang byed pa ste /
avisāro hi samādhīndriyaṃ cittaikāgratālakṣaṇatvāt / / pravicayādhipatyataśceti prajñendriyādhipatyataḥ / / prajñendriyasya dharmapravicayātmakatvāt /
# sems rtse gcig pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas mi 'phro ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang po'o / / rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni shes rab kyi dbang po dbang byed pa ste / / shes rab kyi dbang po chos rnam par 'byed pa'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
ca śabdo vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipattyāt / [p.133] / yathākramaṃ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇi veditavyānīti darśayati /
# kyang zhes bya ba'i sgra ni thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pas dad pa la sogs pa dbang po dag dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o zhes bya bar ston to /
śraddhadhāno hi saṃsāracārakān niḥsaraṇārthaṃ vīryam ārabhate /
# dad par gyur pa ni 'khor ba'i btson ra nas 'byung bar 'gyur bas de'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo /
ārabdhavīryasya triśikṣāniṣpattiḥ smṛtisamādhiprajñendriyāṇi / yathākramaṃ /
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa bslab pa gsum sgrub ste / / dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po rnams go rims bzhin no /
evaṃ darśanamārgaprayogabhūmāv indriyāṇāṃ prādhānyam iṣyate /
# de ltar mthong ba'i lam la sbyor ba'i sa la dbang po di rnams gtso bor 'dod do /
anye tvāhuḥ - na mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ / śraddhādīnām indriyatvaṃ /
# gzhan dag na re thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa la dbang byed pa la dad pa la sogs pa'i dbang po zhes mi bya'o /
kiṃ tarhi ropite mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūle chandādīnām ādhipatyata / etānīndriyāṇy ucyante / / etad eva pradarśayann āha - chandādhipatyataḥ śraddhāyā indriyatvam iti
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed nas 'dun pa la sogs pa la dbang byed pas na 'di dag dbang po zhes bya'o / / de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'dun pa ni dbang byed pa zhes bya ba smos te /
sambadhyate / / prayogo vyāpāraḥ /
# dad pa'i dbang po zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / sbyor ba ni byed pa'o /
asammoṣa ālambanavipraṇāśaḥ /
# mi brjed pa ni dmigs pa chud mi za ba'o /
avisaraṇam avisāraḥ /
# 'phro ba med pas na mi 'phro ba'o /
pravicayanaṃ pravicayaḥ /
# rab tu rnam par 'byed pas na rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'o /
teṣāṃ prayogasammoṣāvisārapravicayānām ādhipatyād / vīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñākhyaścaittā indriyākhyaṃ bhavantīti /
# sbyor ba dang mi brjed pa dang mi 'phro ba dang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa de dag la brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab ces bya ba'i sems las byung ba rnams dbang bas na / / dbang po rnams zhes bya bar gyur zhes zer ro /
atra tvetad vaktavyaṃ - ropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle ropitāvasthātaś / candādyādhipatyasya śraddhādīnāñca kaścid viśiṣṭasvabhāvo nāsti
# 'dir ni ji skad du bshad par bya ste / / thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa dang ma bskyed pa gnyis kyi dus na 'dun pa la sogs pa dbang byed pa dang dad pa la sogs pa rang bzhin du bye brag tu gyur pa gang yang med de /
yasmāt tadavasthāyāṃ tad ādhipatyāt teṣām indriyatvam avasthāpyata / iti // / { pañca balāni } / tānyeva śraddhādīni balavanti balānyucyante indriyānantaram uktānīti
# 'di ltar de'i dus na dbang byed pas de dag dbang por rnam par gzhag go / / dad pa la sogs pa de dag nyid stobs dang ldan par gyur pa la stobs rnams zhes bya ste / / dbang po'i 'og tu bshad pa'i phyir ro / / de dag stobs ldan ji lta bu zhe na /
teṣāṃ punar balavattvaṃ kuta ityata āha - / vipakṣasya {hi} saṃlikhāt iti /
