tadabhāva ānuttaryaṃ / / tat punaḥ pratipattyālambanasamudāgamāḥ /
# de las theg pa khyad par can gzhan med pa'i phyir ro / / de yang sgrub pa dang dmigs pa dang yang dag par 'grub pa ste /
tathāhi tadyogān mahāyānam anuttaram ucyate / / pratipattirevānuttaryaṃ pratipattyānuttaryaṃ / / evam ālambanānuttaryaṃ samudāgamānuttaryañca veditavyaṃ /
# 'di ltar de dag dang ldan pas na theg pa chen po bla na med pa zhes bya'o / / sgrub pa nyid bla na med pa yin pas sgrub pa bla na med pa nyid de / / de bzhin du dmigs pa dang yang dag par 'grub pa bla na med pa nyid kyang rig par bya'o /
etad ānuttaryaṃ yathākramaṃ bodhisattvamārgaṃ tad adhiṣṭhānaṃ tat
# bla na med pa nyid de dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i lam dang de'i gnas dang de'i 'bras bu'i dbang du byas te /
phalañcādhikṛtya vyavasthāpyate /
# go rims bzhin du rnam par gzhag go /
etāvac ca buddhavacanenocyate - yaduta pratipattir ālambanaṃ tat / phalañceti //
# 'di lta ste / / sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab kyis kyang sgrub pa dang dmigs pa dang de'i 'bras bu dang 'di rnams tsam zhig bshad par zad do /
{ pratipattyānuttaryaṃ } / ālambanapūrvikā pratipattir ityālambanapūrvanirdeśanayena pratipattiḥ / pūrvam uktā bodhisattvānāṃ pratipattisāratāsandarśanārthaṃ /
# dmigs pa ni sgrub pa'i sngon du 'gro bas dmigs pa sngar bshad pa'i rigs pa las / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams la sgrub pa snying por bya ba bstan pa'i phyir sgrub pa sngar bshad do /
tatra kathaṃ pratipattyānuttaryam ityata āha - pratipattyānuttaryaṃ
# de la ji ltar na sgrub pa bla na med pa nyid ces bya zhe na / / de'i phyir /
daśapāramitāpratipattito veditavyam iti / / pāramitāpratipattiḥ [p.151] / pāramitānuṣṭhānaṃ / / sā ca pāramitāpratipattir mahāyāna eva nirdiṣṭā nānyatra yāna iti / mahāyānam evānuttaram iti darśayati /
# sgrub pa bla na med pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa bcu la sgrub par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba smos so / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams sgrub pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la nan tan byed pa'o / / pha rol tu phyin pa sgrub pa de yang theg pa chen po nyid du bshad kyi; gzhan ni ma yin pas na theg pa chen po nyid bla na med par ston to /
sā ca pratipattir yiaḥ prakāraiḥ pāramitāsu prayujyamānasyānuttarā / bhavati tān prakārān darśayann āha -
# sgrub pa de yang rnam pa gang gis pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sbyor ba ni bla na med par 'gyur ba'i rnam pa de dag bstan pa'i phyir /
pratipattis tu ṣaḍvidhā
# sgrub pa dag ni rnam drug ste /
iti // / { paramā pratipattiḥ } / sā ca pāramitāpratipattir na vijñāyate kathaṃ paramā yāvat katham / aviśiṣṭetyata āha - tatra paramā dvādaśātmikā // iti /
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sgrub pa ji ltar na dam par 'gyur ba nas / / ji ltar na khyad par can med pa'i bar du 'gyur ba mi shes nas / / de'i phyir de la / / dam pa bcu gnyis bdag nyid de /
dvādaśaprakārā paramā mahatī niruttaretyarthaḥ / / tat prakārapradarśanārtham āha -
# zhes bya ba smos so / / dam pa ni rnam pa bcu gnyis te / / che ba dang bla na med ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de'i rnam pa bstan pa'i phyir /
audāryam āyatattvañca [p.152]
# rgya che ba dang yun ring dang /
iti vistaraḥ / / audāryaparamatā yāvan niṣpattiparamatetyeṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / rgya che ba dam pa nas 'grub pa dam pa zhes bya ba'i bar du rnam pa bcu gnyis pa de dag ni dam pa'o /
tatraudāryaparamatā sarvalaukika sampattyanarthakatvenotkṛṣṭatayā ca / veditavyā /
# de la rgya cher dam pa ni 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad mi 'dod pa dang mchog tu rig par bya'o zhes bya ba la /
sampattir abhyudayaḥ sa ca dvidhākāraḥ - prāptaścāprāptaś ca / / tatra prāpte na sajjate aprāptaṃ na prārthayati
# phun sum tshogs pa zhes bya ba ni mngon par mtho ba'o / / de yang rnam pa gnyis te / / rnyed pa dang ma rnyed pa'o /
svasukhanirapekṣaparaduḥkhāpanayaprayuktatvāt / / yathoktaṃ - / puṇyaṃ hi yat puṇyaphalañca sādhoḥ
# de la bdag gi bde ba la mi chags pa dang gzhan gyi sdug bsngal ba bsal bar zhugs pa'i phyir rnyed pa la mi chags shing ma rnyed pa mi 'tshol ba'o / / ji skad du / / dge ba khyod kyi bsod nams 'bras bu gang /
sarva parārthaṃ tava nātmahetoḥ // iti / / prahāṇajñānaprabhāvasampannabuddhatvapalatvāad utkṛṣṭatvaṃ /
# thams cad gzhan gyi don te bdag gi don rgyur min / / zhes 'byung ba lta bu'o / / spong ba dang ye shes dang mthu phun sum tshogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir mchog go /
athavā loke hi dvividhā evodāra ucyate - yaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ
# yang na 'jig rten na rgya che ba ni rnam pa gnyis su brjod de /
pratyupakārāprārthanaś ca / / tasmād bodhisattvaḥ sarvalokasampattyaprārthako'pyadhimātrā'dhimātrāsu / ca dānādipāramitāsu prayujyata iti tat pratipatter audāryam ucyate /
# che bar mngon pa dang lan du phan 'dogs pa mi 'dod pa'o / / de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' ni 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad mi 'dod kyang sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la je bas je cher sbyor te / / de bas na de sgrub pa rgya che ba nyid ces bya'o /
āyatattvaparamatā āyatatvenotkṛṣṭatā /
# yun ring ba dam pa ni yun ring ba'i phyir mchog ste /
āyatattvaṃ punar dānapāramitādiṣv āyatābhyāsaḥ /
# yun ring ba nyid kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa la yun ring por goms par byed pa'o /
tac ca na jñāyate kiyañciram ityata āha -
# de yang dus ji srid pa mi shes nas de'i phyir /
vikalpāsaṃkhyeyaparibhāvanād iti / / bodhisattvānāṃ hi dānapāramitādibhāvanā / kalpāsaṃkhyeyatrayaparyavasānatvād atyantamāyatā /
# bskal ba grangs med pa gsum du yongs su bsgom pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa bsgom pa bskal ba grangs med pa gsum gyi mthar thug par byed pas shin tu yun ring ba yin no /
adhikāraparamatā sarvasattvārthakriyādhikārād iti / / bodhisattvānāṃ svasukhanirapekṣāṇāṃ dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ
# ched du bya ba dam pa ni sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba'i ched kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba la / / byang chub sems dpa' bdag gi bde ba la mi chags pa rnams ni /
sarvasattvānāṃ hitasukhakriyām adhikṛtyetyato'dhikārataḥ parametyucyate / akṣayatvaparamatā akṣayatvena paramatā /
# sems can la phan pa dang bde bar bya ba'i ched du sbyin pa la zhugs pas de'i phyir ched du bya ba dam pa zhes bya'o / / zad mi shes pa dam pa ni mi zad pa'i phyir dam pa ste / / zad mi shes pa gang zhe na / / de'i phyir /
akṣayatvaṃ punaḥ kuta ityata āha - mahābodhipariṇāmanayā'tyantam
# byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pas / / gtan du yongs su gtugs par mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
apryādānād iti / / mahābodhipariṇāmitā hi dānādayaḥ sarvopapattyāyataneṣu vipākaphalaṃ
# byang chub chen por yongs su bsngo ba'i sbyin pa la sogs pa ni / / skye pa'i gnas thams cad du rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu byin yang gtan du rgyun chad par mi 'gyur te /
dattvāpi nātyantaṃ samucchidyante āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya / dharmakāyasya niṣpādanāt tasya cākṣayatvan nirupādhiśeṣe'pi nirvāṇe na
# gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid chos kyi sku sgrub pa dang de yang mi zad pas phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das par gtan du yongs su gtugs par mi 'gyur gyi /
paryādīyante śrāvakādibodhipariṇāmanayā tu nirupadhiśeṣe / nirvāṇadhātau sarvathā''śrayasya samucchedāt samucchidyante /
# nyan thos la sogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngos pa ni phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su lus rnam pa thams cad du rgyun chad pas rgyun chad par 'gyur ro /
mahābodhipariṇāmanayā vā dānādīnyakṣayāṇi bhavanti / prabhūtavipākatvāt /
# yang na byang chub chen por yongs su bsngo bas sbyin pa la sogs pa mi zad par 'gyur te; rnam par smin pa mang ba'i phyir ro /
prabhūtam apyakṣayam ucyate vipākadānenā'tyantam aparyādānāt na / tvevaṃ śrāvakādipariṇāmanāyām akṣayatvaṃ / [p.153]
# mang ba la yang mi zad pa zhes bya ste / / rnam par smin pa sbyin pas gtan du yongs su gtugs par mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / nyan thos la sogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngos pa la ni de ltar mi zad par mi 'gyur ro /
athavā satvārthaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmitāni kuśalamūlāni bodhisattvānāṃ / sattvadhātuvad akṣayāṇi bhavantītyataś ca sattvadhātuvan nātyantaṃ / paryādīyanta iti /
# yang na sems can rnams kyi don du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa dang sems can gyi khams bzhin du mi zad pa yin te / / de bas na sems can gyi khams bzhin du gtan du yongs su gtugs par mi 'gyur ro /
nairantarya paramatā ātmaparasamatādhimokṣāt sarvasattvadānādibhiḥ / pāramitā paripūraṇād iti /
# rgyun mi 'chad pa dam pa ni bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid du mos pa'i phyir te / / sems can thams cad la sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni /
pramuditāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthāvabodhād / bodhisattva ātmaparasamatām abhimucyate /
# sa rab tu dga' ba la byang chub sems dpas chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro ba'i don rtogs pas bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid du mos so /
sa svaparasamatādhimokṣāt prahīṇasvaparavikalpaḥ svadānādibhir iva / paradānādibhir api sumuditacittaṃ labhate / / tataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pratimuhūrtaṃ pratidivasaṃ ca nirantaraṃ
# de bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid du mos pa'i phyir bdag dang gzhan du rnam par rtog pa spangs pas / / rang gi sbyin pa la sogs pa bzhin du gzhan gyi sbyin pa la sogs pas kyang sems shin tu dga' ba thob po /
dānādipāramitāḥ paripūryanta iti / / akṛcchratvaparamatā anumodanāmātreṇa paradānādīnāṃ / pāramitāparipūraṇād iti /
# de bas na skad cig re re'am yud tsam re re'am nyi ma re rer yang rgyun mi 'chad par de'i sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro /
tathā bodhisattvāḥ sattvānāṃ dānādikuśalamūlāni samuditena / manasā'numodayanti yathaiṣām anumodanāmātreṇa dānādipāramitāḥ / paripūryanta iti / / vittatvaparamatā gaganagañjasamādhyādibhir dānādiparipūraṇād iti / / bodhisattvā dharmadhātuprativedhabhāvanayā gaganagañjasaṃjñakaṃ / samādhiṃ pratilabhante /
# tshogs med pa dam pa ni gzhan gyi sbyin pa la sogs pa la rjes su yi rang ba tsam gyis pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni ci nas kyang de dag la rjes su yi rang ba tsam gyis sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can rnams kyi sbyin pa la sogs pa dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la rab tu dga' ba'i yid kyis rjes su yi rang bar byed do / / dbang 'byor ba dam pa ni nam mkha' mdzod kyi ting nge 'dzin la sogs pas sbyin pa la sogs pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams chos kyi dbyings rtogs pa bsgom pas; ting nge 'dzin nam mkha' mdzod ces bya ba 'thob ste /
tasya pratilambhātsattvānāṃ sarvābhiprāyaparipūraṇād dānapāramitāṃ
# de thob pas sems can rnams kyi bsam pa thams cad yongs su bskang ba'i phyir sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te /
paripūrayanti / / tadādhipatyena hi gaganam eva gañjo bhavatīti samādhir gaganagañja
# de'i dbang gis nam mkha' nyid mdzod dam yang na nam mkha' la mdzod 'cha' ba'i ting nge 'dzin la nam mkha' mdzod ces bya bar brjod de /
ityabhidhīyate yasmāt tad ṛddhyā sarvopakaraṇāni gaganāj jāyante /
# 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus yo byad thams cad nam mkha' las 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
ādiśabdena prajñāpāramitādisūtrapaṭhitānāṃ grahaṇaṃ /
# sogs pa'i sgras ni shes rab kyi rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa mdo las 'byung ba'i ting nge 'dzin rnams bsdu'o /
parigrahaṇaparamatā nirvikalpajñānaparigṛhītatvād iti /
# yongs su bzung ba dam pa ni / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis yongs su bzung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni /
bodhisattvānāṃ hi dāpakadeyapratigrāhakatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ / jñānaṃ /
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes ni sbyin bdag dang sbyin par bya ba dang len pa gsum ni dmigs pas rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes so /
evaṃ yāvaj jñātṛjñeyajñānatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ / / tena parameṇa nirvikalpena jñānena parigṛhītā dānādipratipattiḥ kathaṃ
# de bzhin du shes par byed pa dang shes par bya ba dang shes pa gsum gyis bar du mi dmigs pa'i phyir rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes te / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes dam pa des yongs su gzung ba'i sbyin pa la sogs pa sgrub po /
tad anuparivartitatvāt tad ālambanatvāc cetyataḥ parametyucyate / / ārambhaparamatā adhimukticaryābhūmāvadhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāv iti / / prathamakalpāsaṃkhye yānām adhimukticaryābhūmir ity ucyate / / gotramitrabalena cotpāditabodhicittasya svabhāvatrayamukhenātyarthaṃ
# ji lta zhe na de'i rjes su 'brang ba dang de la dmigs pa'i phyir te / / de'i phyir dam pa zhes bya'o / / rtsol ba dam pa ni mos pas spyod pa'i sa la bzod pa cher gyur pa'o zhes bya ba la / / bskal ba grangs med pa dang po ni mos pas spyod pa'i sa zhes bya ste / / rigs dang bshes gnyen gyi stobs kyis byang chub tu sems bskyed nas /
sarvadharmanairātmyādhimokṣo'dhimātrā kṣāntirāśraddhyādivipakṣair
# ngo bo nyid gsum gyi sgo nas chos thams cad la bdag med par shin tu mos pa'i bzod pa che ba ste /
aparājaya iti / / sā hi bodhisattvasyārambhāvasthā /
# ma dad pa la sogs pa mi mthu pa'i phyogs las rgyal ba la bya'o / / de ni byang chub sems dpa'i rtsom pa'i dus te /
tato'dhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāvārambhaparamatety ucyate /
# de'i phyir bzod pa chen po ni rtsom pa dam pa zhes bya ste /
pratilambhaparamatā prathamāyāṃ bhūmāv iti / / prathamāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvāvabodhāl lokottarāḥ / pāramitāḥ pratilabhate pūrvantu prathamabhūmiprayogasaṅgṛhītā
# 'thob pa dam pa ni sa dang po'o zhes bya ba ni sa dang po la chos kyi dbyings kun du 'gro ba rtogs pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams 'thob po / / sngar sa dang po la sbyor bas bsdus pa ni 'jig rten pa nyid de /
laukikā evetyataḥ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau pratilambhaparamatety ucyate / / niṣyandaparamatā tadanyāsvaṣṭāsv iti /
# de'i phyir sa dang po la 'thob pa dam pa zhes bya'o rgyu mthun pa dam pa ni de ma yin pa gzhan brgyad po dag la'o zhes bya ba ni /
prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ tad anyāsv aṣṭāsu bhūmiṣu / uttarottaraviśiṣṭapratilambho niṣyanda iti niṣyandaparamatā / / athavā'dhimukticaryābhūmau pāramitābhāvanābalena / prathamabhūmipratilambhaḥ pratilambhaparamatā /
# de ma yin pa gzhan sa brgyad po dag la gong nas gong du khyad par thob pa ni sa dang po la thob pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi rgyu mthun pa yin pas rgyu mthun pa dam pa'o / / yang na mos pas spyod pa'i sa la pha rol tu phyin pa rnams bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis sa dang po 'thob pa ni 'thob pa dam pa ste /
prathamā hi bhūmir bodhisattvānāṃ darśanamārgasaṅgṛhītā tat
# sa dang po byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mthong ba'i lam du bsdus pa der zhugs na /
praveśāc ca jātau [p.154] / tathāgatasyotpannaḥ tad anukūlatadātmakadharmapratilambhād iti
# de'i bdag nyid kyi chos rab tu thob pa'i phyir / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su skyes pa yin no zhes mdo las 'byung ngo /
sūtrapāṭhaḥ / / pāramitābhāvanābalena pratilabdhāyāḥ prathamāyā bhūmer avaśiṣṭā
# sa lhag ma rnams pha rol tu phyin pa rnams bsgom pa'i stobs kyis thob pa'i sa dang po'i rgyu mthun pa dam pa'o /
bhūmayo niṣyandatvān niṣyandaparamatā / / athavā prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ pāramitānām aṣṭau bhūmayo
# yang na sa brgyad po 'di dag ni sa dang po la rab tu thob pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi rgyun mthun par gyur pas rgyu mthun pa dam pa'o /
niṣyandabhūtatvān niṣyandapramatā /
# 'grub pa dam pa ni sa bcu pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la /
niṣpattiparamatā daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyāñca bodhisattvaniṣpattyā / buddhaniṣpattyā ca / / daśamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ sarvabodhisattvacaryāniryāta iti tatra / tathāgatair yauvarājye'bhiṣicyate /
# byang chub sems dpa' 'grub pa dang sangs rgyas 'grub pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la / / sa bcu pa la byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad tshar phyin nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi rgyal chab tu dbang bskur te /
acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraparipūrṇatvāt sarvadharmavikalpavigatatvāt / sarvathā svaparārthasampādakatvāc ca bodhisattvānāṃ viṣpattiparamatā
# bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su rdzogs pa dang chos thams cad la rnam par rtog pa dang bral ba dang rnam pa thams cad du bdag dang gzhan gyi don sgrub pa'i phyir / / sa bcu pa la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'grub pa dam pa'o /
tāthāgatyāñca bhūmau prahāṇajñānaprabhāvātiśayalābhād bhagavān / sarvasya jagataḥ śāstā bhavatītyato buddhapariniṣpattyā niṣpattiḥ /
# spong ba dang ye shes dang mthu khyad par can rnams thob pa'i phyir bcom ldan 'das ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi ston pa yin pas de'i phyir sangs rgyas su 'grub pas 'grub pa'o /
kā punar iyaṃ niṣpattiḥ ?
# 'grub pa de yang gang zhe na /
bodhisattvadharmāṇāṃ buddhadharmāṇāñca sarvaprakārābhinirhāraḥ /
# byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams dang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams rnam pa thams cad du mngon par sgrub pa'o /
athavā pāramitānāṃ śaikṣabhūmisaṅgṛhītānāṃ prakarṣo daśamī bhūmiḥ
# yang na slob pa'i sar bsdus pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi phul du byung ba ni sa bcu pa ste /
atas tasyāṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattiḥ /
# de bas na de la byang chub sems dpa' yongs su 'grub po /
aśaikṣabhumisaṅgṛhītānāṃ kāṣṭhā buddhabhūmiḥ /
# mi slob pa'i sar bsdus pa rnams kyi phul du byung ba ni sangs rgyas kyi sa ste /
tasyāṃ bhūmau pāramitānāṃ śaikṣābhāvād buddhapariniṣpattyā
# sa de na pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la slob pa med pa'i phyir / / sangs rgyas su yongs su 'grub pas 'grub pa ste /
pariniṣpattir ityevaṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattyā daśamyāṃ bhūmau / tāthāgatyañca buddhapariniṣpattiparamatā veditavyā /
# de ltar sa bcur byang chub sems dpa'i yongs su 'grub pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas yongs su grub pas 'grub pa dam par rig par bya'o / / de'i phyir dam pa'i don gyis na /
tataś ca paramārthena daśa pāramitā matāḥ / iti /
# pha rol tu phyin pa bcur 'dod do zhes bya ba ni 'di ltar dam pa rnam pa bcu gnyis po 'di dag /
yata eṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā bodhisattvānāṃ dānādiṣu saṃvidyate na / śrāvakādīnāṃ dānādiṣu tataḥ parametyanenārthena bodhisattvānām eva
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa la sogs pa la yod kyi / / nyan thos la sogs pa'i sbyin pa la sogs pa la ni med pa de'i phyir / / dam pa zhes bya ste /
dānādayo jñānaparyantā daśa pāramitā matā iti niruktinyāyeneti / / daśapāramitānāṃ yā pratipattiḥ sā punaḥ paramatety ucyate //5-4//
# don 'dis byang chub sems dpa' rnams nyid kyi sbyin pa la sogs pa ye shes la thug pa rnams nges pa'i tshig gi tshul gyis pha rol tu phyin pa bcu po dag tu ston to / / de bas na pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la sgrub pa gang yin pa de yang dam pa zhes bya'o /
[p.155] / ekeṣām iti yeṣāṃ pāramitānāṃ nāmamātram api na vyutpannaṃ teṣāṃ tan
# kha cig ces bya ba ni gang dag pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi ming tsam yang mi shes pa de rnams la de dag gi ming bstan par bya ba'i phyir /
nāmavyutpādanārtham ucyate -
# sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod brtson 'grus /
dānaṃ śīlaṃ kṣaṃā vīryaṃ dhyānaṃ prajñā upāyatā /
# bsam gtan dang ni shes rab thabs / / smon lam stobs dang ye shes dang /
praṇidānaṃ balaṃ jñānam etāḥ pāramitā daśa // iti /
# 'di dag pha rol phyin bcu'o / / zhes bya ba brjod de /
adhikāraparamatā sarvatattvārthakriyoddeśādityuktam ato'yaṃ praśnaḥ -
# ched du bya ba dam pa ni sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba'i ched kyi phyir ro zhes bshad pa de'i phyir /
kimāsāṃ pratyekaṃ karmeti / / ata āha -
# 'di dag gi so so'i las ci zhe na zhes dris pa de'i phyir /
anugraho'vidhātaś ca karma tasya ca marṣaṇaṃ /
# las ni rjes su 'dzin byed dang / / gnod mi byed dang de la bzod /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
dānena hi bodhisattvaḥ sattvānanugṛhṇātīti / / tatra pūjānugrahakāṅkṣayā bāhyātmikavastuni avadyatvāt
# byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pas ni sems can rnams rjes su 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba ni de la mchod pa dang phan gdags par 'dod pas /
pratyupakāravipākādinirapekṣo yayā cetanayā parityajati / kāya-vāk-karmāṇi ca pratipādayatīdaṃ bodhisattvasyāmiṣadānaṃ / / anena kṣutpipāsādiduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānānugṛhṇāti /
# phyi dang nang gi dngos po kha na ma tho ba med pas lan du phan 'dogs pa dang rnam par smin pa la sogs pa la mi lta bar sems pa gang gis yongs su gtong zhing lus dang ngag gi las kyis kyang sgrub pa 'di ni / / byang chub sems dpa'i zang zing gi sbyin pa ste / / 'dis bkres pa dang skom pa la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal sel bas sems can rnams rjes su 'dzin to /
sattvānupaghātakānām ājīvaśāstrakalānipuṇānāṃ karuṇāpūrvakam / upadeśaḥ sugatimokṣamārgopadeśaś ca dharmadānaṃ / / anenā'pyajīvikādurgatisaṃsāraduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇāti /
# snying rje sngon du btang ste sems can rnams la mi gnod pa'i 'tsho ba dang bstan bcos dang sgyu rtsal dang bzo rnams ston pa dang bde 'gro dang thar pa'i lam ston pa ni chos kyi sbyin pa ste / / 'dis kyang 'tsho ba med pa dang ngan 'gro 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal sel bas sems can rjes su 'dzin to /
rājacauradāyādavyālādibhir āghrātānāṃ tebhyo vimokṣaṇam / abhayadānaṃ / / anenāpi jīvabhogaputradārādivipadbhayāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇātīti / śīlenopaghātam eṣāṃ na karoti /
# rgyal po dang chom rkun dang bgo skal la spyod pa dang gcan gzan la sogs pas zin pa de dag las thar par byed pa ni mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa ste / / 'dis kyang srog dang longs spyod dang bu dang chung ma la sogs pas phongs pa'i 'jigs pa sel bas sems can rnams rjes su 'dzin to; /
sarvakāyavāgduścaritaviratir lokānuvṛttyā ca pratiṣiddhād vihitasya ca / kāya-vāk-karmaṇo viratir anuṣṭhānañca śīlaṃ /
# tshul khrims kyis ni de dag la gnod par mi byed do zhes bya ba ni lus dang ngag gis nyes par spyod pa thams cad spyod pa dang 'jig rten dang mthun pa'i bkag pa dang bsgo bas lus dang ngag gi las ldog cing sgrub pa ni tshul khrims te /
asmin śīle vyavasthānāt sattveṣvapakāraṃ duṣṭopasaṃhāraṃ jīvitahetor / api svayaṃ na karoti nāpi kārayatīti /
# tshul khrims de la rnam par gnas pas sems can la gnod pa dang mi bde bar sgrub pa srog gi phyir yang bdag nyid kyang mi byed cing gzhan la yang byed du mi 'jug pa'o /
kṣāntyā paraiḥ kṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayatīti / / karuṇāpuraḥsareṇa cetasā sarvākāra-duḥkhamarṣaṇādhivāsanātmikā / kṣāntiḥ /
# bzod pa ni gzhan dag gis gnod par byas pa la ji mi snyam par byed do zhes bya ba ni snying rje'i sems sngon du btang bas sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa thams cad la ji mi snyam par byed cing dang du len pa'i bdag nyid kyi bzod pa ste /
tenānvair hiṃsābandhanatāḍanādikṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayati / pratyapakārāsamīhanāt /
# des gzhan dag gis gsod pa dang 'ching ba dang rdeg pa la sogs pa byas pa la slar gnod pa mi byed pas ji mi snyam par byed pa'o /
vīryeṇa guṇān vardhayati / / dānādīnadhikṛtyotsāho vīryaṃ / / tena dānādiguṇābhyāsād viśiṣṭaguṇaniṣpattir vṛddhiḥ /
# brtson 'grus kyis ni yon tan rnams 'phel bar byed do zhes bya ba ni sbyin pa la sogs pa'i phyir spro ba ni brtson 'grus te / / des sbyin pa la sogs pa'i yon tan goms par byas pas yon tan khyad par du 'phags par 'grub pa ni 'phel ba'o /
dhyānena ṛddhyādibhir āvarjyāvatārayatīti / / ādiśabdena cittaparyāyajñānaṃ [p.156]
# bsam gtan gyis ni rdzu 'phrul la sogs pas mgu bar byas te 'dzud do zhes bya ba la sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni /
parigṛhyate / / dhyānaṃ samādhiścittasyaikāgratā /
# sems kyi rnam grangs shes pa bsdu'o / / bsam gtan ni ting nge 'dzin la sems rtse gcig pa'o /
ṛddhirākāśagamanādikā / / avatāraṇaṃ śāsanadharmatāpratipādanaṃ /
# rdzu 'phrul ni nam mkha' la 'gro ba la sogs pa'o / / 'dzud pa ni bstan pa'i chos nyid ston pa ste /
dhyānaphalābhyāṃ hi ṛdhyādeśanāprātihāryābhyām āvarjitaḥ śakyante / śāsana avatartuṃ /
# bsam gtan gyi 'bras bu rdzu 'phrul dang kun brjod pa'i cho 'phrul gnyis kyis mgu bar byas na bstan pa la 'dzud nus par 'gyur ro /
prajñayā samyag avavādadānād vimocanād vimocayati /
# shes rab kyis ni yang dag pa'i gdams ngag byin pas rnam par grol bar byed do zhes bya ba la /
sarvākāradharmapravicayalakṣaṇā prajñā / / tasyāś ca karma samyag avavādadānaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ
# shes rab ni rnam pa thams cad du chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'i mtshan nyid do / / de'i las ni yang dag pa'i gdams ngag sbyin pa ste /
cāviparītānuśāsanapratibaddhamataḥ prajñayā samyag avavādadānād / vimocayati / / upāyakauśalyapāramitayā mahābodhipariṇāmanād dānādīnakṣayān karoti / yasya dharmasya niṣpattaye vivṛddhaye prāptaye prahāṇāya vā yā yuktiḥ
# nyon mongs pa spong ba yang phyin ci ma log par rjes su bstan pa la rag lus pa'o / / de bas na shes rab kyis yang dag pa'i gdams ngag byin pas rnam par grol bar byed do / / thabs la mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pas ni / / byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pas / / sbyin pa la sogs pa mi zad par byed do zhes bya ba ni chos gang 'grub par bya ba dang rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang 'thob par bya ba dang spang bar bya ba'i phyir rigs pa gang yin pa de ni thabs yin no; /
sa tatropāyas tatra kauśalyaṃ vaicakṣaṇyam upāyakauśalyaṃ /
# de la mkhas pa ni thog tu phebs pa ste / / thabs la mkhas pa'o /
tasya kṛutopacitānāṃ dānādīnāṃ mahabodhipariṇāmanayā'kṣayakāraṇāṃ/
# de'i las ni sbyin pa la sogs pa byas shing bsags pa rnams byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pas mi zad par byed pa'o /
mahābodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalamūlāni mahābodhivad akṣayāni bhavantīti
# byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams ni byang chub chen po bzhin du mi zad par 'gyur ro /
praṇidhānapāramitayā'nukūlopapattiparigrahāt sarvajanmasu / buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartate / / praṇidhānam anekavidhaṃ prārthanātmakatvāt / / kuśalānukūlopapattiprārthanam atra praṇidhānam abhipretaṃ tasya janmani
# smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pas ni mthun pa'i skye ba yongs su 'dzin pas tshe rabs thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung ba mnyes par byed cing sbyin pa la sogs pa la rtag tu 'jug go zhes bya ba la / / smon lam ni rnam pa du mar smon pa'i bdag nyid yin mod kyi / / 'dir ni dge ba dang mthun pa'i skye ba la smon pas smon lam du 'dod do /
janmani buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartanaṃ karma /
# de'i las ni tshe rabs tshe rabs su sangs rgyas 'byung ba mnyam par byed pa dang sbyin pa la sogs pa la rtag tu 'jug pa'o /
balapāramitayā pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ niyataṃ dānādiṣu / pravartate vipakṣānabhibhavād iti /
# stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pas ni so sor rtog pa dang bsgom pa'i stobs gnyis kyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis zil gyis mi non pa'i phyir sbyin pa la sogs pa la nges par 'jug go zhes bya ba la so sor rtog pa ni shes rab po /
pratisaṃkhyānaṃ prajñā / / bhāvanā tu kuśaladharmābhyāsaḥ / / tad dvayaṃ vipakṣeṇānabhibhūtaṃ balapāramitety ucyate /
# bsgom pa ni dge ba'i chos goms par byed pa ste / / de gnyis la mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis zil gyis mi non pa ni / / stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o /
tasyāḥ kṣaṇanaiyamyena dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ karma /
# de'i las ni skad cig re re la yang gdon mi za bar sbyin pa la sogs pa la 'jug pa'o /
niyataśabdasya satataparyāyatvāt /
# nges pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni rgyun mi 'chad pa'i rnam grangs so /
na hi pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalād dānādikuśalaṃ vipakṣeṇābhibhūyate / / jñānapāramitayā yathārutadharmasammohāpagamād
# so sor rtog pa dang bsgom pa'i stobs dang ldan pa'i sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba la mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnams kyis zil gyis mi non to / / ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pas ni /
dānādyādhipateyadharmasambhogañca pratyanubhavati sattvāṃśca / paripācayatīti / / sarvasmin mahāyānadeśanādharme yathārutasammohavigatajñānaṃ
# chos la sgra ji bzhin du rmongs pa dang bral bas / / sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad pa'i chos la longs spyod pa myong ba dang sems can rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed do zhes bya ba ni theg pa chen po'i chos bstan pa thams cad la sgra ji bzhin du rmongs pa dang bral pa'i ye shes ni /
jñānapāramitā / / ayaṃ punar yathārutasammohaḥ kaḥ ?
# ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o / / sgra ji bzhin du rmongs pa de yang gang zhe na /
yenābhiprāyikam arthaṃ tyaktvā yathārutam eva kalpayatyayaṃ
# gang gis dgongs pa'i don spangs te sgra ji bzhin nyid du rtog pa 'di ni sgra ji bzhin du rmongs pa'o /
yathārutasammohaḥ / / dānam adhikṛtya dānam ālambya yaḥ sūtrādiko dharmo deśitaḥ sa
# sbyin pa'i dbang du mdzad pa ni sbyin pa la dmigs nas / / mdo la sogs pa'i chos bstan pa gang yin pa de sbyin pa'i dbang du mdzad pa'o /
dānādhipateyaḥ / / evaṃ śīlakṣāntivīryādyādhipateyo draṣṭavyaḥ /
# tshul khrims dang bzod pa dang brtson 'grus la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad pa de yang de bzhin du blta bar bya'o /
mahāyānam ārabhya / buddhabodhisattvenāviparītasāṃkathyaviniścayakāraṇāt sattvānāṃ / cāviparītayā dharmadeśanayā paripācanād dharmsambhogānubhavanaṃ / sattvaparipācanañca jñānapāramitāyāḥ karma /
# sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi theg pa chen po las brtsams te / / phyin ci ma log pa 'brel pa'i gtam nges par mdzad pa dang sems can rnams la phyin ci ma log pa'i chos bstan pas / / yongs su smin par mdzad pas chos la longs spyod pa myong ba dang sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa ni / / ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i las te /
sūtrādidharmopadeśasya jñānapāramitāprabhāvitatvāt // / { manasikārapratipattiḥ } [p.157]
# mdo la sogs pa'i chos bstan pa ni / / ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
paramapratipattinirdeśānantaraṃ manasikārapratipattir vaktavyā tatḥ
# dam bsgrub pa bshad pa'i 'og tu yid la byed pa'i sgrub pa brjod dgos te / / de'i phyir /
pṛcchati - manasikārapratipattiḥ katametyata āha -
# yid la byed pa sgrub pa gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
yathāprajñaptito dharma mahāyānamanaskriyā /
# theg pa chen po ji lta bur / / chos rnams btags pa mdzad pa dag /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
dānādīnyadhikṛtyeti dānaśīlakṣāntivīryādīny uddiśya / / yathāprajñaptānāṃ sūtrādidharmāṇām iti /
# sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad nas zhes bya ba ni sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bzod pa dang brtson 'grus la sogs pa'i ched kyi phyir ro / / mdo la sogs pa ji ltar btags pa'i chos rnams zhes bya ba ni /
atra sūtrageyavyākaraṇādidharmā yena prakāreṇa [p.158]
# bcom ldan 'das kyis rnam pa gang gis sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad de /
dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhagavatā deśitās teṣāṃ tathaivārthato / vyañjanataścādhyāropāpavādarahitānāṃ manasikaraṇaṃ
# mdo dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa dang lung du bstan pa la sogs pa'i chos rnams gsungs pa de bzhin du de dag gi don dang tshig 'bru la sgro 'dogs pa dang skur ba 'debs pa med par yid la byed pa ni yid la byed pa sgrub pa ste /
manasikārapratipattir nānyatheti / mahāyāna iti na śrāvakayāne /
# gzhan du ma yin no / / theg pa chen po zhes bya ba ni nyan thos kyi theg pa ma yin te /
tatra hi svārthā eva dānādayo deśitā na svaparārthā yathā mahāyāne / tasmān mahāyāna eva dānādīnyadhikṛtya yathāprajñaptānāṃ
# nyan thos kyi theg pa bdag gi don nyid du sbyin pa la sogs pa bshad kyi / / ji ltar theg pa chen por bdag dang gzhan gyi don byed pa lta bu ni ma yin te / / de bas na theg pa chen po nyid sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad de /
sūtrādidharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvair manasikaraṇaṃ manasikāra pratipattiḥ /
# mdo la sogs pa'i chos ji ltar btags pa rnams / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams sgrub pa yid la byed pa ni yid la byed pa sgrub pa'o /
śrāvakayāne dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhāṣitānāṃ sūtrādīnāṃ
# nyan thos kyi theg par sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dbang du mdzad de /
manasikaraṇam mithyāmanasikārapratipattiḥ svārthamātrāśrayatvād iti / jñāpitam bhavati /
# gsungs pa'i mdo la sogs pa yid la byed pa ni log par sgrub pa ste / / rang gi don tsam la brten pa'i phyir ro zhes bstan pa yin no /
te ca prāyeṇa cittasamatām asaktim anunnatim anupalaṃbhañcādhikṛtya
# de dag kyang phal cher sems snyoms pa nyid dang mi chags pa dang ma khengs pa dang mi dmigs pa rnams kyi dbang du mdzad de gzhag pa'o /
prajñaptā iti / / tatreya cittasamatā yā guṇyaguṇināṃ samam upakāraprārthanā /
# de la gang yon tan can dang yon tan med pa rnams la mtshungs par phan 'dogs par 'dod pa 'di ni sems snyoms pa nyid do /
tatreyam asaktir yo bhavabhogaprārthanāvigatasya parārtham eva dānādiṣu / prayogaḥ /
# de la gang srid pa dang longs spyod la 'dod pa med par gzhan gyi don nyid du sbyin pa la sogs pa la sbyor ba 'di ni mi chags pa'o /
tatreyam anunnatir yad dānādibhir nātmānaṃ manyate na parān paribhavati
# de la gang sbyin pa la sogs pas bdag rlom sems su mi byed cing / / gzhan la mi brnyas pa 'di ni ma khengs pa'o /
tatrāyam anupalambho yā trimaṇḍalapariśuddhir / dānadāyakapratigrāhakānām anupalambhanyāyeneti /
# de la gang sbyin pa dang sbyin bdag dang len pa rnams mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa gang yin pa 'di ni mi dmigs pa'o /
abhīkṣṇam iti punaḥ punaḥ / / śrutacintābhāvanāmayyā prajñayeti tatrāptavacanaprāmāṇyajo niścayaḥ
# thos pa dang bsams pa dang bsgoms pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyis zhes bya ba de la yid ches pa'i gsung rab las skyes pa'i nges pa ni thos pa las byung ba'o /
śrutamayī / / yuktinidhyānajaścintāmayī /
# rigs pa dang nges par sems pa las skyes pa ni bsams pa las byung ba'i'o /
bhāvanājo bhāvanāmayīti /
# bsgoms pa las skyes pa ni bsgoms pa las byung ba'i'o /
sarvā hi pravṛttiḥ pralārtham ataḥ pṛcchati - sā triprākarayā
# rgyun du zhes bya ba 'di yang dang yang du'o / / 'jug pa thams cad ni 'bras bu'i phyir te /
prajñayā manasikriyā kaṃ guṇam āvahatīty ata āha - / dhātupuṣṭyai praveśāya cārthasiddhai bhavatyasau /
# de bas na shes rab rnam pa gsum gyis yid la byed pa de yon tan ci zhig byed ce na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir; khams brtas byed dang 'jug byed dang /
dhātur gotraṃ bījaṃ /
# de yi don rnams 'grub par 'gyur /
tasya puṣṭir vṛddhiḥ / / dhātupuṣṭyā cāyatyāṃ viśadamahaprajño bhavati /
# zhes gsungs so / / khams ni rigs dang sa bon no / / de'i brtas pa ni 'phel ba'o /
tasya śrutasyārthaṃ bhāvena praviśatīti /
# khams brtas pas ni tshe phyi ma shes rab che zhing gsal bar 'gyur ro /
tasya sūtrādikasya śrutadharmasyārthe yuktibalotpāditayā cintāmayyā
# thos pa de'i don la snying nas 'jug par byed do zhes bya ba ni mdo la sogs pa'i chos thos pa de'i don la rigs pa'i stobs skyed pas /
prajñayā'rthasadbhāvam āśayataḥ praviśatīti /
# bsams pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyis don yod pa phyin ci ma log pa la bsam pa thag pa nas 'jug pa'o /
bhāvanāmayyārthasiddhiṃ prāpnoti / / arthasiddhis tattvādhigamaḥ /
# bsgoms pa las byung ba ni don 'grub par 'gyur te zhes bya ba la / / don grub pa ni de kho na khong du chud pa'o / / ji lta zhe na /
katham ityata āha - bhūmipraveśapariśodhanād iti / / smṛtyupasthānādipariśuddhyā hi bhūmiṃ praviśatītyataḥ
# de'i phyir / / sa la 'jug pa yongs su sbyong ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa la sogs pa yongs su dag pas sa la 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
smṛtyupasthānādibhir eva bhūmiṃ praviśatīti nirdiṣṭaṃ /
# de'i phyir dran pa nye bar gzhag pa la sogs pa nyid kyis sa la 'jug par bstan to /
tataḥ smṛtyupasthānādīnāṃ bhūmipraveśabhūtānāṃ bhāvanāmayyā / prajñayā pariśodhanād arthasiddhiṃ prāpnotīti bhūmiṃ
# de bas na dran pa nye bar gzhag pa la sogs pas sa la 'jug par gyur pa rnams bsgoms pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyis yongs su sbyong bas don 'grub par 'gyur te /
praviśatītyarthaḥ /
# sa la 'jug go zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
sā punar iyaṃ manasikārapratipattiḥ saparivārā vijñeyā na kevalā /
# yid la byed pa sgrub pa 'di yang 'khor dang bcas par shes par bya ste / / 'ba' zhig ni ma yin no /
kastat parivāraḥ ?
# de'i 'khor gang zhe na /
āha - / saṃyuktā dharmacaritaiḥ sā jñeyā daśabhiḥ punaḥ / iti /
# de ni chos spyod rnam bcu dang / / yang dag ldan par shes par bya / / zhes gsungs so /
parigṛhītā veditavyeti parivāritetyarthaḥ /
# yongs su zin par rig par bya ba ste zhes bya ni kun nas bskor ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
dharmātmakāni dharmādhikārikāṇi [p.159]
# chos kyi bdag nyid du'am chos kyi ched du spyod pa dag ni chos spyod pa dag go /
vā caritāni dharmacaritāni / / tāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha - katamad daśadhā dharmacaritam iti /
# de dag kyang mi shes nas / / de'i phyir / / chos spyod rnam pa bcu gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
ata āha - / lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ
# yi ge 'dri mchod sbyin pa dang /
iti vistaraḥ / / tatra mahāyānasya svayaṃ pareṇa vā lekhanaṃ cirasthityarthaṃ
# zhes bya ba rgya cher gsungs so / / de la yi ger 'dri ba ni theg pa chen po yun ring du gnas par bya ba'am /
śravaṇāvācanārthaṃ vā /
# mnyan pa'am klag pa'i phyir bdag gam gzhan gyis so /
pūjanaṃ puṣpadhūpagandhādibhiḥ / / mahāyānasyeti prakṛtaṃ /
# mchod pa ni me tog dang bdug pa dang mar me dang spos la sogs pas theg pa chen po la mchod pa'o /
mahāyānapraviṣṭasya likhitapustakādīnāṃ parebhyaḥ satkṛtya dānaṃ /
# sbyin pa ni theg pa chen po la zhugs pa gzhan dag la yi ger bris pa'i glegs bam la sogs pa bsti stang du byas te sbyin pa'o /
pareṇa vācyamānasya satkṛtya śravaṇaṃ /
# gzhan klog pa la nyan pa ni bsti stang du byas te nyan pa'o /
mahatā gauraveṇa svayaṃ vācanaṃ /
# bdag nyid klog pa ni gus pa cher byas te klog pa'o /
udgrahaṇaṃ mahatā prasādenātmasātkaraṇaṃ /
# len pa ni dad pa chen pos bdag la bdog par byed pa'o /
mahatā yatnena yogyebhyo granthastyārthasya vā āviṣkaraṇaṃ prakāśanaṃ /
# tshig dang don 'chad pa ni 'bad pa chen pos 'os pa rnams la ston par byed pa'o /
svādhyāyanam uddhatasya punaḥ punar abhyasanaṃ /
# kha ton du byed pa ni blangs pa'i phyir zhing goms par byed pa'o /
cintanaṃ yuktidvāreṇa tadarthanirūpaṇaṃ /
# sems pa ni rigs pa'i don la de'i sgo nas spyod pa'o /
bhāvamam abhyasanaṃ samāhitayā prajñayā / / ca śabdaḥ samuccaryārthaḥ /
# bsgom pa ni mnyam par gzhag pa'i shes rab kyis goms par byed pa'o / / dang zhes bya ba ni bsdu ba'i don to /
tatra lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ śravaṇam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padaiḥ kāyakarma
# de la yi ger 'dri ba dang mchod pa dang sbyin pa dang nyan pa zhes bya ba'i tshig bzhi po 'di dag gis ni /
pradarśitaṃ / / vācanam udgrahaṇaṃ prakāśanā svādhyāyanam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padair / vākkarma pradarśitaṃ / / cintanā bhāvanā cetyābhyām api manaḥ karma pradarśitaṃ /
# lus kyi las rab tu bstan to / / klog pa dang len pa dang 'chad pa dang kha ton du byed pa zhes bya ba'i tshig bzhi po 'di dag gis ni ngag gi las rab tu ston to / / sems pa dang sgom pa zhes bya ba de dag gis ni yid kyi las rab tu ston to /
ameyapuṇyaskandhaṃ hi caritaṃ tad daśātmakaṃ /
# spyod pa de bcu'i bdag nyid ni / / bsod nams phung po dpag tu med /
yadet daśaprakāraṃ dharmacaritam uktaṃ tata ekaikasmād dharmacaritādyaḥ / puṇyaskandhodbhavo na sa punaḥ svayaṃ pareṇa vā pramātuṃ śakyate / atibahutvād iti /kasmāt punar dānaśīladhyānādidharmanirdeśe tulye
# gang chos la spyod pa rnam pa bcu gsungs pa de la chos spyod pa gcig las bsod nams kyi phung po skye ba gang yin pa de yang shin tu mang ba'i phyir / / bdag gam gzhan gyis tshod bzung bar mi nus so / / sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bsam gtan la sogs pa'i chos 'dra bar bstan pa las /
mahāyāna eva dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyate sūtreṣu na punaḥ
# ci'i phyir mdo dag las theg pa chen po nyid kyi chos spyod pa shin tu 'bras bu che bar bstan gyi /
śrāvakayāne ? / sūtreṣu dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyata iti sambadhyate /
# nyan thos kyi theg pa la ni ma yin zhe na zhes bya ba ni chos spyod pa 'bras bu che bar bstan zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
dvābhyāṃ kāraṇābhyām iti mahāyāne dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāpalaṃ
# rnam pa gnyis kyi phyir te zhes bya ba ni theg pa chen po'i chos spyod pa 'bras bu shin tu che bar bstan to zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
deśyata iti sambadhyate / / katam ābhyām ityata āha -
# rnam pa gnyis pa gang zhe na / / de'i phyir / / khyad par phyir dang mi zad phyir / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
viśeṣād akṣayatvāc ca iti / / etad api na jñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati - kathaṃ viśeṣāt kahtma akṣayatvād
# de nyid kyang mi shes nas de'i phyir khyad par gyi phyir ni ji lta bu / / mi zad pa'i phyir ni ji lta bu zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
ityata āha - / parānugrahato'śamāt / iti /
# gzhan la phan 'dogs ma zhi phyir / / zhes bya ba gsungs so /
mahāyāne hi bodhisattvānāṃ dānādipratipattiḥ / sarvasattvārthakaraṇaikaṃ deśyate /
# theg pa chen por ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis sbyin pa la sogs pa sgrub pas sems can thams cad kyi don bya bar ro gcig par bstan gyi /
śrāvakayāne tvātmārthapradhānetyataḥ śrāvakāyānān mahāyānaṃ / parānugrahapravṛttatvād viśiṣyate / / evaṃ tāvad hetusamākhyānataḥ śrāvakayānān mahāyānasya viśiṣṭatvaṃ / / acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraphalasya trikāyasaṃgṛhītasya yāval lokas
# nyan thos kyi theg pa las ni bdag gi don gtso bor bshad do / / de bas na nyan thos kyi theg pa las theg pa chen po gzhan la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir khyad par du 'phags te / / de ltar rgyu brjod pas nyan thos kyi theg pa las theg pa chen po khyad par du 'phags so / / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i 'bras bu sku gsum du bsdus pa /
tāvat sattvahitakriyāpravṛttasya nirupadhiśeṣe'pi nirvāṇadhātāv
# 'jig rten ji srid du yod pa de srid du sems can la phan par mdzad par zhugs pa /
anuparatasyāsravaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya dyotanād akṣayatvaṃ /
# phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa na yang rgyun mi 'chad pa gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pas mi zad pa yin no /
na tvevaṃ śrāvakayāne /
# nyan thos kyi theg pa ni de lta ma yin te /
śrāvakasambhāraphalaṃ hi kṣayatvam ākhyātaṃ nirupadhiśeṣanirvṛtānāṃ / sarvātmanā samucchedāt / / evaṃ nirvāṇe'pyanuparataṃ phalaṃ dyotanāc chrāvakayānān mahāyānaṃ
# nyan thos kyi tshogs kyi 'bras bu ni phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa rnam pa thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir zad par bshad do / / de ltar mya ngan las 'das pa na yang 'bras bu rgyun mi 'chad par bstan pas /
viśiṣyate / [p.160] / athavā mahāyānasyārtho dānādikaḥ sarvasattvānugrahapravṛttaḥ natvevaṃ
# nyan thos kyi theg pa las theg pa chen po khyad par du 'phags so / / yang na theg pa chen po'i don ni sbyin pa la sogs pa ste / / sems can thams cad la phan gdags par zhugs pa'o /
śrāvakānārthaḥ / / śrāvakāṇāṃ svārthaparatvāt /
# nyan thos kyi theg pa'i don ni de lta ma yin te / / nyan thos rnams rang gi don la brtson pa'i phyir ro /
dānādayaś ca bodhisattvānāṃ dharmā anāsravakāyatvena parivṛttāḥ
# sbyin pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' dag gi chos rnams zag pa med pa'i lus su gyur pas /
parinirvāṇe'pi na vicchidyante /
# mya ngan las 'das kyang rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur gyi /
śrāvakāṇān tu mārgasya kaulopamatvāt parinirvāṇe samucchidyata iti na
# nyan thos rnams kyi lam ni gzings lta bu yin pas yongs su mya ngan las 'das par rgyun 'chad par 'gyur te /
teṣām akṣayatvaṃ /
# de dag gis ni mi zad pa ma yin no /
tasmādyuktaṃ mahāyānasaiva dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ na śrāvakayāna iti
# de bas na theg pa chen po nyid kyi chos sbyor pa 'bras bu chen por rigs kyi nyan thos kyi theg pa ni ma yin no /
{ anudharmapratipattiḥ } / manasikārapratipattyanantaram anudharmapratipātir vaktavyā ityataḥ
# de la yid la byed pa sgrub pa'i 'og tu rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa brjod par bya ste / / de'i phyir rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
pṛcchataḥ - anudharmapratipattiḥ katametyata āha -
# mi g yeng phyin ci ma log par / / 'gyur bar rjes su mthun pa'i chos /
avikṣiptā'viparyāsapraṇatāvānudhārmikī // iti / / dhyātavyajñeyadharmānugatā anupraviṣṭaśamathavipaśyanābhāvātmikā
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / bsam gtan du bya ba dang shes par bya ba'i chos kyi rjes su song ba rjes su zhugs pa'i zhi gnas dang lhag mthong bsgoms pa'i bdag nyid kyi sgrub pa ni /
pratipattir anudharmpratipattiḥ /
# rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa'o /
tatra śamathabhāvanātmikā'vikṣiptā /
# de la zhi gnas bsgom pa'i bdag nyid ni mi g yeng ba'o /
vipaśyanābhāvanātmikā'viparyāsapariṇatā /
# lhag mthong bsgom pa'i bdag nyid ni phyin ci ma log par gyur pa zhes bya ba ste /
iyaṃ dvividhā'nudharmapratipattiḥ //5-11// / { avikṣepapariṇatā } / ayam akāro bahuṣvartheṣu vartata iti kahtam avivikṣepteti na vijñāyata
# 'di rnam gnyis ni rjes su mthun pa'i cho sgrub pa'o / / mi zhes bya ba ni don mang zhig tu yang bsnyegs pas mi g yeng ba zhes bya ba ji lta bu yin par mi shes nas /
ityata āha - tatra ṣaḍvidhavikṣepābhāvād avikṣipteti /
# de'i phyir / / de la g yeng ba rnam pa drug med pa'i phyir mi g yeng ba'o zhes bya ba smos so /
vikṣepo'pi na jñāyāte kathaṃ ṣaḍvidha ityata āha - ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ - / prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirdhāvikṣepa iti vistaraḥ / [p.161]
# g yeng ba rnam pa drug mi shes te / / ji lta bu zhig snyam pa la / / de'i phyir / / g yeng ba rnam pa drug ni zhes rgya cher smos so /
evam api prabhedamātraṃ darśitaṃ na vikṣepasvarūpam iti pṛcchati - sa eṣa
# de ltar yang rab tu dbye ba tsam zhig bstan gyi g yeng ba'i rang gi ngo bo ni ma bshad pas na /
ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ kiṃ lakṣaṇo veditavya ityata āha -
# g yeng ba rnam pa drug po 'di dag gi mtshan nyid ji lta bur rig par bya zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
vyutthānaṃ viṣaye sāraḥ /
# ldang dang yul la 'jug pa dang /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
dhīmatā iti dhaīmān bodhisattvaḥ /
# blo ldan zhes bya ba ni blo can te byang chub sems dpa'o /
tatra vyutthānaṃ samādhitaḥ pañcabhir vijñānakāyair iti /
# de la ldang ba ni rnam par shes pa lnga rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin las ldang ba ste / / zhes bya ba ni /
yadā hi samāhitasya punaḥ pañcānāṃ cakṣurādivijñānānām anyatamad / ekam utpadyate tadā samādhito vyutthito bhavati /
# gang gi tshe mnyam par gzhag pa la mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa lnga rnams las gang yang rung ba gcig cig 'byung ba de'i tshe ting nge 'dzin las langs par gyur pa 'di ni ngo bo nyid kyi g yeng ba ste /
ayañca prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirmukhapravṛttatvāt / / pañcānāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃ vikṣepātmakatvāt pañcabhir
# phyi rol du bltas pa'i phyir ro / / rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga rnams g yeng ba'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir /
vijñānakāyaiḥ samādhito vyutthānaṃ prakṛtivikṣepa ucyate /
# rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga rnams kyis ting nge 'dzin las ldang bar gyur pas na ngo bo nyid kyis g yeng ba zhes bya'o /
viṣaye visāro bahirdhāvikṣepa iti / / yadā samāhitasya samādhyālambanād akāmakasyālambanāntare / manovijñānaṃ pravartate tadālambanāntarasañcārād bahirdhāvikṣepa
# yul la 'jug pa ni phyi rol du g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni / / kha cig na re gang gi tshe mnyam par gzhag pa ting nge 'dzin la dmigs pa las / / mi 'dod bzhin du dmigs pa gzhan la yid kyi rnam par shes pa 'jug pa de'i tshe /
ityeke / / samāhitasya samādhyālambanaṃ hitvā manovijñānasya
# dmigs pa gzhan la 'phos pas phyi rol du g yeng ba'o zhe'o / / gzhan na re mnyam par gzhag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi dmigs pa spangs te /
viṣayāntarasañcāro bahirdhā vikṣepa ityapare / / samādher āsvānadāṃ layauddhatyaṃ cādhyātmavikṣepa iti /
# yid kyi rnam par shes pa yul gzhan du 'phos pa ni phyi rol du g yeng ba'o zhe'o / / ting nge 'dzin gyi ro myang ba dang bying ba dang rgod pa ni nang gi g yeng ba'o zhes bya ba la /
yadi samāhitastameva samādhiṃ tṛṣṇādinā kleśenāsvādayati tataḥ
# gal te mnyam par gzhag pas ting nge 'dzin de nyid la sred pa la sogs pa nyon mongs pas ro myangs na /
śuddhakāt samādher vikṣepo bhavati kliṣṭasamādhipratyupasthānāt /
# nyon mongs can gyi ting nge 'dzin nye bar gnas pa'i phyir yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin de las g yeng bar 'gyur ro /
layauddhatyañca śamathavipaśyanāsamavāhinaḥ samādher vikṣepo bhavati /
# bying ba dang rgod pa dag gis kyang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong mnyam par 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin las g yeng bar 'gyur ro /
asamāhitattvāc cāsvādānālayauddhatyānām / āsvādanādayo'dhyātmavikṣepa ity ucyante /
# ro myang ba dang bying ba dang rgod pas ting nge 'dzin nyams par 'gyur bas na / / ro myang ba la sogs pa ni nang gi g yeng ba'o /
sambhāvanābhisandhir nimittavikṣepaḥ /
# yid ches pa'i bsam pa ni mtshan ma'i g yeng ba ste zhes bya ba ni /
dhyāyyayaṃ mahātmetyevaṃ sambhāvanātmanītyanena nimittena samādhau
# bdag la 'di ni bsam gtan pa ste / / che ba'i bdag nyid can no zhes de ltar yid ches par 'gyur ro snyam pa'i mtshan ma des /
prayuktasyāśayavilayatvālabdhād alabdhād vā kuśalapakṣād vikṣepo
# ting nge 'dzin la brtson pa ni bsam pa log par zhugs pa'i phyir dge ba'i phyogs thob pa'am /
nimittavikṣepa ityucyate / / atraiva kāraṇam āha - tan nimittaṃ kṛtvā prayogād iti /
# ma thob pa las g yeng bas mtshan ma'i g yeng ba zhes bya ste; 'dir rgyu smos pa / / de la mtshan mar byas nas sbyor ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
jñātukāmatayā taṃ sambhāvanābhisandhiḥ nimittaṃ kṛtveti / sambhāvanātmanīti /
# shes kyi khe 'dod pas yid ches pa'i bsam pa de mtshan mar byas nas bdag la yid ches par 'gyur ro snyam ste /
samādhiprayuktatvād iti /
# ting nge 'dzin du zhugs pa'i phyir ro /
sāhaṅkaramanaskāratā dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti / / āśayena samādhiguṇārthino'pi sāhaṅkaramanaskāro'smimānasam
# ngar 'dzin pa dang bcas pa'i yid la byed pa ni gnas ngan len gyi g yeng ba ste zhes bya ba ni snying nas ting nge 'dzin gyi yon tan 'dod kyang /
prayukto'ham asmi dhyāyīti / / tataścātmotkarṣamanyatrāvajñāṃ karotīti /
# bdag ni bsam gtan pa'o zhes nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang ldan te / / de'i phyir / / bdag la ni bstod gzhan la ni khyad du gsod pas na /
kasmād eṣa dauṣṭhulyamanaskāraḥ ?
# ngar 'dzin pa dang bcas pa'i yid la byed pa'o /
ityata āha - dauṣṭhulyavaśenāsmimānasamudācārād iti /
# ci'i phyir 'di la gnas ngan len gyi yid la byed pa zhes bya zhe na / / de'i phyir /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - dauṣṭhulyaprabhāvito vikṣepo dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti /
# gnas ngan len gyi dbang gis nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal kun 'byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
kiṃ punar dauṣṭhulyaṃ ? / asmimānavāsanāparipuṣṭistayā hyasmimānaḥ samudācaratīti
# de ni 'di skad du / / g yeng ba ni gnas ngan len gyis rab tu phye'o zhes ston par 'gyur ro /
tadvaśenāsmimānasamudācārāt / / satkāyadṛṣṭir dauṣṭhulyam ityanye /
# gnas ngan len ci zhe na / / nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal gyi bag chags yongs su brtas pa ste /
hīnacittatvaṃ manasikāravikṣepa iti /
# des nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal kun du 'byung bas /
aniyataśrāvakādigotrasya [p.162]
# de'i dbang gis nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal kun du 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
mahāyānamanasikāraprayuktasya samsaraduḥkhabhīrutayā
# gzhan dag na re 'jig tshogs la lta ba ni gnas ngan len to zhe'o /
sattvavipratipānatvenākalyāṇamitraniṣevaṇena ca tac / chrāvakapratyekabuddhacittam utpadyate / / taccittaṃ hīnaṃ svārthamātraparāyaṇatvāt / / tacchrāvakapratyekabuddhacittaṃ mahāyānamanasikāravikṣepakatvān / manasikāravikṣepaḥ kathyate /
# dman pa'i sems ni yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba ste zhes bya ba ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i rigs su ma nges pa theg pa chen po yid la byed pa dang ldan pa 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis skrag pa dang sems can log par zhugs pa dang mi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bsten pas na nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sems bskyed par 'gyur te / / rang gi don tsam 'dzin pa'i phyir de ni sems dman pa'o / / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sems de ni / / theg pa chen po yid la byed pa las g yeng bar byed pas yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba zhes bya ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - hīnayāna manasikārasamudācārād iti /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / theg pa dman pa yid la byed pa kun du 'byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
hīnayānaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānaṃ /
# theg pa dman pa ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa ste /
ātmaparinirvāṇādhikārapravṛttatvān manasikārasamudācāro / mahāyānamanasikārebhyo vikṣipatīti hīnaṃ cittaṃ manasikāravikṣepa ity / ucyate / / evam iyaṃ bodhisattvasya ṣaḍvidhavikṣepadoṣarahitā śamathābhāvanā / veditavyā //
# bdag yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar bya ba'i ched du zhugs pa dang yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba kun du 'byung ba'i phyir theg pa chen po yid la byed pa las g yeng bar byed pas na / / dman pa'i sems ni yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba zhes bya'o / / de ltar na 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' g yeng ba rnam pa drug gi skyon dang bral ba'i zhi gnas bsgom par rig par bya'o /
{ aviparyāsapariṇatā } / evam avikṣiptena yathā'viparyāsapariṇatā'nudharmapratipattir
# de ltar g yeng ba med pas ji ltar phyin ci ma log par gyur pa'i rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa bsgom par bya ba de ltar 'chad de /
bhāvayitavyā tathocyate / / aviparyāsātmanā pravṛttā'viparyāsapariṇatā / / tatra yad yathā vyavasthitaṃ vastu tathā tatra jñānam aviparyāsaḥ /
# phyin ci ma log pa'i bdag nyid du zhugs pa ni phyin ci ma log par gyur pa'o / / de la gang ji ltar gnas pa'i gzhi de la de bzhin du shes pa ni phyin ci ma log pa ste /
tad vastuta punar na jñāyate katividhe vastunītyata āha - / tatrāviparyāso daśavidhe vastuni veditavya iti /
# gzhi de yang rnam pa du yod mi shes nas / / de'i phyir / / de la phyin ci ma log pa ni dngos po rnam pa bcur rig par bya ste zhes bya ba smos so /
aviparyāsavastu pradarśanārthaṃ bravīti - yaduta [p.163]
# phyin ci ma log pa'i gzhi bstan pa'i phyir / / 'di lta ste /
vyañjanārthamanaskārāvisāre lakṣaṇadvaye /
# yi ge don dang yid byed dang / / mi 'phro ba dang mtshan nyid gnyis /
iti vistaraḥ / / idānīṃ teṣu vastuṣu yathā viparyāso bhavati tat pradarśanārtham āha -
# zhes bya ba smos so / / da ni gzhi de dag la ji ltar phyin ci ma log par gyur pa de bstan pa'i phyir de la /
tatra / saṃyogāt saṃbhavāc caiva viyogād apyasambhavāt /
# 'brel pa'i phyir dang 'dris phyir dang / / ma 'brel phyir dang ma 'dres phyir / / don yod pa dang med pa ste /
arthasattvam asattvañca vyañjane so'viparyayaḥ // iti / / saṃyoge sati vyañjanānām iti /
# de ni yi ger ma log pa'o / / zhes bya ba smos so / / yi ge rnams 'brel te zhes bya ba la /
saṃyogo hi parasparasaṃśleṣaḥ /
# 'brel pa ni phan tshun 'byar ba yin na /
na cāsau vyañjanānāṃ vidyate yaugapadyābhāvāt /
# cig car 'byung ba med pa'i phyir de yang yi ge rnams la med do /
vyañjanānāṃ yugapad uccāraṇaṃ na yujyate /
# yi ge rnams la cig car brjod du mi rung ste /
pūrvavikalpānām uttaravyañjanoccaraṇakāle'navasthānam / uccāraṇānantaram eva vinaṣṭatvād ityāśaṅkāvyudāsārtham āha -
# sngar brjod pa rnams ni brjod ma thag tu zhig pas yi ge phyi ma brjod pa'i dus su mi sdod do snyam pa'i dogs pa bsal ba'i phyir / / rgyun mi 'chad par brjod pa zhes bya ba smos te /
avicchinnoccāraṇatayeti / / etad uktaṃ bhavati - aviparyastāvilambitoccāraṇam atra vyañjanānāṃ
# de ni 'di skad du / / ma nor ba dang ma thogs par brjod pa la 'dir yi ge rnams 'brel par 'dod kyi /
saṃyoga iṣyate na tu vyañjanānāṃ parasparasaṃśleṣaṇam iti /
# yi ge rnams phan tshun 'byar ba ni ma yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
asya cedaṃ nāmeti sambhavād iti / / yadi cāsya vastuna idaṃ nāmeti saṅketo'bhyasto bhavati evam anena
# 'di'i ming ni 'di zhes bya'o zhes 'dris pas zhes bya ba ni dngos po 'di'i ming 'di'o zhes brdal goms par gyur pa ste /
prakāradvayena sārthakatvaṃ vyañjanānāṃ pratyāyakatvam ityarthaḥ /
# de ltar rnam pa 'di gnyis kyis yi ge rnams don yod pa nyid du khong du chud par byed do zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
viparyayān nirarthakatvam iti /
# bzlog pa ni don med pa nyid do zhes bya ba ni gnyi ga med pa'am /
ubhayābhāvo'nyataravaikalyaṃ vā viparyayaḥ /
# gang yang rung ba ma tshang ba med pa ni bzlog pa'o /
yadevaṃ darśanam iti jñānaṃ / / so'viparyāso vyañjane veditavya iti saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ /
# de ltar bzlog pa gang yin pa zhes bya ba ni shes pa'o / / de ni yi ge la phyin ci ma log par rig par bya'o zhes bya ba ni kun rdzob yin gyi /
paramārthenāviparyāsasya nirvikalpakatvād ityanenāviparyāsena
# don dam par ni ma yin te / / don dam par ni phyin ci ma log par rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
bodhisattvaḥ śabdārtharahitān sarvadharmān pratividhyati / / idānīṃ vyañjanaprajñaptinimitte'rthe'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# phyin ci ma log pa 'dis kyang byang chub sems dpa' sgra'i don dang bral ba'i chos thams cad rtogs par 'gyur ro / / da ni yi ger 'dogs pa'i rgyu'i don la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir /
dvayena pratibhāsatvaṃ tathā cāvidyamānatā /
# gnyis su snang bar gyur pa ni / / de ltar yod pa ma yin te /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
dvayena grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate /
# gnyis ni gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba ste zhes bya ba ni gang zhig ce na /
kaḥ ? / paratantrasvabhāvaḥ /
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid do /
kasmāt ? / grāhyagrāhakabījayuktatvāt / / kah punar atra pratibhāsārtha ityata āha - tadākārotpattita iti / / grāhyagrāhakākārotpattito grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate na punaḥ
# ci'i phyir zhe na / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i phyir ro / / 'di la snang ba'i don gang zhe na / / de'i phyir de'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par 'byung bas gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang gi /
sphāṭikavad upadhānoparāgād iti / / tathā ca na vidyate yathā pratibhāsate advayaprakṛtitvāt /
# shel sgong ltar nye bar gzhag par 'gyur ba lta bu ni ma yin no / / de ltar yod pa ma yin te / / zhes bya ba ni gnyis po med pa'i rang bzhin yin pas ji ltar snang ba'i rnam pa de ltar med pa'o /
iti evaṃ bhrāntivijñānotpattinimittabhūte'rthe yad darśanaṃ sa / tatrāviparyāsaḥ sadasattvavarjanādityabhiprāyaḥ /
# de ltar 'khrul pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rgyur gyur pa'i phyir / / don la mthong ba gang yin pa de ni de la phyin ci ma log pa'o zhes bya ba ni yod pa dang med pa spangs pa'i phyir ro snyam du dgongs pa'o /
arthasya sattvena varjita ityatraiva kāraṇam āha -
# don gyi yod pa spangs pa zhes bya ba la / / 'dir rgyu smos pa /
grāhyagrāhakābhāvād iti / / arthasya sattvaṃ [p.164]
# gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o /
grāhyagrāhakasadbhāvaḥ /
# don gyi yod pa ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa yod pa'o /
tena varjito grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa śūnyatvād iti /
# de spangs pa ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam pas stong pa'i phyir ro /
asattvena varjitaḥ / / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# med pa spangs pa ci'i phyir zhe na /
tat pratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād iti / grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād ityarthaḥ /
# der snang ba'i 'khrul pa yod pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste / / gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba'i 'khrul pa yod do zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ayam api saṃvṛttā'viparyāsa ucyate na paramārthataḥ savikalpatvāt /
# 'di yang kun rdzob tu phyin ci ma log pa zhes bya'i don dam par ni ma yin te / / rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i phyir ro /
anenāviparyāsajñānena bodhisattvo grāhyagrāhakasvabhāvarahitān / sarvadharmān pratividhyatīti / / idānīṃ grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānanimitte / ālayavijñāne'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# phyin ci ma log par shes pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i ngo bo nyid dang bral bar rab tu rtogs so / / da ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rgyu kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir /
tajjalpabhāvito jalpamanaskāras tadāśrayaḥ /
# rtog pa de yis bsgos pa yi / / rtog pa yid byed de'i gnas ni /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
grāhyagrāhakajalpaparibhāvito jalpamaskāra iti / / tasmin grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānalakṣaṇe'rthe'yaṃ grāhyo'yaṃ grāhaka iti
# gzung ba dang 'dzin par rtog pas yongs su bsgos pa ni rtog pa'i yid la byed pa ste zhes bya ba ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i rnam par snang ba'i mtshan nyid kyi don de la 'di ni gzung ba'o /
vāṅmanobhyāṃ yad abhilapanaṃ sa jalpa ity ucyate /
# 'di ni 'dzin pa'o zhes ngag dang yid kyis brjod pa gang yin pa de ni rtog pa zhes bya'o /
anena jalpena paribhāvito'nāgatataj jātīyajalpotpādāya
# rtog pa des yongs su bsgos pa ni ma 'ongs pa na / / rigs 'dra ba'i rtog pa bskyed pa'i phyir /
bījaparipoṣaṇam iti paribhāvita ity ucyate /
# sa bon yongs su brtas par byed pas na bsgos pa zhes bya'o /
so'yaṃ jalpaparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ityākhyāyate kārye / kāraṇopacārāt /
# de ni rtog pa'i yongs su bsgos pa'i phyir / / 'bras bu la rgyu btags te rtog pa yid la byed pa zhes bya'o /
jalpavāsanā stvatra jalpaḥ /
# rtog pa'i bag chags ni 'dir rtog pa ste /
jalpo'trāstītyādhārādheyayor abhedaṃ kṛtvā ādhāraśabdasya vā
# de la rtog pa yod pas na rten dang brten pa dbye ba ma byas pa'i phyir ram /
grahaṇāj jalpamanaskāra ityucyate /
# yang na rten gyi sgra ma smos pa'i phyir rtog pa yid la byed pa zhes bya ba ste /
tasya grāhyagrāhakavikalpasya jalpākhyasya bījādhāratvāt /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin par rnam par rtog pa de'i sa bon gyi rten du gyur pa'i phyir ro /
punaś ca jalpasya tat sanniśrayeṇotpāter āśrayo bhavatītyayaṃ
# de la brten nas yang rtog pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / rten yin pas 'di ni yid la byed pa la phyin ci ma log pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
manaskāre'viparyāsa ityaviparītaṃ jñānam ityarthaḥ /
# phyin ci ma log par shes pa'o zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
sa tu manaskāro na vijṇyāte yasminn aviparyāsa ityataḥ pṛcchati - katam
# yid la byed pa gang la phyin ci ma log pa'i yid la byed pa de yang mi shes nas /
asminmanaskāre'viparyāsa iti / / ato manaskāraviśeṣaṇārtham āha - grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇe
# yid la byed pa gang la phyin ci ma log ce na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir yid la byed pa'i khyad par bstan pa'i phyir / / gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba'i rgyu la ste zhes bya ba smos te /
ālayavijñānaviśeṣātmaka ityarthaḥ / / yathāsau grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavati tat pradarśanārtham / āha - sa hyasau jalpamanaskāro'bhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvād iti /
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i khyad par gyi bdag nyid ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / ji ltar 'di gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba'i rgyur 'gyur ba de bstan pa'i phyir / / rtog pa yid la byed pa ni brjod pa'i 'du shes kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos te /
grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavatīti sambadhyate / / athavā jalpamanaskāra ityato'bhidhānapravṛttinimittam āha /
# gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba'i rgyu yin no zhes bya bar sbyar ro / / yang na rtog pa'i yid la byed pa zhes brjod pa 'jug pa'i rgyu yin par bstan pa'i phyir /
abhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ucyata iti / / abhilāpasamutthā abhilāpasamutthāpikā vā saṃjñā abhilāpasaṃjñā /
# brjod pa'i 'du shes kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i phyir rtog pa yid la byed pa zhes bya'o zhes bya ba smos so / / brjod pa las byung ba'am / / brjod pa kun nas slong ba'i 'du shes pa ni brjod pa'i 'du shes te /
tayā sasamprayogayā jalpamanaskāre svabījaparipoṣaṇāj jalpamanasikāraḥ / paribhāvita ucyate / / ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ / / anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viparyāsanidānaṃ / grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśalakṣaṇaṃ parivarjayati / / evaṃ tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ sukhena varjitaṃ bhavatīti // [p.165] / idānīm avisāre'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# mtshungs par ldan pa dang ldan pa dang bcas pa des / / rtog pa'i yid la byed pa la rang gi sa bon yongs su gsos pas rtog pa yid la byed pa yongs su bsgos pa zhes bya'o / / 'di yang kun rdzob tu phyin ci ma log pa ste; don dam par ni ma yin no / / phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' phyin ci log gi gzhi gzung ba dang 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su spong ste / / de ltar na gnas ngan len de bde blag tu spong bar 'gyur ro / / nga ni mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir /
māyādivad asattvañca sattvañcārthasya tan mataṃ /
# don gyi med dang yod pa ste / / sgyu ma la sogs bzhin du 'dod /
iti vistaraḥ /
# ces rgya cher gsungs so /
yat tadarthasyāsattvaṃ sattvañcānantaramuktam iti /
# don gyi yod pa dang med pa gong du bshad ma thag pa gang yin pa zhes bya ba la /
katham anantaram uktam iti ?
# gong du bshad pa gang zhe na /
dvayena praibhāsatvaṃ tathā cāvidyamānatā /
# gnyis su snang bar gyur ba ni / / de ltar yod pa ma yin te /
arthe sa cā'viparyāsaḥ sadasattvena varjtiaḥ /
# de ni don la ma log pa / / yod dang med pa rnam par spangs /
iti tanamāyādivan mataṃ / / māyādīnām iva māyādivat / / etad eva pradarśayann āha -yathā māyā svātmanyavidyamānena / hastyādyātmanā prakhyānān na hastyādibhāvenāstīti / / hastyādibhāvena nāstīti sarvathaiva nāsti / / kiṃ tarhi na ca naivāsti tad bhrāntimātrāstitvād iti /
# zhes bya ba'o / / de ni sgyu ma la sogs pa bzhin du 'dod de / / sgyu ma la sogs pa dang 'dra bas na / / sgyu ma la sogs pa bzhin no / / de nyid bstan pa'i phyir / / dper na sgyu ma ni rang gi bdag nyid kyis med bzhin du / / glang po che la sogs pa'i bdag nyid du snang bas na / / glang po che la sogs pa'i dngos por yod pa yin la zhes bya ba ni glang po che la sogs pa'i dngos por med pas / / rnam pa thams cad du med pa yang ma yin te / / de ni 'khrul pa tsam du yod pa'i phyir med pa'ang ma yin te /
tasya hastyādyākāreṇa prakhyāyamānasya bhrāntimātrasyāstitvān na / sarvathā nāsti / / tathārtho'pi na cāsti yathā samprakhyāti grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā / naivāsti / [p.166] / tasya traidhātukacittacaittasvarūpasya tathāprakhyāyamānasya
# glang po che la sogs pa'i rnam par snang ba de ni / / 'khrul pa tsam du yod pa'i phyir ye med pa'ang ma yin no / / de bzhin du yod kyang ji ltar gzung ba dang 'dzin par snang ba ltar yod pa'ang ma yin la / / khams gsum pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i rang gi ngo bo de /
bhrāntimātrāstitvān nāpi nāsti / / ādiśabdena marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo dṛṣṭāntā yathāyogaṃ veditavyā  iti / / nahi marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo yathā strīpumātmanā prakhyāyante / tathā santi na ca santyeva bhrāntimātrāstitvāt evam artho'pīti
# de lta bur snang ba de 'khrul pa tsam du yod pa'i phyir med pa'ang ma yin no / / sogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgras ni smig rgyu dang rmi lam dang chu zla la sogs pa chu dang skyes pa dang bud med kyi bdag nyid du ji ltar snang ba de bzhin du yod pa ma yin la / / de la 'khrul pa tsam du yod pa'i phyir med pa'ang ma yin no /
vistareṇa pratyekaṃ yojayitavyaṃ / / atra cādiśabdena gandharvanagarapratiśrutkādayo veditavyāḥ /
# de bzhin du don la rgya cher so sor sbyar bar bya'o / / 'dir yang sogs pa'i sgras ni dri za'i grong khyer dang brag ca la sogs par rig par bya'o /
evaṃ yan māyādyupamārthadarśanāt sattvāsattvapakṣayor avisāraṃ cetasaḥ
# de ltar don la sgyu ma la sogs pa lta bur mthong nas / / yod pa dang med pa'i phyogs la sems mi 'phro ste /
avikṣiptatvaṃ paśyati so'visāre'viparyāsaḥ /
# g yeng ba med par mthong ba gang yin pa de ni mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log pa'o /
kaḥ punar avisāraḥ ?
# mi 'pho ba gang zhe na /
madhyamā pratipat samādhir ityanye /
# gzhan dag na re dbu ma'i lam gyi ting nge 'dzin to zhe'o /
yadyevaṃ katham avisāre'viparyāsa ityata āha - tena
# gal te de lta na ji ltar mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log par 'gyur zhe na / / de'i phyir /
bhāvābhāvayościttasyāvisaraṇād iti /
# des yod pa dang med pa la sems 'phro ba med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
anenāviparyāsena bodhisattvo / bhāvābhāvavikalparahitāchūnyatā'lambane'vikṣepaḥ /
# phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' yod pa dang med par rtog pa med pa'i phyir ro / / stong pa nyid la dmigs pa las mi g yeng ste /
tasmād avisāre viparyāsa ucyate / / ayam api saṃvṛttyairvāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt / idānīṃ svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# de bas na mi 'phro ba la phyin ci ma log pa zhes bya'o / / 'di yang kun rdzob tu phyin ci ma log pa yin gyi / / don dam par ni ma yin te / / de ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro / / da ni rang gi mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa bstan pa'i phyir /
sarvasya nāmamātratvaṃ sarvakalpāpravṛttaye /
# rtog pa thams cad mi 'jug phyir / / thams cad ming tsam kho na ste /
iti vistaraḥ / / sarvam idaṃ nāmamātraṃ yadidaṃ cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā iti /
# zhes bya ba rgya cher gsungs so / / gang 'di mig dang gzugs rnams nas / / yid dang chos rnams zhes bya ba'i bar 'di dag thams cad ni ming tsam mo /
ato dvādaśāyatanātmakaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvaṃ nāmamātraṃ / / tatra nāmasvabhāvaviśeṣaprajñaptiḥ / / na ca prajñaptyasyārthasya prajñapter vā svabhāvo'sti /
# zhes bya ba ni skye mched bcu gnyis kyi bdag nyid shes bya thams cad ni ming tsam mo / / de la ming gi ngo bo nyid dang khyad par du 'dogs pa'o / / gdags par bya ba'i don dang btags pa ni ngo bo nyid med de /
tenātmanā parikalpitatvāt parikalpitasya cāsattvāt / / anyathā nāmanirapekṣayā cakṣurāditvena grahaṇaṃ syāt /
# de'i bdag nyid du kun brtags pa'i phyir ro / / kun brtags pa yang med pa'i phyir ro / / gzhan du na ni ming la mi ltos par mig la sogs par 'dzin par 'gyur te /
na cāstyavyutpannasaṅketasya grahaṇaṃ /
# brda la ma byang bar mi 'dzin pa med do /
tasmāc cakṣūrupam ityādyasyātat svabhāvatvān nāmamātram eva / cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā ityevaṃ yaj jñānaṃ sarvavikalpānāṃ
# de bas na mig dang gzugs zhes bya ba de ni / / don gyi ngo bo nyid ma yin pas mig dang gzugs nas yid dang chos rnams zhes bya ba'i bar dag ni ming tsam mo zhes /
pratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsa iti parikalpitadharmamukhena / sarvadharmeṣu sarvavikalpapravṛttiḥ / / ato nāmamātraprativedhajñānaṃ sarvavikalpapratipakṣaḥ
# de ltar gang shes pa ni rnam par rtog pa thams cad kyi gnyen po yin pas 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa'o zhes bya ba ni kun brtags pa'i chos kyi sgo nas / / chos thams cad la rnam par rtog pa thams cad 'jug ste / / de bas na ming tsam du rtogs pa'i shes pa rnam par rtog pa thams cad kyi gnyen po ni /
svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsa ity uktaṃ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa zhes bstan to /
tatra na jñāyate kiṃ paramārthe svalakṣaṇe āhosvit saṃvṛtāv ityataḥ
# de'ang ci don dam pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid la'am 'on te kun rdzob kyi la bya ba mi shes nas / / de'i phyir /
pṛcchati - katam asmin svalakṣaṇa iti / / ata āha - / paramārthe svalakṣaṇe / / ayam aviparyāsaḥ /
# rang gi mtshan nyid gang la zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir don dam pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid la'o zhes bya ba gsungs te / / 'di ni phyin ci ma log pa'o /
paramārthasya svalakṣaṇasyānabhilāpyatvān na saṃvṛteḥ /
# don dam pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid ni brjod du med pa'i phyir kun rdzob tu ni ma yin no /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ? / saṃvṛttyā yato nedaṃ nāmamātram iti gṛhyate abhilāpadvāreṇa
# ci'i phyir zhe na / / 'di ltar kun rdzob tu ni ming 'di tsam mo zhes 'dzin pa med de /
dharmasvarūpe saṅkalpapravṛtteḥ ayam api saṃvṛtyaiva na paramārthato / nāmamātram iti vikalpanāt / / anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvaḥ saṃvṛtiparamārthakuśalo bhavati / [p.167]
# brjod pa'i sgo nas chos kyi ngo bo nyid la kun tu rtog pa 'jug pa'i phyir / / 'di ni kun rdzob nyid yin gyi don dam par ni ma yin te / / ming tsam du rnam par rtog pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' kun rdzob dang don dam pa la mkhas par 'gyur ro /
idānīṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇe'viparyāsapradarśanāyāha - / dharmadhātuvinirmukto yasmād dharmo na vidyate /
# da ni spyi'i mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir; chos kyi dbyings ni ma rtogs par / / 'di ltar chos yod ma yin te /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
na hi dharmanairātmyena vinā kaścid rūpyarūpī vā dharmo vidyate /
# chos la dbang med pa ma rtogs pa'i chos / / gzugs can nam gzugs med pa gang yang med de /
sarva dharmāṇām anabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtatvād grāhagrāhakabhāvena
# chos thams cad ni brjod du med pa'i rang bzhin la / / gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i dngos po dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
rahitatvāt / / tasmād dharmadhātuḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇam iti /
# de bas na chos kyi dbyings ni / / chos thams cad ni spyi'i mtshan nyid do zhes bya ba ste /
sarvadharmeṣv apṛthaktvena tat sat sāmānyalakṣaṇam ucyate / / yadevaṃ jñānamayaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇo'viparyāsaḥ saṃvṛttyā na tu
# chos thams cad la bye brag med par de yod pa'i spyi'i mtshan nyid ces bya'o / / de ltar shes pa gang yin pa de ni spyi'i mtshan nyid la phyin ci ma log pa ste /
paramārthataḥ / / tasya nirvikalpatvāt / / tad anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viśuddhyālambanakuśalo bhavati / nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt / / viśeṣaḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇasvalaksaṇayoḥ ko vidyate ?
# kun rdzob tu yin gyi don dam par ni ma yin te de rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' rnams par dag pa'i dmigs pa la mkhas par 'gyur te / / rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid gnyis la khyad par ci yod ce na /
abhilāpasvabhāvasamāropitatvasya pratipakṣeṇānabhilāpyasvabhāvatā / paramārthalakṣaṇaṃ /
# brjod pa'i ngo bo nyid du sgro btags pa'i gnyen por brjod du med pa'i ngo bo nyid ni don dam pa'i mtshan nyid do /
parikalpitasvabhāva-nairātmyaṃ punaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtir iti
# kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi bdag med pa ni chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin te /
sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ / / evaṃ darśanabhedavaśād viśeṣo bhavati na tv arthād iti / / idānīṃ dharmadhātv aviśuddhiviśuddhāv aviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# spyi'i mtshan nyid do / / de ltar mthong ba tha dad pa'i dbang gis khyad par du gyur gyi / / don las ni ma yin no / / da ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par ma dag pa dang rnam par dag pa la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir /
viparyasta manaskārāvihāniparihāṇitaḥ /
# phyin ci log gi yid la byed / / ma spangs pa dang spangs pa las /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
viparyasta manaskāraprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ tat prahāṇaṃ
# phyin ci log gi yid la byed pa ma spangs pa ni / / chos kyi dbyings de rnam par ma dag pa'o /
viśuddhir iti / / tatra viparyasta manaskāra ālayavijñānahetur viparyayavikalpaḥ /
# spangs pa ni rnam par dag pa'o zhes bya ba de la / / phyin ci log gi yid la byed pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i rgyu phyin ci log tu rnam par rtog pa ste /
tasyāprahāṇaṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ /
# de ma spangs pa ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par ma dag pa'o / / spangs pa ni rnam par dag pa ste /
yadevaṃ jñānamayam aviśuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāso yathākramam iti /
# de ltar shes pa gang yin pa de ni rnam par ma dag pa dang rnam par dag pa la phyin ci ma log pa ste / / go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba la /
viparyasta manaskārāprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhir iti / dharmadhātor aviśuddhāvaviparyāsaḥ / / tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir iti viśuddhāv aviparyāsaḥ /
# phyin ci log gi yid la byed pa ma spangs pa ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par ma dag pa'o zhes bya ba ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par ma dag pa la phyin ci ma log pa'o / / de spangs pa ni rnam par dag pa'o zhes bya ba ni rnam par dag pa la phyin ci ma log pa'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# ci'i phyir zhe na /
dharmadhātor āgantukenopakleśenopakliṣṭatvāt /
# chos kyi dbyings la glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pas nyon mongs par gyur pa'i phyir ro /
ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ /
# 'di yang kun rdzob tu phyin ci ma log pa ste / / don dam par ni ma yin no /
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo'prahīṇāvaraṇaṃ dharmadhātoḥ / prahāṇañca prajānāti / / idānīṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddher / viśuddheścāgantukatve'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi dbyings la sgrib pa spangs pa dang ma spangs pa rab tu shes so / / da ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa dang rnam par ma dag pa glo bur du 'byung ba la phyin ci ma log pa bstan pa'i phyir /
dharmadhātor viśuddhatvāt prakṛtyā vyomavat punaḥ /
# chos kyi dbyings ni rang bzhin gyis / / rnam par dag phyir nam mkha' bzhin /
iti vistaraḥ / / dharmadhātoḥ punar ākāśavat prakṛtiviśuddhitatvād dvayam
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so / / chos kyi dbyings nam mkha' bzhin du rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa'i phyir /
apyetadāgantukam aviśuddhir viśuddhiś ca paścād iti /
# rnam par ma dad pa dang phyis rnam par dag ces bya ba 'di gnyis kyang glo bur yin zhes bya ba de la /
tatra dharmadhātorabhūtavikalpopakliṣṭatvād aśuddhir uktā / / paścāc ca pratipakṣodayena tat prahāṇād viśuddhiḥ /
# chos kyi dbyings sa la yang dag pa ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pas rnam par ma dag pa zhes bshad do / / phyis gnyen po byung nas de spangs pas rnam par dag pa ste /
etad dvayam api dharmadhātāv āgantukaṃ /
# de gnyi ga yang chos kyi dbyings la glo bur yin no /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# ci'i phyir zhe na /
ākāśavad dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvāt /
# nam mkha' bzhin du chos kyi dbyings rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa'i phyir ro /
prakṛtiviśuddhasyāviśuddhir āgantukī bhaved viśuddhes tu nityaviśuddhitaḥ / katham āgantukībhāva iti ?
# rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa la rnam par ma dag pa ni glo bur yin grang na rnam par dag pa ni rtag tu rnam par dag pa yin pas ji ltar glo bur du 'gyur zhe na /
yā malavigamatātmatayā viśuddhiḥ sātra vivakṣiteti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ /
# dri ma dang bral bas rnam par dag pa gang yin pa de 'dir brjod pas 'dod pas na nyes pa 'di med de /
ata evoktaṃ viśuddhiś ca paścād iti /
# de bas na 'di skad du rnam par dag pa ni phyis rnam par dag ces bshad do /
yadevaṃ dharmadhātor jñānam etad dharmadhātor viśuddhi viśuddhyor / āgantukatve'viparyāsaḥ / / ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ /
# de ltar shes pa gang yin pa de ni chos kyi dbyings la rnam par ma dag pa dang rnam par dag pa glo bur du byung ba nyid la phyin ci ma log pa'o / / 'di yang kun rdzob tu yin gyi don dam par ni ma yin no /
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo dharmadhātoḥ / saṅkleśavyavadānāvasthayoḥ kṛtrimatvaṃ prajānātīti // [p.168] / idānīmatrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha -
# phyin ci ma log pa 'dis byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings la kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i dus na bcos ma ma yin par rab tu shes so / / da ni mi skrag pa dang ma khengs pa la phyin ci ma log par bstan pa'i phyir /
saṅkleśaś ca viśuddhiś ca dharmapudgalayor na hi /
# chos rnams dang ni gang zag gi / / kun nas nyon mongs rnam dag med /
iti vistaraḥ /
# ces rgya cher gsungs so /
na hi pudgalasya saṅkleśo na viśuddhiḥ nāpi dharmasya /
# gang zag gis kun nas nyon mongs pa med / / rnam par dag pa med / / chos kyang med de /
saṅkleśo viśuddhirśceti vartate /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag pa zhes bya bar bsnyegs so /
atraiva kāraṇam āha - yasmān na pudgalo'sti na dharmaḥ /
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / 'di ltar gang zag med cing chos med pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
astītyanuvartate / / yaḥ saṅkleśavyavadānavyatirekeṇa vidyate yasya saṅkleśo vyavadānaṃ vā
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis kyi dus na / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba ma gtogs par gang zhig yod na ni /
parikalpayituṃ yujyate yat pṛthaktvena ca saṃkleśaviśuddhī syātāṃ  sa
# de'i kun nas nyon mongs pa'am rnam par byang bar yongs su brtag tu rung ste / / de tha dad pas 'grib pa dang 'phel bar yang 'gyur na /
tādṛśaḥ pudgalo nāsti pratyakṣānumānāviṣayatvāt /
# de lta bu'i gang zag ni med de / / mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa'i yul ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
dharmo'pi parikalpitātmako naivāsti ekasminn vastuny ekaparikalpapravṛtteḥ
# dngos po gcig la du mar yongs su rtog pa 'jug pa'i phyir kun brtags pa'i bdag nyid kyi chos kyang yod pa ma yin te /
na caikasyānekātmakatā yujyate ato'sattvāt pudgaladharmayordvayo
# gcig ni du ma'i bdag nyid du mi rung ngo / / de bas na gang zag dang chos gnyis mo gsham gyi bu la sogs pa bzhin du med pas na /
bandhnyaputrādivanna saṅleśo na vyavadānaṃ /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba med do /
paratantrsyāpi ṣuddaloukikajñanagocarasya saṅkleśaviśuddhī naiveṣyate /
# dag pa 'jig rten pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul gzhan gyi dbang la ni / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar mi 'dod do /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ ?
# ci'i phyir zhe na /
tasya nirabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtitvāt /
# brjod du med pa dang gnyis su med pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro /
yadi paratantrasyāpi neṣyate kasya te syātāṃ ?
# gal te gzhan gyi dbang gi yang ma yin par 'dod na go de dag gi yin te /
tasminn asati saṅkleśaparihāre vyavadānaprāptiyatnavaiyarthyaṃ /
# de med na kun nas nyon mongs pa spang ba dang rnam par byang ba thob par bya ba'i phyir 'bad pa don med par 'gyur ro zhe na /
dharmadhātoḥ saṅkleśaviśuddhī bhavata ity ayam adoṣaḥ /
# chos kyi dbyings kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par dag par 'gyur bas nyes pa 'di med do /
dharmadhātor apyatanmayasyaiva te vyavasthāpyete dharmadhātau tayor
# chos kyi dbyings de'i bdag nyid ma yin pa nyid la de dag rnam par gzhag ste /
āgantukatvād dharmadhātoścākāśavad avikārāt / / tataḥ na saṃkleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe vā kaścid viśeṣo
# chos kyi dbyings la de gnyi ga la yang glo bur yin la chos kyi dbyings kyang nam mkha' bzhin du 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir / / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs la su'i 'grib pa yang med la / / rnam par byang ba'i phyogs la su'i khyad par du 'gyur ba yang med na /
yatas trāso vā syān mānovetyamatrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsa iti /
# gang gi phyir skrag pa'am nga rgyal du 'gyur te / / 'di ni skrag pa med pa dang khengs pa med pa la phyin ci ma log pa'o /
anye tvāhuḥ - na saṅkleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe
# gzhan dag na re kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs la yang su'i 'grib pa yang med la /
viśeṣo'sti tad ubhayavataḥ kasyacid abhāvāt /
# rnam par byang ba'i phyogs la yang su'i khyad par du 'gyur ba yang med de /
yataḥ punas ta evaṃ bhavatas tatra kim iti trāso bhavaty ayaṃ me nāstīti / kim iti māno bhavaty ayaṃ me viśeṣa iti / [p.169]
# de gnyi ga dang ldan pa su yang med pa'i phyir ro / / gang gi phyir de dag ni de lta ma yin pas de la nga'i 'di med do zhes skrag par 'gyur du'ang ci yod / / nga'i khyad par ni 'di yin no zhes nga rgyal du 'gyur du yang ci yod ces zer ro /
apare tu manyate - pudgalas tāvan naivāsti / / dharmo'pi naivāsti / / avasthādvayaṃ yo'nubhavati yasyaitad dvayaṃ kalpyeta /
# gzhan dag ni 'di snyam du sems te / / gang zag ni med pa nyid do / / gang gnas 'di gnyis myong ba dang 'di gnyis gang la brtag pa'i chos de yang med pa nyid do /
kiṃ tarhi pratītyasamutpādamātram etat saṅkleśavyavadānam iti /
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba 'di dag ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba nyid du zad do snyam mo /
ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt /
# 'di yang kun rdzob tu'o don dam par ni ma yin te / / de ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
anena cāviparyāsena kṣayavṛddhyasadbhāvād avikāritvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ / pratividhyatīti /
