# byung nas kyang shing gnyis tshig par byed do / / de bzhin du yang dag pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid ma yin pa yang dag par so sor rtog pa las /
āryaṃ prajñendriyaṃ jāyate / / jātaś ca tām eva bhūtaparatyavekṣāṃ dahati /
# yang dag pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid 'phags pa'i shes rab kyi dbang po skye ste / / skyes nas kyang yang dag par so sor rtog pa nyid tshig par byed de /
vibhāvayatītyarthaḥ / / sā hi vibhāvanād eva dagdheva dagdhety ucyate vikṛtidarśanāt /
# rnam par 'jig par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / rnam par 'jig pa de yang tshig pa dang 'dra bar byed pas na tshig par byed ces bya ste /
iyañca bhūtapratyavekṣā sāsravāpi satī samyaktvānukūlyād
# gyur par mthong ba'i phyir ro / / yang dag par so sor rtog pa 'di zag pa dang bcas pa yin yang /
bhūtapratyavekṣety ucyata iti / / vyāpṛtāv api vikalpo'ntaḥ avyāpṛtāv api /
# yang dag pa nyid kyi rjes su mthun pa'i phyir yang dag par so sor rtog pa zhes bya bar ston to / / byed par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o /
vikalpo'nta ity adhikṛtaṃ /
# mi byed par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha' ste /
katham ityata āha - jñānasya buddhipūrvāṃ kriyāṃ niḥsāmarthyaṃ vā
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / ye shes ni blo sngon du 'gro bas byed pa'am /
kalpayata iti / / yadi [p.185]
# mthu med par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
jñānam idam ajñānaṃ prajahāmītyavadhārya tat prahāṇāya pravartata / ityayaṃ vyāpṛtau vikalpo'ntaḥ /
# gal te ye shes 'dis mi shes pa spong ngo snyam du rtogs nas de spang ba'i phyir 'jug go zhes bya ba 'di ni byed pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i mtha'o /
jñānasya kṣaṇikatvān na prahāṇavyāpārakāle saṃbhavaḥ /
# ye shes ni skad cig pa yin pas spyod pa byed pa'i dus na mi srid de /
ato'jñānaprahāṇasya niḥsāmarthyam tiyayam avyāpṛtau vikalpo'ntaḥ /
# de bas na mi shes pa spang ba'i mthu med do zhes bya ba 'di ni mi byed par rnam par rtog pa'i mtha'o /
etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ tailapradyota dṛṣṭāntaḥ /
# rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang ba'i phyir dpe mar me ste / / 'od srungs 'di lta ste /
tadyathā kāśyapa tailapradyote kṛte tamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchati na khalu / punaḥ kāśyapa tailapradyotasyaivaṃ bhavaty ahaṃ sarvam andhakāraṃ / vidhamāmīti /
# dper na mar me byung na mun pa mun nag thams cad med par 'gyur yang / / 'od srungs mar me 'di ltar bdag gis mun pa mun nag thams cad bsal lo snyam du mi sems mod kyi /
api tu khalu tailapradyotaṃ pratītya tamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchatīti / / evam eva kāśyapa jñāna utpanne'jñānaṃ vigacchati na khalu punaḥ
# 'on kyang mar me la brten nas mun pa mun nag med par 'gyur ba de bzhin du 'od srungs ye shes skyes na ni mi shes pa med par 'gyur te /
kāśyapa jñānasyaivaṃ bhavaty aham ajñānaṃ vidhamāmīti /
# ye shes ni 'di snyam du bdag gis mi shes pa bsal lo snyam du mi sems mod kyi /
api tu khalu jñānaṃ pratītyājñānaṃ vigacchatīti /
# 'on kyang ye shes la brten nas / / mun pa med par 'gyur ro zhes 'byung ba'o /
etad uktaṃ bhavati - yathā pradīpo vyāpāraśūnyas / tamo'ndhakāravyudāsābhiprāyarahitaś ca punar yasmin pradeśe kriyate / tasmāt pradeśāt pradīpasattāmātreṇa sarvatamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchatīti / evam eva yasmin santāne nirvikalpaṃ jñānam utpadyate tat / sattāmātrasadbhāvād eva tasmāt santānād ajñānaṃ vigacchati
# 'di skad du bstan par 'gyur te / / dper na mar me ni byed pas stong zhing mun pa mun nag bsal bar bsam pa med kyang / / phyogs dang du byung ba'i phyogs der mar me yod pa tsam gyis mun pa mun nag thams cad med par 'gyur ro / / de bzhin du rgyud gang la rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes skyes par gyur na de yod pa tsam gyis rgyud de las mi shes pa med par 'gyur te /
jñānasya nirvikalpatvāt kriyā'bhāvārtheti /
# ye shes ni rnam par mi rtog pa dang dpyod pa med pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ jñānasya vyāpārābhāvāt sāmarthyābhāvāt sāmarrthyābhāvaḥ / pradīpavat sattāmātreṇa pratipakṣanirākaraṇād iti / / ajanmatve'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ samakālatve'pi /
# de ltar ye shes ni byed pa'i mthu med la / / mar me bzhin du yod pa tsam gyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs sel to / / skye ba med par rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o / / dus mnyam pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa yang mtha'o /
vikalpo'nta ityanuvartate / / katham ityata āha - yadi pratipakṣasyānutpattiṃ vā kalpayati yatheyatā / kālena notpannapūrvaḥ pratipakṣas tathedānīm api notpatsyata iti ayam / ajanmatve vikalpo'ntaḥ /
# ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / gal te gnyen po ma skyes pa'am zhes bya ba smos te / / de ltar dus ji srid du sngon gnyen po ma skyes pa de bzhin du da yang mi skye'o snyam pa 'di ni skye ba med par rtog pa'i mtha'o /
saṅkleśasya vā dīrghakālatvam iti / / na hy ajñāne jñānapratiyoginyavasthita eva jñānam utpattuṃ samarthaṃ /
# yang na kun nas nyon mongs pa yun ring ba nyid du rtog pa zhes bya ba ni mi shes pa dang ye shes mi mthun par gnas pas ye shes 'byung ba'i mthu med do /
athāpi kathañcid utpadyeta tathāpi cirakālaviruddhatvād ajñānasya na
# ji ste brgya la skyes su zin na yang mi shes pa de yun ring po nas gnas gnas pa'i phyir /
jñānena tat kṣaṇikena vyudāsaḥ śakyate kartuṃ /
# ye shes skad cig pa des bsal bar bya mi nus so /
tataśca saṅkleśavyavadānayoḥ samānakālatvam iti / / etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ dvitīyas
# de bas na nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis dus mnyam pa nyid do snyam pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i mtha' de gnyis yongs su spang ba'i phyir mar me'i dpe gnyis pa ste /
tailapradyotadṛṣṭānta iti / / tadyathā kāśyapa gṛhe vā layane vā'vacarake vā varṣasahasrasyātyayān / na kenacit tailapradyotaḥ kuto bhavati /
# 'od srungs 'di lta ste / / dper na khyim mam khang pa'am khang phran lo brgya stong 'das par sus kyang lan 'ga' yang mar me ma bus pa der mi la la zhig gis mar me bus na /
atha tatra kaścid eva puruṣas tailapradyotaṃ kuryāt / / tat kiṃ manyase kāśyapāpi tu tamo'ndhākārasyaivaṃ bhaved / varṣasahasrasañcito'haṃ nāham ato vigamiṣyāmīti /
# 'od srungs de ji snyam du sems / / mun pa mun nag de 'di ltar bdag ni lo brgya stong du bsags pa yin te / / bdag 'di nas mi 'gro'o snyam du sems sam / / gsol ba bcom ldan 'das mi sems te /
āha - no bhagavan na hi tamo'ndhakārasya śaktir asti tailapradyote kṛte na
# mar me byung na mun pa mun nag la mi mchi ba'i nus pa ma mchis kyi / / gdon mi 'tshal bar ma mchis par 'gyur ro /
vigantum avaśyaṃ tena vigantavyaṃ /
# bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa /
bhagavān āha - evam eva kāśyapa kalpaśatasahasrasañcito'pi karmakleśa / ekena yoniśomanaskāreṇa vigacchati /
# 'od srungs de bzhin du las dang nyon mongs pa bskal pa brgya stong du bsags pa yang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa'i so sor rtog pa gcig gis med par 'gyur ro /
tailapradyota iti kāśyapa [p.186} / āryasyaitat prajñendriyasyādhivacanaṃ / / tamo'ndhakāra iti śabalasyaitat karmakleśasyādhivacanam iti /
# 'od srungs mar me zhes bya ba de ni 'phags pa'i shes rab kyi dbang po'i tshig bla dags so / / 'od srungs mun pa mun nag ces bya ba ni las dang nyon mongs pa'i tshig bla dags so zhes 'byung ba'o /
nidarśanena pratipakṣasyānutpattiṃ pariharati pratyayapratibuddhatvāt tad / utpatteḥ saṅkleśatulyakālatāñca / / kṛṣṇapakṣasya durbalatvāt balavattvāñca tat pratipakṣasya / tamo'ndhakārapradīpavad iti /
# de lta bas na 'dis ni skye ba rkyen las rag las pa'i phyir gnyen po mi skye ba dang kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyogs dang dus mnyam pa nyid kyi lan btab pa ste / / nag po'i phyogs stobs chung zhing gnyen po de stobs dang ldan pa'i phyir mun pa mun nag dang mar me bzhin no /
uktāntadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ //
# mtha' gnyis spangs pa sgrub pa bshad zin to /
{ viśīṣṭā cā'viśiṣṭā ca pratipattiḥ } / antadvayavarjanapratipatter anantaraṃ viśiṣṭā cāviśiṣṭā ca pratipattir / uddiṣṭetyato'ntadvayavarjanapratipattinirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati - viśiṣṭā
# mtha' gnyis spangs pa sgrub pa'i 'og tu khyad par can dang khyad par med pa sgrub pa smos pas / / de'i phyir mtha' gnyis spangs pa sgrub pa bshad pa'i 'og tu khyad par can dang khyad par med pa sgrub pa gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang de'i phyir /
cāviśiṣṭā ca pratipattiḥ kathameti / / ata āha -
# khyad par can dang khyad med ni / / sa bcu dag tu shes par bya /
viśiṣṭā cāviśiṣṭā ca jñeyā daśasu bhūmiṣu // / tāsu daśasu bhūmiṣv ekaikaśo dviprakārāpi pratipattiḥ / / katham ityata āha - yasyāṃ bhūmau yā pāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavatīti
# zhes bya ba gsungs so / / sa bcu po de dag re re la yang sgrub pa rnam pa gnyi ga'o / / ji lta zhe na de'i phyir / / sa gang la pha rol tu phyin pa gang gi shas che ba zhes bya ba rgya cher smos so /
vistaraḥ / / yasyāṃ bodhisattvabhūmau vyavasthito boshisattvo yasyāṃ pāramitāyām
# byang chub sems dpa'i sa gang la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' pha rol tu phyin pa gang la lhag par spyod pa de ni /
ādhikyena prayujyate sā tasyāṃ bodhisattvabhūmāv itarābhyaḥ / pāramitā'bhyo'tiriktatarā bhavatīti viśiṣṭocyate / / tadyathā prathamāyāṃ bhūmau dānapāramitātiriktatarā bhavatīti / / tatra pratipattir viśiṣṭocyate / / evaṃ yāvad daśamyāṃ jñānapāramiteti /
# byang chub sems dpa' sa de la pha rol tu phyin pa / / gzhan dag pas shas cher gyur pas na khyad par can zhes bya ste / / 'di ltar sa dang po la sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa shas che ba yin te / / de la sgrub pa khyad par can zhes bya'o / / de bzhin du sa bcu pa la ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du'o /
aviśeṣeṇa śeṣāsu sarvāsu pāramitāsu tasyāṃ bhūmau samudāgacchatīti / tāsu pratipattir aviśiṣṭocyate /
# sa de dang der pha rol tu phyin pa lhag ma thams can la yang / / khyad par med par yang dag par sgrub pa ni de dag la sgrub pa khyad par med pa zhes bya ste /
yathoktaṃ pramuditāyāṃ bhūmau dānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavatīti /
# ji skad du sa rab tu dga' ba la sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i shas che ba yin te /
na ca śeṣāsu na samudāgacchati yathābalaṃ yathābhājamānam iti /
# lhag ma rnams kyang ci nus kyi 'os su yang dag par mi sgrub pa ma yin no zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
evaṃ śeṣāsu bhūmiṣu yathāsūtraṃ nirdeśo veditavyaḥ / / uktaṃ pratipattyānuttaryaṃ //5-27// / { ālambanānuttaryaṃ } [p.187] / idānīm ālambanānuttaryaṃ nirdeśāvasara ityata āha -
# de bzhin du sa lhag ma rnams la yang mdo las ji skad bshad pa bzhin du rig par bya'o / / sgrub pa bla na med pa nyid bshad zin to / / da ni dmigs pa bla na med pa nyid bshad pa'i skabs su bab ste /
ālambanānuttaryaṃ katamad iti / / atas tannirdhāraṇārthaṃ bravīti -
# de'i phyir dmigs pa bla na med pa nyid gang zhe na zhes bya ba smos so / / de'i 'og tu de dmigs kyis dbye ba'i phyir /
vyavasthānaṃ tathā dhātuḥ
# rnam par gzhag dang de bzhin dbyings /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
ityetad dvādaśavidham ālambanaṃ vyavasthānālambanam ārabhya yāvat
# dmigs pa ni rnam pa bcu gnyis po 'di dag ste / / rnam par gzhag pa'i dmigs pa nas /
prakarṣālambanaṃ /
# phul du byung ba'i dmigs pa'i bar du'o /
tadanyasarvālambanotkṛṣṭatvād ālambanānuttaryam ucyate /
# de ma yin pa'i dmigs pa gzhan thams cad pas mchog yin pas na / / dmigs pa bla na med pa nyid ces bya'o /
tatra prathamaṃ ye pāramitādayo dharmāste'pi buddhair bodhisattvaiś ca / sattvānugrahārthaṃ vyavasthāpyanta iti vyavasthānaṃ /
# de la dang po ni pha rol tu phyin pa'i chos gang dag ste / / de dag kyang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis sems can la phan gdags pa'i phyir / / rnam par gzhag pas na rnam par gzhag pa'o /
etad eva pradarśayan bhāṣyakāro'pyāha - / dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānālambanam iti /
# de nyid bstan pa'i phyir 'grel pa byed pas kyang chos brtags pa rnam par gzhag pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba smos so /
dharmāṇāṃ dānapāramitādibodhipakṣāryasatyādīnāṃ prajñaptir / dharmaprajñaptiḥ / / tayā vyavatiṣṭhate sā vā'tra vyavasthānam iti / dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānaṃ /
# chos rnams ni pha rol tu phyin pa dang byang chub kyi phyogs dang phung po la sogs pa brtags pa ste / / 'dis rnam par gzhag pa'am yang na de 'dir gzhag pas na / / chos brtags pa rnam par gzhag pa'o /
abhisamayānukūlyāc cātra vyavasthānālambanādīnām ānupūrvīṃ
# mngon par rtogs pa dang mthun pa'i phyir / / 'dir rnam par gzhag pa'i dmigs pa la sogs pa'i go rims su blta'o /
draṣṭavyeti / / dvitīyaṃ tathatā dharmadhātuparyāyatvāt / / tṛtīyacaturthe iti / / tatra tṛtītaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ caturthaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ /
# gnyis pa de ni de bzhin nyid de chos kyi dbyings kyi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'i phyir ro / / gsum pa dang bzhi pa zhes bya ba de la / / gsum pa ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa'o / / bzhi pa ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa'o /
te eveti prathamadvitīya eva / / yathākramam iti prathamaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ dvitīyaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ /
# de dag nyid la zhes bya ba ni dang po dang gnyis pa'o / / go rims bzhin te zhes bya ba la dang po ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa'o / / gnyis pa ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa ste /
tatraiva kāraṇam āha - dharmadhātuprativedhena
# 'dir rgyu smos pa / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs pas /
pāramitādidharmādhigamād iti / / dharmadhātuprativedhād anāsravāḥ pāramitā adhigacchatītyataḥ / sādhyālambanaṃ prathamaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ dvitīyam iti / / pañcamaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ /
# pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa'i chos rnams khong du chud pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'o / / chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs pas zag pa med pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams mngon par khong du chud ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste dang po ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa'o / / gnyis pa ni sgrub pa'i dmigs pa'o / / lnga pa ni 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa ste /
tac chrutamayasya jñānasya /
# thos pa las byung ba'i shes pa'i dmigs pa'o /
śrutamātreṇa pāramitādīn dharmān dharmadhātuñca dhārayatīti
# thos pa tsam gyis pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa'i chos rnams dang chos kyi dbyings 'dzin pas na /
śrutamayaṃ jñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate / / dhāraṇāyā ālambanaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ / / tat punaḥ prathamam eva dvayaṃ vyavasthānālambanaṃ
# thos pa las byung ba'i shes pa ni 'dzin pa zhes bya'o / / 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa ni 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa ste / / de yang dang po dang gnyis pa de nyid de /
dharmādhātvālambanañca / / ṣaṣṭhaṃ cintāmayasyāvagamya dhāraṇād iti /
# rnam par gzhag pa dang chos kyi dbyings kyi dmigs pa'o / / drug pa ni bsam pa las byung ba ste / / rtogs nas 'dzin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni /
apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattisādhanadharmatāyuktibhir avagamya / śrutārthadhāraṇād avadhāraṇā cintāmayaṃ jñānaṃ tasyālambanam
# ltos pa dang bya ba byed pa dang 'thad pa sgrub pa dang chos nyid kyi rigs pa rnams kyis thos pa'i don khong du chud nas 'dzin pa'i phyir ro / / nges par 'dzin pa ni bsams pa las byung ba'i shes pa ste /
avadhāraṇālambanaṃ / / saptamaṃ bhāvanāmayasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ /
# de'i nges pa ni nges par 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa'o / / bdun pa ni bsgoms pa las byung ba ste zhes bya ba ni dmigs pa zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
pratyātmaṃ dhāraṇād iti pratyātmam arthasya [p.188] / dhāraṇāt pradhāraṇā prathamabhūmipraveśaprāyogikaṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ
# so so rang gis rig pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni / / so so rang gis don 'dzin pas na rab tu 'dzin pa ste / / sa dang po la 'jug par sbyor ba can bsgoms pa las byung ba'i shes pa'o /
jñānaṃ / / tat punaḥ smṛtyupasthānānyārabhya yāvad balāni / / tasyālambanaṃ pradhāraṇālambanaṃ /
# de yang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa nas brtsams nas stobs kyi bar du ste / / de'i dmigs pa ni rab tu 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa'o /
aṣṭamaṃ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau darśanamārgasyeti /
# brgyad pa ni sa dang po la mthong ba'i lam gyi'o zhes bya ba ni /
pratyātmam advayasya dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvaprativedhaḥ /
# so so rang gi chos kyi dbyings gnyis su med pa thams cad du song ba rtogs pa'o /
athavā darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānām akliṣṭasya cājñānasya / sarvatragārthaviṣayasya pratyanīko vedhaḥ prativedhaḥ /
# yang na mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams dang thams cad du 'gro ba'i don gyi yul la nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i mi shes pa'i dgra bo rtogs pa ni rab tu rtogs pa ste /
sa punar darśanamārgaḥ / / tasyālambanaṃ prativedhālambanaṃ /
# de yang mthong ba'i lam mo / / de'i dmigs pa ni rab tu rtogs pa'i dmigs pa'o /
navamaṃ bhāvanāmārgasya yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmāv iti /
# dgu pa ni bsgom pa'i lam gyi ste / / sa bdun pa'i bar du'o zhes bya ba ni /
tasyaiva dharmadhātuprativedhasyābhyāsād uttarottaraprakarṣaṃ gatiḥ / pratānatā bhāvanāmārgo yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmau /
# chos kyi dbyings rab tu rtogs pa de nyid goms par byas pas / / gong nas gong du khyad zhugs par 'gro bas rab tu rgyas pa ste / / bsgom pa'i lam sa bdun pa'i bar du'o /
tasya bhāvanāmārgasyālambanaṃ pratānatālambanaṃ / / daśamaṃ tatraiva laukikalokottarasya mārgasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ /
# bsgom pa'i lam de'i dmigs pa ni rab tu rgyas pa'i dmigs pa'o / / bcu pa ni de nyid na 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi ste zhes bya ba ni /
prakāraśo dharmādhigamād iti /
# dmigs pa'o zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
tasyām eva bhūmau / sarvasūtrādidharmanimittaprakārādyabhiniveśavigamamukhena prakāreṇa / dharmādhigamāt pragama iti / / sa eva bhāvanāmārga ucyate saptamyām eva bhūmau /
# chos rnam par khong du chud pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni sa de nyid na mdo la sogs pa'i chos kyi mtshan ma'i rnam pa la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa dang bral pa'i sgo nas chos rnam par khong du chud pas na rnam par khong du chud pa'o / / de nyid ni bsgom pa'i lam zhes bya ste / / sa bdun pa nyid du'o / / rnam par khong du chud pa'i dmigs pa ni /
pragamasyālambanaṃ pragamālambanaṃ /
# rnam par khong du chud pa'i dmigs pa'o /
ekādaśamaṣṭamyāṃ bhūmau /
# bcu gcig pa ni sa brgyad pa la'o zhes bya ba ni /
aṣṭamyāṃ hi bhūmau sarvanimittābhogamanasikāravigatasya svarasena
# mtshan ma dang 'bad pa'i yid la byed pa thams cad dang bral nas rang gi tshul gyis rnal du 'dug pas 'jug pa'i phyir te /
praśaṭhabvahanāt sa eva bhāvanāmārgaḥ /
# bsgom pa'i lam de nyid la rnal du 'dug pa zhes bya'o /
praśaṭhasyālambanaṃ praśaṭhālambanaṃ /
# rnal du 'dug pa'i dmigs pa ni / / rnal du 'dug pa'i dmigs pa'o /
dvādaśaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye navamyāṃ pratisaṃvijjñānaprakarṣalābhāt
# bcu gnyis pa ni sa dgu pa la sogs pa gsum la'o zhes bya ba ni; sa dgu pa la so so yang dag par rig pa'i ye shes phul du byung ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
daśamyāṃ karmavaśitāprakarṣalābhāt /
# sa bcu pa la ni las la dbang ba phul du byung ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
buddhabhūmāv aśeṣakleśajñayāvaraṇaviśuddhiprakarṣālābhāt /
# sangs rgyas kyi sar ni nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa lhag ma rnam par dag pa phul du byung ba thob pa'i phyir te /
evaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye jñānakarmaviśuddhiprakarṣagamanāt tad / bhūmivyavasthitasya yadālambanaṃ tat prakarṣālambanam ucyate / / anyaḥ punar āha - mārgaprakarṣasyaiva mṛdumadhyādhimātrabhedaṃ kṛtvā
# de ltar sa dgu pa la sogs pa gsum la ye shes dang las dang rnam par dag pa phul du byung bas sa de dag la gnas pa'i dmigs pa gang yin pa de dag ni / / phul du byung ba'i dmigs pa zhes bya'o / / gzhan dag na re lam phul du byung ba nyid chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen por phye nas /
prakarṣālambanaṃ tisṛṣu bhūmiṣūktam iti /
# sa gsum po dag la phul du byung ba'i dmigs par bshad do zhe'o /
tadeva hi prathamadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyām avasthāyāṃ tat tadālambananāma / pratilabhata iti / / etac cālambanaṃ yad uta dharmavyavasthānālambanaṃ / dharmadhātvālambanañca / / taccaitad ālambanadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyāṃ jñānāvasthāyāṃ tat tan nāma / labhate /
# dang po dang gnyis pa de dag ni de dang de'i dmigs pa'i ming 'thob po zhes bya ba ni / / dmigs pa de dag kyang 'di lta ste / / chos rnam par gzhag pa'i dmigs pa dang chos kyi dbyings kyi dmigs pa'o / / de la dmigs pa de nyid kyang ye shes de dang de dag tu na de dang de'i ming 'thob ste /
śrutamayajñānāvasthāyāṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ dhāraṇājñānaviṣayatvāc / chrutasya /
# thos pa las byung ba'i shes pa'i dus ni 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa ste / / 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi yul ni thos pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
tena ca dhāraṇājñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate /
# de bas na 'dzin pa'i shes pa la 'dzin pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ yāvat prakarṣālambanaṃ vaktavyaṃ /
# de bzhin du phul du byung ba'i dmigs pa'i rab tu brjod par bya'o /
navamyāṃ daśamyāṃ buddhabhūmau ca prakarṣāprāptaṃ lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ / tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ ca laukikaṃ /
# sa dgu pa dang bcu pa dang sangs rgyas kyi sar ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes dang de'i rjes las thob pa dag pa 'jig rten pa phul du byung ba brnyes te /
tasyālambanaṃ prakarṣālambanaṃ /
# 'di'i dmigs pa ni phul du byung ba'i dmigs pa'o /
uktam ālambanānuttaryaṃ //
# dmigs pa bla na med pa nyid bshad zin to /
{ samudāgamānuttaryaṃ } [p.189] / idānīṃ samudāgamānuttaryasyāvasaraprāptasyā'vadhāraṇārtham āha - / samudāgamaḥ katama iti /
# da ni yang dag par 'grub pa bra na med pa nyid kyi skabs su bab pas de bstan pa'i phyir / / yang dag par 'grub pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba smos te /
tayā tayā pratipattyā samudānīyata iti samudāgamaḥ /
# sgrub pa de dang des yang dag par 'grub pas na yang dag par 'grub pa'o /
tad anyebhyaḥ samudāgamebhyo viśiṣṭatvāt tataścānyasya samudāgamasya / viśiṣṭābhāvād ānuttaryam ucyate / / tat pradarśanārtham āha -
# de las gzhan pa'i yang dag par 'grub pa rnams las khyad par du 'phags pa dang yang dag par 'grub pa khyad par can de las gzhan med pa'i phyir bla na med pa zhes bya'o / / de bstan pa'i phyir /
avaikalyāpratikṣepo vikṣepaś ca prapūraṇā /
# ma tshang med dang mi spong dang / / mi g yeng ba dang rab rdzogs dang /
iti vistaraḥ /
# zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
tatra pratyayāvaikalyam ārabhya yāvad bodhisandarśanam ityeṣa daśavidhaḥ / samudāgamaḥ / / tatra pratyayāvaikalyaṃ gotrasamudāgama iti /
# de la rkyen ma tshang ba med pa nas brtsams te / / byang chub kun du ston pa zhes bya ba'i bar du rnam pa bcu po de lta bu ni yang dag par 'grub pa'o / / de la rkyen ma tshang ba med pa ni rigs yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba la /
pratyayānām avaikalyaṃ samagrāṇāṃ sānnidhyaṃ /
# rkyen rnams ma tshang ba med pa ni thams cad tshogs pa'o /
teṣv āhṛteṣu gotraṃ samudāgaccyati sphītaṃ tad viśiṣṭataraṃ / bhavatītyarthaḥ /
# de dag tshogs na rigs yang dag par 'grub ste / / rgyas pa dang khyad par can du 'gyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tat punaḥ satpuruṣasaṃsevā saddharmaśravaṇaṃ yoniśo manaskāra ityevam / ādayaḥ / / teṣāṃ tad gotramitrādivaikalyād vaikalyaṃ / / mahāyānāpratikṣepo'dhimuktisamudāgama iti /
# de yang skyes bu dam pa la brten pa dang dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa la sogs pa'o / / rigs dang bshes gnyen la sogs pa de dag ma tshang ba'o / / theg pa chen po mi spong ba de ni mos pa yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
yadi gāmbhīryaudāryalakṣaṇamahāyānadharmaṃ na pratikṣipatyevam asya
# gal te zab cing rgya che ba'i mtshan nyid theg pa chen po'i chos mi spong na /
niścayasya dhāraṇātmikāyā adhimukteḥ puṣṭir bhavati /
# de lta na de'i nges par 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyi mos pa rgyas par 'gyur ro /
hīnayānāvikṣepaścittorpādasamudāgama iti / / yadutpāditabodhicittasya satsvapi bodhicittavyāvṛttipratyayeṣu
# theg pa dman par mi g yeng ba ni sems bskyed pa yang dag par 'gyur ba'o zhes bya ba ni / / gal te byang chub tu sems bskyed la / / byang chub kyi sems las ldog pa'i rkyen yod du zin kyang /
śrāvakayāne pratyekabuddhayāne vā cittam asya na krāmatyevam asya tad
# nyan thos kyi theg pa'am / / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg par des sems mi 'jug na /
bodhicittaṃ puṣṭim āpadyate /
# de lta na byang chub kyi sems de brtas par 'gyur ro /
pāramitāparipūraṇā pratipattisamudāgama iti /
# pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pa ni 'grub pa yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba la /
utpāditabodhicittānāṃ tadvaśād dānādipāramitānāṃ paripūryā / sarvajñatā pratipattipuṣṭir bhavati /
# byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa dag de'i dbang gis sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su rdzogs pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid sgrub pa rgyas par 'gyur ro / / 'phags pa'i lam bskyed pa ni /
āryamārgotpādo nyāmāvakrāntisamudāgama iti /
# skyon med par 'jug pa yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
prathamata evāpūrvasyāryamārgasyotpādo nyāmāvakrāntir bhavati /
# thog ma nyid du sngon ma skyes pa'i 'phags pa'i lam bskyed pas skyon med pa la 'jug par 'gyur ro /
āma ucyate doṣaḥ kṣayo vā /
# skyon zhes bya ba ni nyes pa'am zag pa ste /
sa yatra nāsti sā nyāmā nivātavadanāsravā bhūmiḥ
# gang na de med pa de ni skyon med pa ste / / rlung med pa bzhin te zag pa med pa'i sa'o /
nyāmāyāmavakrāntir nyāmāvakrāntiḥ praveśa ityarthaḥ / [p.190] / niyamāvakrāntipāṭhe'pi niyama eva niyamaḥ / / tathā hy utpannadarśanamārgo niyato bhavati sugatau nirvāṇe ceti /
# nges par 'jug pa zhes 'byung ba yang nges pa nyid nges pa ste / / 'di ltar mthong ba'i lam skyes na / / bde 'gro dang mya ngan las 'das pa nyid du nges par 'gyur ro / / dge ba'i rtsa ba 'phel ba ni yun ring po nas 'dris par bya ba'i phyir /
kuśalamūlanirūḍhir dīrghakālaparicayāt sattvaparipākasamudāgama iti /
# sems can yongs su smin par byed pa yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba ni mthong ba'i lam thos nas /
labdhadarśanamārgāṇāṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhasya bhāvanāmārgasya / dīrghakālaparicayād abhyāsāt kuśalamūlavṛddhiḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ / / tayā sattvaparipācanasamartho bhavati /
# de'i rjes las thob pa bsgom pa'i lam la yun ring por 'dris par byas goms par byas pas / / dge ba'i rtsa ba 'grub pa ni dge ba'i rtsa ba 'phel ba'o / / des sems can yongs su smin par byed nus par 'gyur te /
ataḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ sattvaparipākasamudāgamaḥ /
# de'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba 'phel ba ni / / sems can yongs su smin par byed par yang dag par 'grub pa'o /
anye tvāhuḥ - evam asya sattvaparipākaḥ samudāgato bhavatiḥ yadyanena / dīrghakālābhyāsamāgamya sattvasantāneṣu kuśalamūlaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtaṃ / / cittakarmañatā kṣetrapariśuddhisamudāgama iti /
# gzhan dag na re de'i sems can yongs su smin par byed pa yang dag par 'grub pa ni 'di lta bu yin te / / 'di ltar 'dis yun ring po nas goms par byed pa la brten nas / / sems can rnams kyi rgyud la dge ba'i rtsa ba brtan por byas par 'gyur pa'o zhes zer ro / / sems las su rung ba ni zhing yongs su dag pa yang dag par 'grub pa'o zhes bya ba la /
evaṃ bhāvanayā vivṛddhakuśalamūlānām ekāyatanamārgavipakṣayor / nimittābhogayor vigamāc cittasya karmañatā /
# de ltar bsgoms pas / / dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams 'phel nas gcig tu bgrod pa'i lam gyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs mtshan ma dang 'bad pa dang bral ba'i phyir sems las su rung ste /
# slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so /
